AVŚa ulūkayātuṃ śuśulūkayātuṃ jahi śvayātum uta kokayātum 
AVŚc suparṇayātum uta gṛdhrayātuṃ dṛṣadeva pra mṛṇa rakṣa indra 
AVŚa mā no rakṣo abhi naḍ yātumāvad apochantu mithunā ye kimīdinaḥ 
AVŚc pṛthivī naḥ pārthivāt pātv aṃhaso 'ntarikṣaṃ divyāt pātv asmān 
AVŚa indra jahi pumāṃsaṃ yātudhānam uta striyaṃ māyayā śāśadānām 
AVŚc vigrīvāso mūradevā ṛdantu mā te dṛśant sūryam uccarantam 
AVŚa prati cakṣva vi cakṣvendraś ca soma jāgṛtam 
AVŚc rakṣobhyo vadham asyatam aśaniṃ yātumadbhyaḥ  
AVŚa ayaṃ pratisaro maṇir vīro vīrāya badhyate 
AVŚc vīryavānt sapatnahā śūravīraḥ paripāṇaḥ sumaṅgalaḥ 
AVŚa ayaṃ maṇiḥ sapatnahā suvīraḥ sahasvān vājī sahamāna ugraḥ 
AVŚc pratyak kṛtyā dūṣayann eti vīraḥ 
AVŚa anenendro maṇinā vṛtram ahann anenāsurān parābhāvayan manīṣī 
AVŚc anenājayad dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime anenājayat pradiśaś catasraḥ 
AVŚa ayaṃ srāktyo maṇiḥ pratīvartaḥ pratisaraḥ 
AVŚc ojasvān vimṛdho vaśī so asmān pātu sarvataḥ 
AVŚa tad agnir āha tad u soma āha bṛhaspatiḥ savitā tad indraḥ 
AVŚc te me devāḥ purohitāḥ pratīcīḥ kṛtyāḥ pratisarair ajantu 
AVŚa antar dadhe dyāvāpṛthivī utāhar uta sūryam 
AVŚc te me devāḥ purohitāḥ pratīcīḥ kṛtyāḥ pratisarair ajantu 
AVŚa ye srāktyaṃ maṇiṃ janā varmāṇi kṛṇvate 
AVŚc sūrya iva divam āruhya vi kṛtyā bādhate vaśī 
AVŚa srāktyena maṇinā ṛṣiṇeva manīṣiṇā 
AVŚc ajaiṣaṃ sarvāḥ pṛtanā vi mṛdho hanmi rakṣasaḥ 
AVŚa yāḥ kṛtyā āṅgirasīr yāḥ kṛtyā āsurīr yāḥ 
AVŚc kṛtyāḥ svayaṃkṛtā yā u cānyebhir ābhṛtāḥ 
AVŚe ubhayīs tāḥ parā yantu parāvato navatiṃ nāvyā ati 
AVŚa asmai maṇiṃ varma badhnantu devā indro viṣṇuḥ savitā rudro agniḥ 
AVŚc prajāpatiḥ parameṣṭhī virāḍ vaiśvānara ṛṣayaś ca sarve  
AVŚa uttamo asy oṣadhīnām anaḍvān jagatām iva vyāghraḥ śvapadām iva 
AVŚḍ yam aichāmāvidāma taṃ pratispāśanam antitam 
AVŚa sa id vyāghro bhavaty atho siṃho atho vṛṣā 
AVŚc atho sapatnakarśano yo bibhartīmaṃ maṇim 
AVŚa nainaṃ ghnanty apsaraso na gandharvā na martyāḥ 
AVŚc sarvā diśo vi rājati yo bibhartīmaṃ maṇim 
AVŚa kaśyapas tvām asṛjata kaśyapas tvā sam airayat 
AVŚc abibhas tvendro mānuṣe bibhrat saṃśreṣiṇe 'jayat 
AVŚe maṇiṃ sahasravīryaṃ varma devā akṛṇvata 
AVŚa yas tvā kṛtyābhir yas tvā dīkṣābhir yajñair yas tvā jighāṃsati 
AVŚc pratyak tvam indra taṃ jahi vajreṇa śataparvaṇā 
AVŚa ayam id vai pratīvarta ojasvān saṃjayo maṇiḥ 
AVŚc prajāṃ dhanaṃ ca rakṣatu paripāṇaḥ sumaṅgalaḥ 
AVŚa asapatnaṃ no adharād asapatnaṃ na uttarāt 
AVŚc indrāsapatnaṃ naḥ paścāj jyotiḥ śūra puras kṛdhi 
AVŚa varma me dyāvāpṛthivī varmāhar varma sūryaḥ 
AVŚc varma ma indraś cāgniś ca varma dhātā dadhātu me 
AVŚa aindrāgnaṃ varma bahulaṃ yad ugraṃ viśve devā nātividhyanti sarve 
AVŚc tan me tanvaṃ trāyatāṃ sarvato bṛhad āyuṣmāṃ jaradaṣṭir yathāsāni 
AVŚa ā mārukṣad devamaṇir mahyā ariṣṭatātaye 
AVŚc imaṃ methim abhisaṃviśadhvaṃ tanūpānaṃ trivarūtham ojase 
AVŚa asminn indro ni dadhātu nṛmṇam imaṃ devāso abhisaṃviśadhvam 
AVŚc dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāyāyuṣmān jaradaṣṭir yathāsat 
AVŚa svastidā viśāṃ patir vṛtrahā vimṛdho vaśī 
AVŚc indro badhnātu te maṇiṃ jigīvāṃ aparājitaḥ 
AVŚe somapā abhayaṅkaro vṛṣā 
AVŚa yau te mātonmamārja jātāyāḥ pativedanau 
AVŚc durṇāmā tatra mā gṛdhad aliṃśa uta vatsapaḥ 
AVŚa palālānupalālau śarkuṃ kokaṃ malimlucaṃ palījakam 
AVŚc āśreṣaṃ vavrivāsasam ṛkṣagrīvaṃ pramīlinam 
AVŚa mā saṃ vṛto mopa sṛpa ūrū māva sṛpo 'ntarā 
AVŚc kṛṇomy asyai bheṣajaṃ bajaṃ durṇāmacātanam 
AVŚa durṇāmā ca sunāmā cobhā samvṛtam ichataḥ 
AVŚc arāyān apa hanmaḥ sunāmā straiṇam ichatām 
AVŚa yaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ keśy asura stambaja uta tuṇḍikaḥ 
AVŚc arāyān asyā muṣkābhyāṃ bhaṃsaso 'pa hanmasi 
AVŚa anujighraṃ pramṛśantaṃ kravyādam uta reriham 
AVŚc arāyāṃ chvakiṣkiṇo bajaḥ piṅgo anīnaśat 
AVŚa yas tvā svapne nipadyate bhrātā bhūtvā piteva ca 
AVŚc bajas tānt sahatām itaḥ klībarūpāṃs tirīṭinaḥ 
AVŚa yas tvā svapantīṃ tsarati yas tvā dipsati jāgratīm 
AVŚc chāyām iva pra tānt sūryaḥ parikrāmann anīnaśat 
AVŚa yaḥ kṛṇoti mṛtavatsām avatokām imāṃ striyam 
AVŚc tam oṣadhe tvaṃ nāśayāsyāḥ kamalam añjivam 
AVŚa ye śālāḥ parinṛtyanti sāyaṃ gardabhanādinaḥ 
AVŚc kusūlā ye ca kukṣilāḥ kakubhāḥ karumāḥ srimāḥ 
AVŚe tān oṣadhe tvaṃ gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya  
AVŚa ye kukundhāḥ kukirabhāḥ kṛttīr dūrśāni bibhrati 
AVŚc klībā iva pranṛtyanto vane ye kurvate ghoṣaṃ tān ito nāśayāmasi 
AVŚa ye sūryaṃ na titikṣanta ātapantam amuṃ divaḥ 
AVŚc arāyān bastavāsino durgandhīṃl lohitāsyān makakān nāśayāmasi 
AVŚa ya ātmānam atimātram aṃsa ādhāya bibhrati 
AVŚc strīṇāṃ śroṇipratodina indra rakṣāṃsi nāśaya 
AVŚa ye pūrve badhvo yanti haste śṛṅgāni bibhrataḥ 
AVŚc āpākesthāḥ prahāsina stambe ye kurvate jyotis tān ito nāśayāmasi 
AVŚa yeṣām paścāt prapadāni puraḥ pārṣṇīḥ puro mukhā 
AVŚc khalajāḥ śakadhūmajā uruṇḍā ye ca maṭmaṭāḥ kumbhamuṣkā ayāśavaḥ 
AVŚe tān asyā brahmaṇas pate pratībodhena nāśaya 
AVŚa paryastākṣā apracaṅkaśā astraiṇāḥ santu paṇḍagāḥ 
AVŚc ava bheṣaja pādaya ya imāṃ saṃvivṛtsaty apatiḥ svapatiṃ striyam 
AVŚa uddharṣiṇaṃ munikeśaṃ jambhayantaṃ marīmṛśam 
AVŚc upeṣantam udumbalaṃ tuṇḍelam uta śāluḍam 
AVŚe padā pra vidhya pārṣṇyā sthālīṃ gaur iva spandanā 
AVŚa yas te garbhaṃ pratimṛśāj jātaṃ vā mārayāti te 
AVŚc piṅgas tam ugradhanvā kṛṇotu hṛdayāvidham 
AVŚa ye amno jatān mārayanti sūtikā anuśerate 
AVŚc strībhāgān piṅgo gandharvān vāto abhram ivājatu 
AVŚa parisṛṣṭaṃ dharayatu yad dhitaṃ māva pādi tat 
AVŚc garbhaṃ ta ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvibhāryau  
AVŚa pavīnasāt taṅgalvāc chāyakād uta nagnakāt 
AVŚc prajāyai patye tvā piṅgaḥ pari pātu kimīdinaḥ 
AVŚa dvyāsyāc caturakṣāt pañcapadād anaṅgureḥ 
AVŚc vṛntād abhi prasarpataḥ pari pāhi varīvṛtāt 
AVŚa ya āmaṃ māṃsam adanti pauruṣeyaṃ ca ye kraviḥ 
AVŚc garbhān khādanti keśavās tān ito nāśayāmasi 
AVŚa ye sūryāt parisarpanti snuṣeva śvaśurād adhi 
AVŚc bajaś ca teṣāṃ piṅgaś ca hṛdaye 'dhi ni vidhyatām 
AVŚa piṅga rakṣa jāyamānaṃ mā pumāṃsaṃ striyaṃ kran 
AVŚc āṇḍādo garbhān mā dabhan bādhasvetaḥ kimīdinaḥ 
AVŚa aprajāstvaṃ mārtavatsam ād rodam agham āvayam 
AVŚc vṛkṣād iva srajam kṛtvāpriye prati muñca tat  
AVŚa yā babhravo yāś ca śukrā rohiṇīr uta pṛśnayaḥ 
AVŚc asiknīḥ kṛṣṇā oṣadhīḥ sarvā achāvadāmasi 
AVŚa trāyantām imaṃ purusaṃ yakṣmād deveṣitād adhi 
AVŚc yāsām dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā samudro mūlaṃ vīrudhāṃ babhūva 
AVŚa āpo agraṃ divyā oṣadhayaḥ 
AVŚc tās te yakṣmam enasyam aṅgādaṅgād anīnaśan 
AVŚa prastṛṇatī stambinīr ekaśuṅgāḥ pratanvatīr oṣadhīr ā vadāmi 
AVŚc aṃśumatīḥ kaṇḍinīr yā viśākhā hvayāmi te vīrudho vaiśvadevīr ugrāḥ puruṣajīvanīḥ 
AVŚa yad vaḥ sahaḥ sahamānā vīryaṃ yac ca vo balam 
AVŚc tenemam asmād yakṣmāt puruṣaṃ muñcatauṣadhīr atho kṛṇomi bheṣajam 
AVŚa jīvalāṃ naghāriṣāṃ jīvantīm oṣadhīm aham 
AVŚc arundhatīm unnayantīṃ puṣpām madhumatīm iha huve 'smā ariṣṭatātaye 
AVŚa ihā yantu pracetaso medinīr vacaso mama 
AVŚc yathemaṃ pārayāmasi puruṣaṃ duritād adhi 
AVŚa agner ghāso apāṃ garbho yā rohanti punarṇavāḥ 
AVŚc dhruvāḥ sahasranāmnīr bheṣajīḥ santv ābhṛtāḥ 
AVŚa avakolbā udakātmāna oṣadhayaḥ 
AVŚc vyṛṣantu duritaṃ tīkṣṇaśṛṅgyaḥ 
AVŚa unmuñcantīr vivaruṇā ugrā yā viṣadūṣanīḥ 
AVŚc atho balāsanāśanīḥ kṛtyādūṣaṇīś ca yās tā ihā yantv oṣadhīḥ  
AVŚa apakrītāḥ sahīyasīr vīrudho yā abhiṣṭutāḥ 
AVŚc trāyantām asmin grāme gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ paśum 
AVŚa madhuman mūlaṃ madhumad agram āsām madhuman madhyaṃ vīrudhāṃ babhūva 
AVŚc madhumat parṇaṃ madhumat puṣpam āsāṃ madhoḥ sambhaktā amṛtasya bhakṣo ghṛtam annaṃ duhratāṃ gopurogavam 
AVŚa yāvatīḥ kiyatīś cemāḥ pṛthivyām adhy oṣadhīḥ 
AVŚc tā mā sahasraparṇyo mṛtyor muñcantv aṃhasaḥ 
AVŚa vaiyāghro maṇir vīrudhāṃ trāyamāno 'bhiśastipāḥ 
AVŚc amīvāḥ sarvā rakṣāṃsy apa hantv adhi dūram asmat 
AVŚa siṃhasyeva stanathoḥ saṃ vijante 'gner iva vijante ābhṛtābhyaḥ 
AVŚc gavāṃ yakṣmaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ vīrudbhir atinutto nāvyā etu srotyāḥ 
AVŚa mumucānā oṣadhayo 'gner vaiśvānarād adhi 
AVŚc bhūmiṃ saṃtanvatīr ita yāsāṃ rājā vanaspatiḥ 
AVŚa yā rohanty āṅgirasīḥ parvateṣu sameṣu ca 
AVŚc tā naḥ payasvatīḥ śivā oṣadhīḥ santu śaṃ hṛde 
AVŚa yāś cāhaṃ veda vīrudho yāś ca paśyāmi cakṣuṣā 
AVŚc ajñātā jānīmaś ca yā yāsu vidma ca saṃbhṛtam 
AVŚa sarvāḥ samagrā oṣadhīr bodhantu vacaso mama 
AVŚc yathemaṃ pārayāmasi puruṣam duritād adhi 
AVŚa aśvattho darbho vīrudhāṃ somo rājāmṛtaṃ haviḥ 
AVŚc vrīhir yavaś ca bheṣajau divasi putrāv amartyau  
AVŚa uj jihīdhve stanayaty abhikrandaty oṣadhīḥ 
AVŚc yadā vaḥ pṛśnimātaraḥ parjanyo retasāvati 
AVŚa tasyāmṛtasyemaṃ balaṃ puruṣaṃ payayāmasi 
AVŚc atho kṛṇomi bheṣajaṃ yathāsac chatahāyanaḥ 
AVŚa varāho veda vīrudhaṃ nakulo veda bheṣajīm 
AVŚc sarpā gandharvā yā vidus tā asmā avase huve 
AVŚa yāḥ suparṇā āṅgirasīr divyā yā raghato viduḥ 
AVŚc vayāṃsi haṃsā yā vidur yās ca sarve patatriṇaḥ 
AVŚe mṛgā yā vidur oṣadhīs tā asmā avase huve 
AVŚa yāvatīnām oṣadhīnāṃ gāvaḥ prāśnanty aghnyā yavatīnām ajāvayaḥ 
AVŚc tāvatīs tubhyam oṣadhīḥ śarma yachantv ābhṛtāḥ 
AVŚa yāvatīṣu manuṣyā bheṣajaṃ bhiṣajo viduḥ 
AVŚc tāvatīr viśvabheṣajīr ā bharāmi tvām abhi 
AVŚa puṣpavatīḥ prasūmatīḥ phalinīr aphalā uta 
AVŚc saṃmātara iva duhrām asmā ariṣṭatātaye 
AVŚa ut tvāhārṣaṃ pañcaśalād atho daśaśalād uta 
AVŚc atho yamasya paḍvīśād viśvasmād devakilbiṣāt  
AVŚa indro manthatu manthitā śakraḥ śūraḥ puraṃdaraḥ 
AVŚc yathā hanāma senā amitrāṇāṃ sahasraśaḥ 
AVŚa pūtirajjur upadhmānī pūtiṃ senāṃ kṛṇotv amūm 
AVŚc dhūmam agnim parādṛśyā 'mitrā hṛtsv ā dadhatāṃ bhayam 
AVŚa amūn aśvattha niḥ śṛṇīhi khādāmūn khadirājiram 
AVŚc tājadbhaṅga iva bhajantāṃ hantv enān vadhako vadhaiḥ 
AVŚa paruṣān amūn paruṣāhvaḥ kṛṇotu hantv enān vadhako vadhaiḥ 
AVŚc kṣipraṃ śara iva bhajantāṃ bṛhajjālena saṃditāḥ 
AVŚa antarikṣaṃ jālam āsīj jāladaṇḍā diśo mahīḥ 
AVŚc tenābhidhāya dasyūnāṃ śakraḥ senām apāvapat 
AVŚa bṛhad dhi jālaṃ bṛhataḥ śakrasya vājinīvataḥ 
AVŚc tena śatrūn abhi sarvān ny ubja yathā na mucyātai katamaś canaiṣām 
AVŚa bṛhat te jālaṃ bṛhata indra śūra sahasrārghasya śatavīryasya 
AVŚc tena śataṃ sahasram ayutaṃ nyarbudaṃ jaghāna śakro dasyūnām abhidhāya senayā 
AVŚa ayaṃ loko jālam āsīc chakrasya mahato mahān 
AVŚc tenāham indrajālenāmūṃs tamasābhi dadhāmi sarvān 
AVŚa sedir ugrā vyṛddhir ārtiś cānapavācanā 
AVŚc śramas tandrīś ca mohaś ca tair amūn abhi dadhāmi sarvān 
AVŚa mṛtyave 'mūn pra yachāmi mṛtyupāśair amī sitāḥ 
AVŚc mṛtyor ye aghalā dūtās tebhya enān prati nayāmi baddhvā  
AVŚa nayatāmūn mṛtyudūtā yamadūtā apombhata 
AVŚc paraḥsahasrā hanyantāṃ tṛṇeḍhv enān matyaṃ bhavasya 
AVŚa sādhyā ekaṃ jāladaṇḍam udyatya yanty ojasā 
AVŚc rudrā ekaṃ vasava ekam ādityair eka udyataḥ 
AVŚa viśve devāḥ upariṣṭād ubjanto yantv ojasā 
AVŚc madhyena ghnanto yantu senām aṅgiraso mahīm 
AVŚa vanaspatīn vānaspatyān oṣadhīr uta vīrudhaḥ 
AVŚc dvipāc catuṣpād iṣṇāmi yathā senām amūṃ hanan 
AVŚa gandharvāpsarasaḥ sarpān devān puṇyajanān pitṝn 
AVŚc dṛṣṭān adṛṣṭān iṣṇāmi yathā senām amūṃ hanan 
AVŚa ima uptā mṛtyupāśā yān ākramya na mucyase 
AVŚc amuṣyā hantu senāyā idaṃ kūṭaṃ sahasraśaḥ 
AVŚa gharmaḥ samiddho agnināyaṃ homaḥ sahasrahaḥ 
AVŚc bhavaś ca pṛśnibāhuś ca śarva senām amūṃ hatam 
AVŚa mṛtyor āṣam ā padyantāṃ kṣudhaṃ sediṃ vadham bhayam 
AVŚc indraś cākṣujālābhyāṃ śarva senām amūṃ hatam 
AVŚa parājitāḥ pra trasatāmitrā nuttā dhāvata brahmaṇā 
AVŚc bṛhaspatipranuttānāṃ māmīṣāṃ moci kaś cana 
AVŚa ava padyantām eṣām āyudhāni mā śakan pratidhām iṣum 
AVŚc athaiṣāṃ bahu bibhyatām iṣavaḥ ghnantu marmaṇi 
AVŚa saṃ krośatām enān dyāvāpṛthivī sam antarikṣaṃ saha devatābhiḥ 
AVŚc mā jñātāraṃ mā pratiṣṭhāṃ vidanta mitho vighnānā upa yantu mṛtyum 
AVŚa diśaś catasro 'śvataryo devarathasya purodāśāḥ śaphā antarikṣam uddhiḥ 
AVŚc dyāvāpṛthivī pakṣasī ṛtavo 'bhīśavo 'ntardeśāḥ kimkarā vāk parirathyam 
AVŚa saṃvatsaro rathaḥ parivatsaro rathopastho virāḍ īṣāgnī rathamukham 
AVŚc indraḥ savyaṣṭhāś candramāḥ sārathiḥ 
AVŚa ito jayeto vi jaya saṃ jaya jaya svāhā 
AVŚc ime jayantu parāmī jayantāṃ svāhaibhyo durāhāmībhyaḥ 
AVŚe nīlalohitenāmūn abhyavatanomi  
AVŚa kutas tau jātau katamaḥ so ardhaḥ kasmāl lokāt katamasyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ 
AVŚc vatsau virājaḥ salilād ud aitāṃ tau tvā pṛchāmi katareṇa dugdhā 
AVŚa yo akrandayat salilaṃ mahitvā yoniṃ kṛtvā tribhujaṃ śayānaḥ 
AVŚc vatsaḥ kāmadugho virājaḥ sa guhā cakre tanvaḥ parācaiḥ 
AVŚa yāni trīṇi bṛhanti yeṣāṃ caturthaṃ viyunakti vācam 
AVŚc brahmainad vidyāt tapasā vipaścid yasminn ekaṃ yujyate yasminn ekam 
AVŚa bṛhataḥ pari sāmāni ṣaṣṭhāt pañcādhi nirmitā 
AVŚc bṛhad bṛhatyā nirmitaṃ kuto 'dhi bṛhatī mitā 
AVŚa bṛhatī pari mātrāyā mātur mātrādhi nirmitā 
AVŚc māyā ha jajñe māyāyā māyāyā mātalī pari 
AVŚa vaiśvānarasya pratimopari dyaur yāvad rodasī vibabādhe agniḥ 
AVŚc tataḥ ṣaṣṭhād āmuto yanti stomā ud ito yanty abhi ṣaṣṭham ahnaḥ 
AVŚa ṣaṭ tvā pṛchāma ṛṣayaḥ kaśyapeme tvaṃ hi yuktaṃ yuyukṣe yogyaṃ ca 
AVŚc virājam āhur brahmaṇaḥ pitaraṃ tāṃ no vi dhehi yatidhā sakhibhyaḥ 
AVŚa yāṃ pracyutām anu yajñāḥ pracyavanta upatiṣṭhanta upatiṣṭhamānām 
AVŚc yasyā vrate prasave yakṣam ejati sā virāṭ ṛṣayaḥ parame vyoman 
AVŚa aprāṇaiti prāṇena prāṇatīnāṃ virāṭ svarājam abhy eti paścāt 
AVŚc viśvaṃ mṛśantīm abhirūpāṃ virājaṃ paśyanti tve na tve paśyanty enām 
AVŚa ko virājo mithunatvaṃ pra veda ka ṛtūn ka u kalpam asyāḥ 
AVŚc kramān ko asyāḥ katidhā vidugdhān ko asyā dhāma katidhā vyuṣṭīḥ  
AVŚa iyam eva sā yā prathamā vyauchad āsv itarāsu carati praviṣṭā 
AVŚc mahānto asyāṃ mahimāno antar vadhūr jigāya navagaj janitrī 
AVŚa chandaḥpakṣe uṣasā pepiśāne samānaṃ yonim anu saṃ careme 
AVŚc sūryapatnī saṃ carataḥ prajānatī ketumatī ajare bhūriretasā 
AVŚa ṛtasya panthām anu tisra āgus trayo gharmā anu reta āguḥ 
AVŚc prajām ekā jinvaty ūrjam ekā rāṣṭram ekā rakṣati devayūnām 
AVŚa agnīṣomāv adadhur yā turīyāsīd yajñasya pakṣāv ṛṣayaḥ kalpayantaḥ 
AVŚc gāyatrīṃ triṣṭubhaṃ jagatīm anuṣṭubhaṃ bṛhadarkīṃ yajamānāya svar ābharantīm 
AVŚa pañca vyuṣṭīr anu pañca dohā gāṃ pañcanāmnīm ṛtavo 'nu pañca 
AVŚc pañca diśaḥ pañcadaśena kḷptās tā ekamūrdhnīr abhi lokam ekam 
AVŚa ṣaṭ jātā bhūtā prathamajā ṛtasya ṣaṭ u sāmāni ṣaṭahaṃ vahanti 
AVŚc ṣaṭyogaṃ sīram anu sāmasāma ṣaṭ āhur dyāvāpṛthivīḥ ṣaṭ urvīḥ 
AVŚa ṣaḍ āhuḥ śītān ṣaḍ u māsa uṣṇān ṛtuṃ no brūta yatamo 'tiriktaḥ 
AVŚc sapta suparṇāḥ kavayo ni ṣeduḥ sapta chandāṃsy anu sapta dīkṣāḥ 
AVŚa sapta homāḥ samidho ha sapta madhūni sapta ṛtavo ha sapta 
AVŚc saptājyāni pari bhūtam āyan tāḥ saptagṛdhrā iti śuśrumā vayam 
AVŚa sapta chandāṃsi caturuttarāṇy anyo anyasminn adhy ārpitāni 
AVŚc kathaṃ stomāḥ prati tiṣṭhanti teṣu tāni stomeṣu katham ārpitāni 
AVŚa kathaṃ gāyatrī trivṛtaṃ vy āpa kathaṃ triṣṭup pañcadaśena kalpate 
AVŚc trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭup katham ekaviṃśaḥ  
AVŚa aṣṭa jātā bhūtā prathamajā ṛtasyāṣṭendra ṛtvijo daivyā ye 
AVŚc aṣṭayonir aditir aṣṭaputrāstamīṃ rātrim abhi havyam eti 
AVŚa itthaṃ śreyo manyamānedam āgamaṃ yuṣmākaṃ sakhye aham asmi śevā 
AVŚc samānajanmā kratur asti vaḥ śivaḥ sa vaḥ sarvāḥ saṃ carati prajānan 
AVŚa aṣṭendrasya ṣaḍ yamasya ṛṣīṇāṃ sapta saptadhā 
AVŚc apo manuṣyān oṣadhīs tāṃ u pañcānu secire 
AVŚa kevalīndrāya duduhe hi gṛṣṭir vaśam pīyūṣaṃ prathamaṃ duhānā 
AVŚc athātarpayac caturaś caturdhā devān manuṣyāṃ asurān uta ṛṣīn 
AVŚa ko nu gauḥ ka ekaṛṣiḥ kim u dhāma kā āśiṣaḥ 
AVŚc yakṣam pṛthivyām ekavṛd ekartuḥ katamo nu saḥ 
AVŚa eko gaur eka ekaṛṣir ekaṃ dhāmaikadhāśiṣaḥ 
AVŚc yakṣaṃ pṛthivyām ekavṛd ekartur nāti ricyate  
AVŚa virāḍ vā idam agra āsīt tasyā jātāyāḥ sarvam abibhed iyam evedaṃ bhaviṣyatīti 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā gārhapatye ny akrāmat 
AVŚc gṛhamedhī gṛhapatir bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sāhavanīye ny akrāmat 
AVŚc yanty asya devā devahūtiṃ priyo devānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā dakṣiṇāgnau ny akrāmat 
AVŚc yajñarto dakṣiṇīyo vāsateyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā sabhāyāṃ ny akrāmat 
AVŚc yanty asya sabhāṃ sabhyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā samitau ny akrāmat 
AVŚc yanty asya samitiṃ sāmityo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sāmantraṇe ny akrāmat 
AVŚc yanty asyāmantraṇam āmantraṇīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa sod akrāmat sāntarikṣe caturdhā vikrāntātiṣṭhat 
AVŚa tāṃ devamanuṣyā abruvann iyam eva tad veda yad ubhaya upajīvememām upa hvayāmahā iti 
AVŚa tām upāhvayanta 
AVŚa ūrja ehi svadha ehi sūnṛta ehīrāvaty ehīti 
AVŚa tasyā indro vatsa āsīd gāyatry abhidhāny abhram ūdhaḥ 
AVŚa bṛhac ca rathaṃtaraṃ ca dvau stanāv āstāṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca dvau 
AVŚa oṣadhīr eva rathaṃtareṇa devā aduhran vyaco bṛhatā 
AVŚa apo vāmadevyena yajñaṃ yajñāyajñiyena 
AVŚa oṣadhīr evāsmai rathaṃtaraṃ duhe vyaco bṛhat 
AVŚa apo vāmadevyaṃ yajñaṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ya veda  
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā vanaspatīn āgachat tāṃ vanaspatayo 'ghnata sā saṃvatsare sam abhavat 
AVŚc tasmād vanaspatīnāṃ saṃvatsare vṛkṇam api rohati vṛścate 'syāpriyo bhrātṛvyo ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā pitṝn āgachat tāṃ pitaro 'ghnata sā māsi sam abhavat 
AVŚc tasmāt pitṛbhyo māsy upamāsyaṃ dadati pra pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā devān āgachat tāṃ devā aghnata sārdhamāse sam abhavat 
AVŚc tasmād devebhyo 'rdhamāse vaṣaṭ kurvanti pra devayānaṃ panthāṃ jānāti ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā manuṣyān āgachat tāṃ manuṣyā aghnata sā sadyaḥ sam abhavat 
AVŚc tasmān manuṣyebhya ubhayadyur upa haranty upāsya gṛhe haranti ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa sod akrāmat sāsurān āgachat tām asurā upāhvayanta māya ehīti 
AVŚc tasyā virocanaḥ prāhrādir vatsa āsīd ayaspātraṃ pātram 
AVŚe tāṃ dvimūrdhārtvyo 'dhok tāṃ māyām evādhok 
AVŚg tāṃ māyām asurā upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā pitṝn āgachat tāṃ pitara upāhvayanta svadha ehīti 
AVŚc tasyā yamo rājā vatsa āsīd rajatapātraṃ pātram 
AVŚe tām antako mārtyavo 'dhok tāṃ svadhām evādhok 
AVŚg tāṃ svadhāṃ pitara upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā manuṣyān āgachat tāṃ manuṣyā upāhvayanterāvaty ehīti 
AVŚc tasyā manur vaivasvato vatsa āsīt pṛthivī pātram 
AVŚe tāṃ pṛthī vainyo 'dhok tāṃ kṛṣiṃ ca sasyaṃ cādhok 
AVŚg te svadhāṃ kṛṣiṃ ca sasyaṃ ca manuṣyā upa jīvanti kṛṣṭarādhir upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā saptaṛṣīn āgachat tāṃ saptaṛṣaya upāhvayanta brahmaṇvaty ehīti 
AVŚc tasyāḥ somo rājā vatsa āsīc chandaḥ pātram 
AVŚe tāṃ bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso 'dhok tāṃ brahma ca tapaś cādhok 
AVŚg tad brahma ca tapaś ca saptaṛṣaya upa jīvanti brahmavarcasy upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā devān āgachat tāṃ devā upāhvayantorja ehīti 
AVŚc tasyā indro vatsa āsīc camasaḥ pātram 
AVŚe tāṃ devaḥ savitādhok tām ūrjām evādhok 
AVŚg tāṃ ūrjāṃ devā upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā gandharvāpsarasa āgachat tāṃ gandharvāpsarasa upāhvayanta puṇyagandha ehīti 
AVŚc tasyāś citrarathaḥ sauryavarcaso vatsa āsīt puṣkaraparṇaṃ pātram 
AVŚe tāṃ vasuruciḥ sauryavarcaso 'dhok tāṃ puṇyam eva gandham adhok 
AVŚg taṃ puṇyaṃ gandhaṃ gandharvāpsarasa upa jīvanti puṇyagandhir upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat setarajanān āgachat tām itarajanā upāhvayanta tirodha ehīti 
AVŚc tasyāḥ kubero vaiśravaṇo vatsa āsīd āmapātraṃ pātram 
AVŚe tāṃ rajatanābhiḥ kaberako 'dhok tāṃ tirodhām evādhok 
AVŚg tāṃ tirodhām atirajanā pitara upa jīvanti tiro dhatte sarvaṃ pāpmānam upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa sod akrāmat sā sarpān āgachat tāṃ sarpā upāhvayanta viṣavaty ehīti 
AVŚc tasyās takṣako vaiśaleyo vatsa āsīd alābupātraṃ pātraṃ 
AVŚe tāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭra airāvato 'dhok tāṃ viṣam evādhok 
AVŚg tad viṣaṃ sarvā upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa tad yasmā evaṃ viduṣe 'lābunābhiṣiñcet pratyāhanyāt 
AVŚa na ca pratyāhanyān manasā tvā pratyāhanmīti pratyāhanyāt 
AVŚa yat pratyāhanti viṣam eva tat pratyāhanti 
AVŚa viṣam evāsyāpriyaṃ bhrātṛvyam anuviṣicyate ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa divas pṛthivyā antarikṣāt samudrād agner vātān madhukaśā hi jajñe 
AVŚc tāṃ cāyitvāmṛtaṃ vasānāṃ hṛdbhiḥ prajāḥ prati nandanti sarvāḥ 
AVŚa mahat payo viśvarūpam asyāḥ samudrasya tvota reta āhuḥ 
AVŚc yata aiti madhukaśā rarāṇā tat prāṇas tad amṛtaṃ niviṣṭam 
AVŚa paśyanty asyāś caritaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pṛthaṅ naro bahudhā mīmāṃsamānāḥ 
AVŚc agner vātān madhukaśā hi jajñe marutām ugrā naptiḥ 
AVŚa mātādityānāṃ duhitā vasūnāṃ prāṇaḥ prajānām amṛtasya nābhiḥ 
AVŚc hiraṇyavarṇā madhukaśā ghṛtācī mahān bhargaś carati martyeṣu 
AVŚa madhoḥ kaśām ajanayanta devās tasyā garbho abhavad viśvarūpaḥ 
AVŚc taṃ jātaṃ taruṇaṃ piparti mātā sa jāto viśvā bhuvanā vi caṣṭe 
AVŚa kas taṃ pra veda ka u taṃ ciketa yo asyā hṛdaḥ kalaśaḥ somadhāno akṣitaḥ 
AVŚc brahmā sumedhāḥ so asmin madeta 
AVŚa sa tau pra veda sa u tau ciketa yāv asyāḥ stanau sahasradhārāv akṣitau 
AVŚc ūrjaṃ duhāte anapasphurantau 
AVŚa hiṅkarikratī bṛhatī vayodhā uccairghoṣābhyeti yā vratam 
AVŚc trīn gharmān abhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyuṃ payate payobhiḥ 
AVŚa yām āpīnām upasīdanty āpaḥ śākvarā vṛṣabhā ye svarājaḥ 
AVŚc te varṣanti te varṣayanti tadvide kāmam ūrjam āpaḥ 
AVŚa stanayitnus te vāk prajāpate vṛṣā śuṣmaṃ kṣipasi bhūmyām adhi 
AVŚc agner vātān madhukaśā hi jajñe marutām ugrā naptiḥ  
AVŚa yathā somaḥ prātaḥsavane aśvinor bhavati priyaḥ 
AVŚc evā me aśvinā varca ātmani dhriyatām 
AVŚa yathā somo dvitīye savana indrāgnyor bhavati priyaḥ 
AVŚc evā ma indrāgnī varca ātmani dhriyatām 
AVŚa yathā somas tṛtīye savana ṛbhūṇāṃ bhavati priyaḥ 
AVŚc evā ma ṛbhavo varca ātmani dhriyatām 
AVŚa madhu janiṣīya madhu vaṃsiṣīya 
AVŚc payasvān agna āgamaṃ taṃ mā saṃ sṛja varcasā 
AVŚa saṃ māgne varcasā sṛja saṃ prajayā sam āyuṣā 
AVŚc vidyur me asya devā indro vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ 
AVŚa yathā madhu madhukṛtaḥ saṃbharanti madhāv adhi 
AVŚc evā me aśvinā varca ātmani dhriyatām 
AVŚa yathā makṣāḥ idaṃ madhu nyañjanti madhāv adhi 
AVŚc evā me aśvinā varcas tejo balam ojaś ca dhriyatām 
AVŚa yad giriṣu parvateṣu goṣv aśveṣu yan madhu 
AVŚc surāyāṃ sicyamānāyāṃ yat tatra madhu tan mayi 
AVŚa aśvinā sāragheṇa mā madhunāṅktaṃ śubhas patī 
AVŚc yathā varcasvatīṃ vācam āvadāni janāṃ anu 
AVŚa stanayitnus te vāk prajāpate vṛṣā śuṣmaṃ kṣipasi bhūmyāṃ divi 
AVŚc tāṃ paśava upa jīvanti sarve teno seṣam ūrjaṃ piparti 
AVŚa pṛthivī daṇḍo 'ntarikṣaṃ garbho dyauḥ kaśā vidyut prakaśo hiraṇyayo binduḥ 
AVŚa yo vai kaśāyāḥ sapta madhūni veda madhumān bhavati 
AVŚc brāhmaṇaś ca rājā ca dhenuś cānaḍvāṃś ca vrīhiś ca yavaś ca madhu saptamam 
AVŚa madhumān bhavati madhumad asyāhāryaṃ bhavati 
AVŚc madhumato lokān jayati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa yad vīdhre stanayati prajāpatir eva tat prajābhyaḥ prādur bhavati 
AVŚc tasmāt prācīnopavītas tiṣṭhe prajāpate 'nu mā budhyasveti 
AVŚe anv enaṃ prajā anu prajāpatir budhyate ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa sapatnahanam ṛṣabhaṃ ghṛtena kāmaṃ śikṣāmi haviṣājyena 
AVŚc nīcaiḥ sapatnān mama padaya tvam abhiṣṭuto mahatā vīryeṇa 
AVŚa yan me manaso na priyaṃ cakṣuṣo yan me babhasti nābhinandati 
AVŚc tad duṣvapnyaṃ prati muñcāmi sapatne kāmaṃ stutvod ahaṃ bhideyam 
AVŚa duṣvapnyaṃ kāma duritaṃ ca kamāprajastām asvagatām avartim 
AVŚc ugra īśānaḥ prati muñca tasmin yo asmabhyam aṃhūraṇā cikitsāt 
AVŚa nudasva kāma pra ṇudasva kāmāvartiṃ yantu mama ye sapatnāḥ 
AVŚc teṣāṃ nuttānām adhamā tamāṃsy agne vāstūni nir daha tvam 
AVŚa sā te kāma duhitā dhenur ucyate yām āhur vācaṃ kavayo virājam 
AVŚc tayā sapatnān pari vṛṅgdhi ye mama pary enān prāṇaḥ paśavo jīvanaṃ vṛṇaktu 
AVŚa kāmasyendrasya varuṇasya rājño viṣṇor balena savituḥ savena 
AVŚc agner hotreṇa pra ṇude sapatnāṃ chambīva nāvam udakeṣu dhīraḥ 
AVŚa adhyakṣo vājī mama kāma ugraḥ kṛṇotu mahyam asapatnam eva 
AVŚc viśve devā mama nāthaṃ bhavantu sarve devā havam ā yantu ma imam 
AVŚa idam ājyaṃ ghṛtavaj juṣāṇāḥ kāmajyeṣṭhā iha mādayadhvam 
AVŚc kṛṇvanto mahyam asapatnam eva 
AVŚa indrāgnī kāma sarathaṃ hi bhūtvā nīcaiḥ sapatnān mama pādayāthaḥ 
AVŚc teṣāṃ pannānām adhamā tamāṃsy agne vāstūny anunirdaha tvam 
AVŚa jahi tvam kāma mama ye sapatnā andhā tamāṃsy ava pādayainān 
AVŚc nirindriyā arasāḥ santu sarve mā te jīviṣuḥ katamac canāhaḥ  
AVŚa avadhīt kāmo mama ye sapatnā uruṃ lokam akaran mahyam edhatum 
AVŚc mahyaṃ namantāṃ pradiśaś catasro mahyaṃ ṣaḍ urvīr ghṛtam ā vahantu 
AVŚa te 'dharāñcaḥ pra plavantāṃ chinnā naur iva bandhanāt 
AVŚc na sāyakapraṇuttānāṃ punar asti nivartanam 
AVŚa agnir yava indro yavaḥ somo yavaḥ 
AVŚc yavayāvāno devā yavayantv enam 
AVŚa asarvavīraś caratu praṇutto dveṣyo mitrānāṃ parivargyaḥ svānām 
AVŚc uta pṛthivyām ava syanti vidyuta ugro vo devaḥ pra mṛṇat sapatnān 
AVŚa cyutā ceyaṃ bṛhaty acyutā ca vidyud bibharti stanayitnūṃś ca sarvān 
AVŚc udyann ādityo draviṇena tejasā nīcaiḥ sapatnān nudatāṃ me sahasvān 
AVŚa yat te kāma śarma trivarūtham udbhu brahma varma vitatam anativyādhyaṃ kṛtam 
AVŚc tena sapatnān pari vṛṅgdhi ye mama pary enān prāṇaḥ paśavo jīvanaṃ vṛṇaktu 
AVŚa yena devā asurān prāṇudanta yenendro dasyūn adhamaṃ tamo nināya 
AVŚc tena tvaṃ kāma mama ye sapatnās tān asmāl lokāt pra ṇudasva dūram 
AVŚa yathā devā asurān prāṇudanta yathendro dasyūn adhamaṃ tamo babādhe 
AVŚc tathā tvaṃ kāma mama ye sapatnās tān asmāl lokāt pra ṇudasva dūram 
AVŚa kāmo jajñe prathamo nainaṃ devā āpuḥ pitaro na martyāḥ 
AVŚc tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛnomi 
AVŚa yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī varimṇā yāvad āpaḥ siṣyadur yāvad agniḥ 
AVŚc tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi  
AVŚa yāvatīr diśaḥ pradiśo viṣūcīr yāvatīr āśā abhicakṣaṇā divaḥ 
AVŚc tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi 
AVŚa yāvatīr bhṛṅgā jatvaḥ kurūravo yāvatīr vaghā vṛkṣasarpyo babhūvuḥ 
AVŚc tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi 
AVŚa jyāyān nimiṣato 'si tiṣṭhato jyāyānt samudrād asi kāma manyo 
AVŚc tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛnomi 
AVŚa na vai vātaś cana kāmam āpnoti nāgniḥ sūryo nota candramāḥ 
AVŚc tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi 
AVŚa yās te śivās tanvaḥ kāma bhadrā yābhiḥ satyaṃ bhavati yad vṛṇiṣe 
AVŚc tābhiṣ ṭvam asmāṃ abhisaṃviśasvānyatra pāpīr apa veśayā dhiyaḥ  
AVŚa upamitāṃ pratimitām atho parimitām uta 
AVŚc śālāyā viśvavārāyā naddhāni vi cṛtāmasi 
AVŚa yat te naddhaṃ viśvavāre pāśo granthiś ca yaḥ kṛtaḥ 
AVŚc bṛhaspatir ivāhaṃ balaṃ vācā vi sraṃsayāmi tat 
AVŚa ā yayāma saṃ babarha granthīṃś cakāra te dṛḍhān 
AVŚc parūṃṣi vidvāṃ chastevendreṇa vi cṛtāmasi 
AVŚa vaṃśānāṃ te nahanānāṃ prāṇāhasya tṛṇasya ca 
AVŚc pakṣāṇāṃ viśvavāre te naddhāni vi cṛtāmasi 
AVŚa saṃdaṃśānāṃ paladānāṃ pariṣvañjalyasya ca 
AVŚc idaṃ mānasya patnyā naddhāni vi cṛtāmasi 
AVŚa yāni te 'ntaḥ śikyāny ābedhū raṇyāya kam 
AVŚc pra te tāni cṛtāmasi śivā mānasya patni na uddhitā tanve bhava 
AVŚa havirdhānam agniśālaṃ patnīnāṃ sadanaṃ sadaḥ 
AVŚc sado devānām asi devi śāle 
AVŚa akṣum opaśaṃ vitataṃ sahasrākṣaṃ viṣūvati 
AVŚc avanaddham abhihitaṃ brahmaṇā vi cṛtāmasi 
AVŚa yas tvā śāle pratigṛhṇāti yena cāsi mitā tvam 
AVŚc ubhau mānasya patni tau jīvatāṃ jaradaṣṭī 
AVŚa amutrainam ā gachatād dṛḍhā naddhā pariṣkṛtā 
AVŚc yasyās te vicṛtāmasy aṅgamaṅgaṃ paruṣparuḥ  
AVŚa yas tvā śāle nimimāya saṃjabhāra vanaspatīn 
AVŚc prajāyai cakre tvā śāle parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ 
AVŚa namas tasmai namo dātre śālāpataye ca kṛṇmaḥ 
AVŚc namo 'gnaye pracarate puruṣāya ca te namaḥ 
AVŚa gobhyo aśvebhyo namo yac chālāyāṃ vijāyate 
AVŚc vijāvati prajāvati vi te pāśāṃś cṛtāmasi 
AVŚa agnim antaś chādayasi puruṣān paśubhiḥ saha 
AVŚc vijāvati prajāvati vi te pāśāṃś cṛtāmasi 
AVŚa antarā dyāṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca yad vyacas tena śālāṃ prati gṛhṇāmi ta imām 
AVŚc yad antarikṣaṃ rajaso vimānaṃ tat kṛṇve 'ham udaraṃ śevadhibhyaḥ 
AVŚe tena śālāṃ prati gṛhṇāmi tasmai 
AVŚa ūrjasvatī payasvatī pṛthivyāṃ nimitā mitā 
AVŚc viśvānnaṃ bibhratī śāle mā hiṃsīḥ pratigṛhṇataḥ 
AVŚa tṛṇair āvṛtā paladān vasānā rātrīva śālā jagato niveśanī 
AVŚc mitā pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhasi hastinīva padvatī 
AVŚa iṭasya te vi cṛtāmy apinaddham aporṇuvan 
AVŚc varuṇena samubjitāṃ mitraḥ prātar vy ubjatu 
AVŚa brahmaṇā śālāṃ nimitāṃ kavibhir nimitāṃ mitām 
AVŚc indrāgnī rakṣatāṃ śālām amṛtau somyaṃ sadaḥ 
AVŚa kulāye 'dhi kulāyaṃ kośe kośaḥ samubjitaḥ 
AVŚc tatra marto vi jāyate yasmād viśvaṃ prajāyate  
AVŚa yā dvipakṣā catuṣpakṣā ṣaṭpakṣā yā nimīyate 
AVŚc aṣṭāpakṣāṃ daśapakṣāṃ śālāṃ mānasya patnīm agnir garbha ivā śaye 
AVŚa pratīcīṃ tvā pratīcīnaḥ śāle praimy ahiṃsatīm 
AVŚc agnir hy antar āpaś ca ṛtasya prathamā dvāḥ 
AVŚa imā āpaḥ pra bharāmy ayakṣmā yakṣmanāśanīḥ 
AVŚc gṛhān upa pra sīdāmy amṛtena sahāgninā 
AVŚa mā naḥ pāśaṃ prati muco gurur bhāro laghur bhava 
AVŚc vadhūm iva tvā śāle yatrakāmaṃ bharāmasi 
AVŚa prācyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
AVŚa dakṣiṇāyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
AVŚa pratīcyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
AVŚa udīcyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
AVŚa dhruvāyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
AVŚa ūrdhvāyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ 
AVŚa diśodiśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ  
AVŚa sāhasras tveṣa ṛṣabhaḥ payasvān viśvā rūpāṇi vakṣaṇāsu bibhrat 
AVŚc bhadraṃ dātre yajamānāya śīkṣan bārhaspatya usriyas tantum ātān 
AVŚa apāṃ yo agne pratimā babhūva prabhūḥ sarvasmai pṛthivīva devī 
AVŚc pitā vatsānāṃ patir aghnyānāṃ sāhasre poṣe api naḥ kṛṇotu 
AVŚa pumān antarvānt sthaviraḥ payasvān vasoḥ kabandhaṃ ṛṣabho bibharti 
AVŚc tam indrāya pathibhir devayānair hutam agnir vahatu jātavedāḥ 
AVŚa pitā vatsānāṃ patir aghnyānāṃ atho pitā mahatāṃ gargarāṇām 
AVŚc vatso jarāyu pratidhuk pīyūṣa āmikṣā ghṛtaṃ tad v asya retaḥ 
AVŚa devānāṃ bhāga upanāha eṣo 'pāṃ rasa oṣadhīnāṃ ghṛtasya 
AVŚc somasya bhakṣam avṛṇīta śakro bṛhann adrir abhavad yac charīram 
AVŚa somena pūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ bibharṣi tvastā rupāṇāṃ janitā paśūnām 
AVŚc śivās te santu prajanva iha yā imā ny asmabhyaṃ svadhite yacha yā amūḥ 
AVŚa ājaṃ bibharti ghṛtam asya retaḥ sāhasraḥ poṣas tam u yajñam āhuḥ 
AVŚc indrasya rūpam ṛṣabho vasānaḥ so asmān devāḥ śiva aitu dattaḥ 
AVŚa indrasyaujo varuṇasya bāhū aśvinor aṃsau marutām iyaṃ kakut 
AVŚc bṛhaspatiṃ saṃbhṛtam etam āhur ye dhīrāsaḥ kavayo ye manīṣiṇaḥ 
AVŚa daivīr viśaḥ payasvān ā tanoṣi tvām indraṃ tvāṃ sarasvantam āhuḥ 
AVŚc sahasraṃ sa ekamukhā dadāti yo brāhmaṇa ṛṣabham ājuhoti 
AVŚa bṛhaspatiḥ savitā te vayo dadhau tvaṣṭur vāyoḥ pary ātmā ta ābhṛtaḥ 
AVŚc antarikṣe manasā tvā juhomi barhiṣ ṭe dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām  
AVŚa ya indra iva deveṣu goṣv eti vivāvadat 
AVŚc tasya ṛṣabhasyāṅgāni brahmā saṃ stautu bhadrayā 
AVŚa pārśve āstām anumatyā bhagasyāstām anūvṛjau 
AVŚc aṣṭhīvantāv abravīn mitro mamaitau kevalāv iti 
AVŚa bhasad āsīd ādityānāṃ śroṇī āstāṃ bṛhaspateḥ 
AVŚc puchaṃ vātasya devasya tena dhūnoty oṣadhīḥ 
AVŚa gudā āsant sinīvālyāḥ sūryāyās tvacam abruvan 
AVŚc utthātur abruvan pada ṛṣabhaṃ yad akalpayan 
AVŚa kroḍa āsīj jāmiśaṃsasya somasya klaśo dhṛtaḥ 
AVŚc devāḥ saṃgatya yat sarva ṛṣabhaṃ vyakalpayan 
AVŚa te kuṣṭhikāḥ saramāyai kurmebhyo adadhuḥ śaphān 
AVŚc ūbadhyam asya kītebhyaḥ śvavartebhyo adhārayan 
AVŚa śṛṅgābhyāṃ rakṣa ṛṣaty avartim hanti cakṣuṣā 
AVŚc śṛṇoti bhadraṃ karṇābhyāṃ gavāṃ yaḥ patir aghnyaḥ 
AVŚa śatayājaṃ sa yajate nainaṃ dunvanty agnayaḥ 
AVŚc jinvanti viśve taṃ devā yo brāhmaṇa ṛṣabham ājuhoti 
AVŚa brāhmaṇebhya ṛṣabhaṃ dattvā varīyaḥ kṛṇute manaḥ 
AVŚc puṣṭiṃ so aghnyānāṃ sve goṣṭhe 'va paśyate 
AVŚa gāvaḥ santu prajāḥ santv atho astu tanūbalam 
AVŚc tat sarvam anu manyantāṃ devā ṛṣabhadāyine 
AVŚa ayaṃ pipāna indra id rayiṃ dadhātu cetanīm 
AVŚc ayaṃ dhenuṃ sudughāṃ nityavatsāṃ vaśaṃ duhāṃ vipaścitaṃ paro divaḥ 
AVŚa piśaṅgarūpo nabhaso vayodhā aindraḥ śuṣmo viśvarūpo na āgan 
AVŚc āyur asmabhyaṃ dadhat prajāṃ ca rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacatām 
AVŚa upehopaparcanāsmin goṣṭha upa pṛñca naḥ 
AVŚc upa ṛṣabhasya yad reta upendra tava vīryam 
AVŚa etaṃ vo yuvānaṃ prati dadhmo atra tena krīḍantīś carata vaśāṃ anu 
AVŚc mā no hāsiṣṭa januṣā subhāgā rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacadhvam  
AVŚa ā nayaitam ā rabhasva sukṛtāṃ lokam api gachatu prajānan 
AVŚc tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā mahānty ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam 
AVŚa indrāya bhāgaṃ pari tvā nayāmy asmin yajñe yajamānāya sūrim 
AVŚc ye no dviṣanty anu tān rabhasvānāgaso yajamānasya vīrāḥ 
AVŚa pra pado 'va nenigdhi duścaritaṃ yac cacāra śuddhaiḥ śaphair ā kramatāṃ prajānan 
AVŚc tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā vipaśyann ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam 
AVŚa anuchya śyāmena tvacam etāṃ viśastar yathāparv asinā mābhi maṃsthāḥ 
AVŚc mābhi druhaḥ paruśaḥ kalpayainaṃ tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayainam 
AVŚa ṛcā kumbhīm adhy agnau śrayāmy ā siñcodakam ava dhehy enam 
AVŚc paryādhattāgninā śamitāraḥ śṛto gachatu sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ 
AVŚa ut krāmātaḥ pari ced ataptas taptāc caror adhi nākaṃ tṛtīyam 
AVŚc agner agnir adhi saṃ babhūvitha jyotiṣmantam abhi lokaṃ jayaitam 
AVŚa ajo agnir ajam u jyotir āhur ajaṃ jīvatā brahmaṇe deyam āhuḥ 
AVŚc ajas tamāṃsy apa hanti dūram asmiṃl loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ 
AVŚa pañcaudanaḥ pañcadhā vi kramatām ākraṃsyamānas trīṇi jyotīṃṣi 
AVŚc ījānānāṃ sukṛtāṃ prehi madhyaṃ tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayasva 
AVŚa ajā roha sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ śarabho na catto 'ti durgāny eṣaḥ 
AVŚc pañcaudano brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ sa dātāraṃ tṛptyā tarpayāti 
AVŚa ajas trināke tridive tripṛṣṭhe nākasya pṛṣṭhe dadivāṃsaṃ dadhāti 
AVŚc pañcaudano brahmaṇe dīyamāno viśvarūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughāsy ekā  
AVŚa etad vo jyotiḥ pitaras tṛtīyaṃ pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe 'jaṃ dadāti 
AVŚc ajas tamāṃsy apa hanti dūram asmiṃl loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ 
AVŚa ījānānāṃ sukṛtāṃ lokam īpsan pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe 'jaṃ dadāti 
AVŚc sa vyāptim abhi lokaṃ jayaitaṃ śivo 'smabhyaṃ pratigṛhīto astu 
AVŚa ajo hy agner ajaniṣṭa śokād vipro viprasya sahaso vipaścit 
AVŚc iṣṭaṃ pūrtam abhipūrtaṃ vaṣaṭkṛtaṃ tad devā ṛtuśaḥ kalpayantu 
AVŚa amotaṃ vāso dadyād dhiraṇyam api dakṣiṇām 
AVŚc tathā lokānt sam āpnoti ye divyā ye ca pārthivāḥ 
AVŚa etās tvājopa yantu dhārāḥ somyā devīr ghṛtapṛṣṭhā madhuścutaḥ 
AVŚc stabhān pṛthivīm uta dyāṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhe 'dhi saptaraśmau 
AVŚa ajo 'sy aja svargo 'si tvayā lokam aṅgirasaḥ prājānan 
AVŚc taṃ lokaṃ puṇyaṃ pra jñeṣam 
AVŚa yenā sahasraṃ vahasi yenāgne sarvavedasam 
AVŚc tenemaṃ yajñaṃ no vaha svar deveṣu gantave 
AVŚa ajaḥ pakvaḥ svarge loke dadhāti pañcaudano nirṛtiṃ bādhamānaḥ 
AVŚc tena lokānt sūryavato jayema 
AVŚa yaṃ brāhmaṇe nidadhe yaṃ ca vikṣu yā vipruṣa odanānām ajasya 
AVŚc sarvaṃ tad agne sukṛtasya loke jānītān naḥ saṃgamane pathīnām 
AVŚa ajo vā idam agne vy akramata tasyora iyam abhavad dyauḥ pṛṣṭiham 
AVŚc antarikṣaṃ madhyam diśaḥ pārśve samudrau kukṣī  
AVŚa satyaṃ ca rtaṃ ca cakṣuṣī viśvaṃ satyaṃ śraddhā prāṇo virāṭ śiraḥ 
AVŚc eṣa vā aparimito yajño yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ 
AVŚa aparimitam eva yajñam āpnoty aparimitaṃ lokam ava runddhe 
AVŚc yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti 
AVŚa nāsyāsthīni bhindyān na majjño nir dhayet 
AVŚc sarvam enaṃ samādāyedamidaṃ pra veśayet 
AVŚa idamidam evāsya rūpaṃ bhavati tenainaṃ saṃ gamayati 
AVŚc iṣaṃ maha ūrjam asmai duhe yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti 
AVŚa pañca rukmā pañca navāni vastrā pañcāsmai dhenavaḥ kāmadughā bhavanti 
AVŚc yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti 
AVŚa pañca rukmā jyotir asmai bhavanti varma vāsāṃsi tanve bhavanti 
AVŚc svargaṃ lokam aśnute yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣam dadāti 
AVŚa yā pūrvaṃ patiṃ vittvā 'thānyaṃ vindate 'param 
AVŚc pañcaudanaṃ ca tāv ajaṃ dadāto na vi yoṣataḥ 
AVŚa samānaloko bhavati punarbhuvāparaḥ patiḥ 
AVŚc yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti 
AVŚa anupūrvavatsāṃ dhenum anaḍvāham upabarhaṇam 
AVŚc vāso hiraṇyaṃ dattvā te yanti divam uttamām 
AVŚa ātmānaṃ pitaraṃ putraṃ pautraṃ pitāmaham 
AVŚc jāyāṃ janitrīṃ mātaraṃ ye priyās tān upa hvaye  
AVŚa yo vai naidāghaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda 
AVŚc eṣa vai naidāgho nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ 
AVŚe nir evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ dahati bhavaty ātmanā 
AVŚa yo vai kurvantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda 
AVŚc kurvatīṃkurvatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte 
AVŚe eṣa vai kurvan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ 
AVŚa yo vai saṃyantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda 
AVŚc saṃyatīṃsaṃyatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte 
AVŚe eṣa vai saṃyan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ 
AVŚa yo vai pinvantaṃ nāma rtum veda 
AVŚc pinvatīṃpinvatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte 
AVŚe eṣa vai pinvan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ 
AVŚa yo vā udyantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda 
AVŚc udyatīṃudyatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte 
AVŚe eṣa vā udyann nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ 
AVŚa yo vā abhibhuvaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda 
AVŚc abhibhavantīmabhibhavantīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte 
AVŚe eṣa vā abhibhūr nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ 
AVŚa ajaṃ ca pacata pañca caudanān 
AVŚc sarvā diśaḥ saṃmanasaḥ sadhrīcīḥ sāntardeśāḥ prati gṛhnantu ta etam 
AVŚa tās te rakṣantu tava tubhyam etaṃ tābhya ājyaṃ havir idaṃ juhomi  
AVŚa yo vidyād brahma pratyakṣaṃ parūṃṣi yasya saṃbhārā ṛco yasyānūkyam 
AVŚa sāmāni yasya lomāni yajur hṛdayam ucyate paristaraṇam id dhaviḥ 
AVŚa yad vā atithipatir atithīn pratipaśyati devayajanaṃ prekṣate 
AVŚa yad abhivadati dīkṣām upaiti yad udakaṃ yācaty apaḥ pra ṇayati 
AVŚa yā eva yajña āpaḥ praṇīyante tā eva tāḥ 
AVŚa yat tarpaṇam āharanti ya evāgnīṣomīyaḥ paśur badhyate sa eva saḥ 
AVŚa yad āvasathān kalpayanti sadohavirdhānāny eva tat kalpayanti 
AVŚa yad upastṛṇanti barhir eva tat 
AVŚa yad upariśayanam āharanti svargam eva tena lokam ava runddhe 
AVŚa yat kaśipūpabarhaṇam āharanti paridhaya eva te 
AVŚa yad āñjanābhyañjanam āharanty ājyam eva tat 
AVŚa yat purā pariveṣāt svādam āharanti purodāśāv eva tau 
AVŚa yad aśanakṛtaṃ hvayanti haviṣkṛtam eva tad dhvayanti 
AVŚa ye vrīhayo yavā nirupyante 'ṃśava eva te 
AVŚa yāny ulūkhalamusalāni grāvāṇa eva te 
AVŚa śūrpaṃ pavitraṃ tuṣā ṛjīṣābhiṣavaṇīr āpaḥ 
AVŚa srug darvir nekṣaṇam āyavanaṃ droṇakalaśāḥ kumbhyo vāyavyāni pātrāṇīyam eva kṛṣṇājinam  
AVŚa yajamānabrāhmaṇaṃ vā etad atithipatiḥ kurute yad āhāryāṇi prekṣata idaṃ bhūyā idām iti 
AVŚa yad āha bhūya ud dhareti prāṇam eva tena varṣīyāṃsaṃ kurute 
AVŚa upa harati havīṃṣy ā sādayati 
AVŚa teṣām āsannānām atithir ātman juhoti 
AVŚa srucā hastena prāṇe yūpe srukkāreṇa vaṣaṭkāreṇa 
AVŚa ete vai priyāś cāpriyāś ca rtvijaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayanti yad atithayaḥ 
AVŚa sa ya evaṃ vidvān na dviṣann aśnīyān na dviṣato 'nnam aśnīyān na mīmāṃsitasya na mīmāṃsamānasya 
AVŚa sarvo vā eṣa jagdhapāpmā yasyānnam aśnanti 
AVŚa sarvo vā eso 'jagdhapāpmā yasyānnam nāśnanti 
AVŚa sarvadā vā eṣa yuktagrāvārdrapavitro vitatādhvara āhṛtayajñakratur ya upaharati 
AVŚa prājāpatyo vā etasya yajño vitato ya upaharati 
AVŚa prajāpater vā eṣa vikramān anuvikramate ya upaharati 
AVŚa yo 'tithīnāṃ sa āhavanīyo yo veśmani sa gārhapatyo yasmin pacanti sa dakṣiṇāgniḥ  
AVŚa iṣṭaṃ ca vā eṣa pūrtaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti 
AVŚa payaś ca vā eṣa rasaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti 
AVŚa ūrjāṃ ca vā eṣa sphātiṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti 
AVŚa prajāṃ vā eṣa paśūṃś ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti 
AVŚa kīrtiṃ vā eṣa yaśaś ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti 
AVŚa śriyaṃ vā eṣa saṃvidaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti 
AVŚa eṣa vā atithir yac chrotriyas tasmāt pūrvo nāśnīyāt 
AVŚa aśitāvaty atithāv aśnīyād yajñasya sātmatvāya yajñasyāvichedāya tad vratam 
AVŚa etad vā u svādīyo yad adhigavaṃ kṣīraṃ vā māṃsaṃ vā tad eva nāśnīyāt  
AVŚa sa ya evaṃ vidvān kṣīram upasicyopaharati 
AVŚc yāvad agniṣṭomeneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe 
AVŚa sa ya evaṃ vidvānt sarpir upasicyopaharati 
AVŚc yāvad atirātreṇeṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe 
AVŚa sa ya evaṃ vidvān madhūpasicyopaharati 
AVŚc yāvad sattrasadyeneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe 
AVŚa sa ya evaṃ vidvān māṃsam upasicyopaharati 
AVŚc yāvad dvādaśāheneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe 
AVŚa sa ya evaṃ vidvān udakam upasicyopaharati 
AVŚc prajānāṃ prajananāya gachati pratiṣṭhāṃ priyaḥ prajānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān upasicyopaharati  
AVŚa tasmā uṣā hiṅ kṛṇoti savitā pra stauti 
AVŚc bṛhaspatir ūrjayod gāyati tvaṣṭā puṣṭyā prati harati viśve devā nidhanam 
AVŚe nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa tasmā udyant sūryo hiṅ kṛṇoti saṃgavaḥ pra stauti 
AVŚc madhyandina ud gāyaty aparāhṇaḥ prati haraty astaṃyan nidhanam 
AVŚe nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa tasmā abhro bhavan hiṅ kṛṇoti stanayan pra stauti 
AVŚc vidyotamānaḥ prati harati varṣann ud gāyaty udgṛhṇan nidhanam 
AVŚe nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda 
AVŚa atithīn prati paśyati hiṅ kṛṇoty abhi vadati pra stauty udakam yācaty ud gāyati 
AVŚc upa harati prati haraty ucchiṣṭaṃ nidhanam 
AVŚe nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evam veda  
AVŚa yat kṣattāraṃ hvayaty ā śrāvayaty eva tat 
AVŚa yat pratiśṛṇoti pratyāśrāvayaty eva tat 
AVŚa yat pariveṣṭāraḥ pātrahastāḥ pūrve cāpare ca prapadyante camasādhvaryava eva te 
AVŚa teṣāṃ na kaś canāhotā 
AVŚa yad vā atithipatir atithīn pariviṣya gṛhān upodaity avabhṛtham eva tad upāvaiti 
AVŚa yat sabhāgayati dakṣiṇāḥ sabhāgayati yad anutiṣṭhata udavasyaty eva tat 
AVŚa sa upahūtaḥ pṛthivyāṃ bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yat pṛthivyāṃ viśvarūpam 
AVŚa sa upahūto 'ntarikṣe bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam 
AVŚa sa upahūto divi bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam 
AVŚa sa upahūto deveṣu bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam 
AVŚa sa upahūto lokeṣu bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam 
AVŚa sa upahūta upahūtaḥ 
AVŚa āpnotīmaṃ lokam āpnoty amum 
AVŚa jyotiṣmato lokān jayati ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa prajāpatiś ca parameṣṭhī ca śṛṅge indraḥ śiro agnir lalāṭaṃ yamaḥ kṛkāṭam 
AVŚa somo rājā mastiṣko dyaur uttarahanuḥ pṛthivy adharahanuḥ 
AVŚa vidyuj jihvā maruto dantā revatir grīvāḥ kṛttikā skandhā gharmo vahaḥ 
AVŚa viśvaṃ vāyuḥ svargo lokaḥ kṛṣṇadraṃ vidharaṇī niveṣyaḥ 
AVŚa śyenaḥ kroto 'ntarikṣaṃ pājasyaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ kakud bṛhatīḥ kīkasāḥ 
AVŚa devānāṃ patnīḥ pṛṣṭaya upasadaḥ parśavaḥ 
AVŚa mitraś ca varuṇaś cāṃsau tvaṣṭā cāryamā ca doṣaṇī mahādevo bāhū 
AVŚa indrāṇī bhasad vāyuḥ puchaṃ pavamāno bālāḥ 
AVŚa brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca śroṇī balam ūrū 
AVŚa dhātā ca savitā cāṣṭhīvantau jaṅghā gandharvā apsarasaḥ kuṣṭhikā aditiḥ śaphāḥ 
AVŚa ceto hṛdayaṃ yakṛn medhā vrataṃ purītat 
AVŚa kṣut kukṣir irā vaniṣṭhuḥ parvatāḥ plāśayaḥ 
AVŚa krodho vṛkkau manyur āṇḍau prajā śepaḥ 
AVŚa nadī sūtrī varṣasya pataya stanā stanayitnur ūdhaḥ 
AVŚa viśvavyacās carmauṣadhayo lomāni nakṣatrāṇi rūpam 
AVŚa devajanā gudā manuṣyā āntrāṇy atrā udaram 
AVŚa rakṣāṃsi lohitam itarajanā ūbadhyam 
AVŚa abhraṃ pībo majjā nidhanam 
AVŚa agnir āsīna utthito 'śvinā 
AVŚa indraḥ prāṅ tiṣṭhan dakṣiṇā tiṣṭhan yamaḥ 
AVŚa pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan dhātodaṅ tiṣṭhant savitā 
AVŚa tṛṇāni prāptaḥ somo rājā 
AVŚa mitra īkṣamāṇa āvṛtta ānandaḥ 
AVŚa yujyamāno vaiśvadevo yuktaḥ prajāpatir vimuktaḥ sarvam 
AVŚa etad vai viśvarūpaṃ sarvarūpaṃ gorūpam 
AVŚa upainaṃ viśvarūpāḥ sarvarūpāḥ paśavas tiṣṭhanti ya evaṃ veda  
AVŚa śīrṣaktiṃ śīrṣāmayaṃ karṇaśūlaṃ vilohitam 
AVŚc sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa karṇābhyāṃ te kaṅkūṣebhyaḥ karṇaśūlaṃ visalpakam 
AVŚc sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa yasya hetoḥ pracyavate yakṣmaḥ karṇato āsyataḥ 
AVŚc sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa yaḥ kṛṇoti pramotam andhaṃ kṛṇoti pūruṣam 
AVŚc sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa aṅgabhedam aṅgajvaram viśvāṅgyaṃ visalpakam 
AVŚc sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa yasya bhīmaḥ pratīkāśa udvepayati pūruṣam 
AVŚc takmānaṃ viśvaśāradaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa ya ūrū anusarpaty atho eti gavīnike 
AVŚc yakṣmaṃ te antar aṅgebhyo bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa yadi kāmād apakāmād dhṛdayāj jāyate pari 
AVŚc hṛdo balāsam aṅgebhyo bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa harimāṇaṃ te aṅgebhyo 'pvām antarodarāt 
AVŚc yakṣmodhām antar ātmano bahir nir mantrayāmahe 
AVŚa āso balāso bhavatu mūtraṃ bhavatv āmayat 
AVŚc yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat  
AVŚa bahir bilaṃ nir dravatu kāhābāhaṃ tavodarāt 
AVŚc yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat 
AVŚa udarāt te klomno nābhyā hṛdayād adhi 
AVŚc yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat 
AVŚa yāḥ sīmānaṃ virujanti mūrdhānaṃ praty arṣanīḥ 
AVŚc ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam 
AVŚa yā hṛdayam uparṣanty anutanvanti kīkasāḥ 
AVŚc ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam 
AVŚa yāḥ pārśve uparṣanty anunikṣanti pṛṣṭīḥ 
AVŚc ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam 
AVŚa yās tiraścīḥ uparṣanty arṣaṇīr vakṣaṇāsu te 
AVŚc ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam 
AVŚa yā gudā anusarpanty āntrāṇi mohayanti ca 
AVŚc ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam 
AVŚa yā majjño nirdhayanti parūṃṣi virujanti ca 
AVŚc ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam 
AVŚa ye aṅgāni madayanti yakṣmāso ropaṇās tava 
AVŚc yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat 
AVŚa visalpasya vidradhasya vātīkārasya vālajeḥ 
AVŚc yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat 
AVŚa pādābhyāṃ te jānubhyāṃ śroṇibhyāṃ pari bhaṃsasaḥ 
AVŚc anūkād arṣaṇīr uṣṇihābhyaḥ śīrṣṇo rogam anīnaśam 
AVŚa saṃ te śīrṣṇaḥ kapālāni hṛdayasya ca yo vidhuḥ 
AVŚc udyann āditya raśmibhiḥ śīrṣṇo rogam anīnaśo 'ṅgabhedam aśīśamaḥ  
AVŚa asya vāmasya palitasya hotus tasya bhrātā madhyamo asty aśnaḥ 
AVŚc tṛtīyo bhrātā ghṛtapṛṣṭho asyātrāpaśyaṃ viśpatiṃ saptaputram 
AVŚa sapta yuñjanti ratham ekacakram eko aśvo vahati saptanāmā 
AVŚc trinābhi cakram ajaram anarvaṃ yatremā viśvā bhuvanādhi tasthuḥ 
AVŚa imaṃ ratham adhi ye sapta tasthuḥ saptacakraṃ sapta vahanty aśvāḥ 
AVŚc sapta svasāro abhi saṃ navanta yatra gavām nihitā sapta nāma 
AVŚa ko dadarśa prathamaṃ jāyamānam asthanvantaṃ yad anasthā bibharti 
AVŚc bhūmyā asur asṛg ātmā kva svit ko vidvāṃsam upa gāt praṣṭum etat 
AVŚa iha bravītu ya īm aṅga vedāsya vāmasya nihitaṃ padaṃ veḥ 
AVŚc śīrṣṇaḥ kṣīraṃ duhrate gāvo asya vavriṃ vasānā udakaṃ padā 'puḥ 
AVŚa pākaḥ pṛchāmi manasā 'vijānan devānām enā nihitā padāni 
AVŚc vatse baṣkaye 'dhi sapta tantūn vi tatnire kavaya otavā u 
AVŚa acikitvāṃs cikituṣaś cid atra kavīn pṛchāmi vidvano na vidvān 
AVŚc vi yas tastambha ṣaṭ imā rajāṃsy ajasya rūpe kiṃ api svid ekam 
AVŚa mātā pitaram ṛta ā babhāja 'dhīty agre manasā saṃ hi jagme 
AVŚc sā bībhatsur garbharasā nividdhā namasvanta id upavākam īyuḥ 
AVŚa yuktā mātāsid dhuri dakṣiṇāyā atiṣṭhad garbho vṛjanīṣv antaḥ 
AVŚc amīmed vatso anu gām apaśyad viśvarūpyaṃ triṣu yoganeṣu 
AVŚa tisro matṝs trīn pitṝn bibhrad eka urdhvas tasthau nem ava glāpayanta 
AVŚc mantrayante divo amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśvavido vācam aviśvavinnām  
AVŚa pañcāre cakre parivartamāne yasminn ātasthur bhuvanāni viśvā 
AVŚc tasya nākṣas tapyate bhūribhāraḥ sanād eva na chidyate sanābhiḥ 
AVŚa pañcapādaṃ pitaraṃ dvādaśākṛtiṃ diva āhuḥ pare ardhe purīṣiṇam 
AVŚc atheme anya upare vicakṣaṇe saptacakre ṣaḍara āhur arpitam 
AVŚa dvādaśāraṃ nahi taj jarāya varvarti cakraṃ pari dyām ṛtasya 
AVŚc ā putrā agne mithunāso atra sapta śatāni viṃśatiś ca tasthuḥ 
AVŚa sanemi cakram ajaraṃ vi vavṛta uttānāyāṃ daśa yuktā vahanti 
AVŚc sūryasya cakṣū rajasaity āvṛtaṃ yasminn ātasthur bhuvanāni viśvā 
AVŚa striyaḥ satīs tām u me puṃsaḥ āhuḥ paśyad akṣaṇvānn vi cetad andhaḥ 
AVŚc kavir yaḥ putraḥ sa īm ā ciketa yas tā vijānāt sa pituṣ pitāsat 
AVŚa sākaṃjānāṃ saptatham āhur ekajaṃ ṣaḍ id yamā ṛṣayo devajā iti 
AVŚc teṣām iṣṭāni vihitāni dhāmaśa sthātre rejante vikṛtāni rūpaśaḥ 
AVŚa avaḥ pareṇa para enā avareṇa padā vatsaṃ bibhratī gaur ud asthāt 
AVŚc sā kadrīcī kaṃ svid ardhaṃ parāgāt kva svit sūte nahi yūthe asmin 
AVŚa avaḥ pareṇa pitaraṃ yo asya vedāvaḥ pareṇa para enāvareṇa 
AVŚc kavīyamānaḥ ka iha pra vocad devaṃ manaḥ kuto adhi prajātam 
AVŚa ye arvāñcas tām u parāca āhur ye parāñcas tāṃ u arvāca āhuḥ 
AVŚc indraś ca yā cakrathuḥ soma tāni dhurā na yuktā rajaso vahanti 
AVŚa dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānaṃ vṛkṣaṃ pari ṣasvajāte 
AVŚc tayor anyaḥ pippalaṃ svādv atty anaśnann anyo abhi cākaśīti 
AVŚa yasmin vṛkṣe madhvadaḥ suparṇā niviśante suvate cādhi viśve 
AVŚc tasya yad āhuḥ pippalaṃ svādv agre tan non naśad yaḥ pitaraṃ na veda 
AVŚa yatrā suparṇā amṛtasya bhakṣam animeṣaṃ vidathābhisvaranti 
AVŚc enā viśvasya bhuvanasya gopāḥ sa mā dhīraḥ pākam atrā viveśa  
AVŚa yad gāyatre adhi gāyatram āhitaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ vā traiṣṭubhān niratakṣata 
AVŚc yad vā jagaj jagaty āhitaṃ padaṃ ya it tad vidus te amṛtatvam ānuśuḥ 
AVŚa gāyatreṇa prati mimīte arkam arkeṇa sāma traiṣṭubhena vākam 
AVŚc vākena vākaṃ dvipadā catuṣpadākṣareṇa mimate sapta vāṇīḥ 
AVŚa jagatā sindhuṃ divy askabhāyad rathaṃtare sūryaṃ pary apaśyat 
AVŚc gāyatrasya samidhas tisra āhus tato mahnā pra ririce mahitvā 
AVŚa upa hvaye sudughāṃ dhenum etāṃ suhasto godhug uta dohad enām 
AVŚc śreṣṭhaṃ savaṃ savitā sāviṣan no 'bhīddho gharmas tad u ṣu pra vocat 
AVŚa hiṅkṛṇvatī vasupatnī vasūnāṃ vatsam ichantī manasābhyāgāt 
AVŚc duhām aśvibhyāṃ payo aghnyeyaṃ sā vardhatāṃ mahate saubhagāya 
AVŚa gaur amīmed abhi vatsaṃ miṣantaṃ mūrdhānaṃ hiṅṅ akṛṇon mātavā u 
AVŚc sṛkvāṇaṃ gharmam abhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyuṃ payate payobhiḥ 
AVŚa ayaṃ sa śiṅkte yena gaur abhivṛtā mimāti mayuṃ dhvasanāv adhi śritā 
AVŚc sā cittibhir ni hi cakāra martyān vidyud bhavantī prati vavrim auhata 
AVŚa anac chaye turagātu jīvam ejad dhruvaṃ madhya ā pastyānām 
AVŚc jīvo mṛtasya carati svadhābhir amartyo martyenā sayoniḥ 
AVŚa vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe yuvānaṃ santaṃ palito jagāra 
AVŚc devasya paśya kāvyaṃ mahitvādya mamāra sa hyaḥ sam āna 
AVŚa ya īṃ cakāra na so asya veda ya īṃ dadarśa hirug in nu tasmāt 
AVŚc sa mātur yonā parivīto antar bahuprajā nirṛtir ā viveśa  
AVŚa apaśyaṃ gopām anipadyamānam ā ca parā ca pathibhiś carantam 
AVŚc sa sadhrīcīḥ sa viṣūcīr vasāna ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣv antaḥ 
AVŚa dyaur naḥ pitā janitā nābhir atra bandhur no mātā pṛthivī mahīyam 
AVŚc uttānayoś camvor yonir antar atrā pitā duhitur garbham ādhāt 
AVŚa pṛchāmi tvā param antaṃ pṛthivyāḥ pṛchāmi vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ 
AVŚc pṛchāmi viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhiṃ pṛchāmi vācaḥ paramaṃ vyoma 
AVŚa iyaṃ vediḥ paro antaḥ pṛthivyā ayaṃ somo vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ 
AVŚc ayaṃ yajño viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhir brahmāyaṃ vācaḥ paramaṃ vyoma 
AVŚa na vi jānāmi yad ivedam asmi niṇyaḥ saṃnaddho manasā carāmi 
AVŚc yadā māgan prathamajā ṛtasyād id vāco aśnuve bhāgam asyāḥ 
AVŚa apāṅ prāṅ eti svadhayā gṛbhīto 'martyo martyenā sayoniḥ 
AVŚc tā śaśvantā viṣūcīnā viyantā ny anyaṃ cikyur na ni cikyur anyam 
AVŚa saptārdhagarbhā bhuvanasya reto viṣṇos tiṣṭhanti pradiśā vidharmaṇi 
AVŚc te dhītibhir manasā te vipaścitaḥ paribhuvaḥ pari bhavanti viśvataḥ 
AVŚa ṛco akṣare parame vyoman yasmin devā adhi viśve niṣeduḥ 
AVŚc yas tan na veda kim ṛcā kariṣyati ya it tad vidus te amī sam āsate 
AVŚa ṛcaḥ padaṃ mātrayā kalpayanto 'rdharcena cakḷpur viśvam ejat 
AVŚc tripād brahma pururūpaṃ vi taṣṭhe tena jīvanti pradiśaś catasraḥ 
AVŚa sūyavasād bhagavatī hi bhūyā adhā vayaṃ bhagavantaḥ syāma 
AVŚc addhi tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīṃ piba śuddham udakam ācarantī  
AVŚa gaur in mimāya salilāni takṣatī ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpadī 
AVŚc aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī sahasrākṣarā bhuvanasya paṅktis tasyāḥ samudrā adhi vi kṣaranti 
AVŚa kṛṣṇaṃ niyānaṃ harayaḥ suparṇā apo vasānā divam ut patanti 
AVŚc taṃ āvavṛtrant sadanād ṛtasyād id ghṛtena pṛthivīṃ vy ūduḥ 
AVŚa apād eti prathamā padvatīnāṃ kas tad vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā ciketa 
AVŚc garbho bhāraṃ bharaty ā cid asyā ṛtaṃ piparti anṛtaṃ ni pāti 
AVŚa virāḍ vāg virāṭ pṛthivī virāḍ antarikṣaṃ virāṭ prajāpatiḥ 
AVŚc virāṇ mṛtyuḥ sādhyānām adhirājo babhūva tasya bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ vaśe sa me bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ vaśe kṛṇotu 
AVŚa śakamayaṃ dhūmam ārād apaśyaṃ viṣūvatā para enāvareṇa 
AVŚc ukṣāṇaṃ pṛśnim apacanta vīrās tāni dharmāṇi prathamāny āsan 
AVŚa trayaḥ keśina ṛtuthā vi cakṣate saṃvatsare vapata eka eṣām 
AVŚc viśvam anyo abhicaṣṭe śacībhir dhrājir ekasya dadṛśe na rūpam 
AVŚa catvāri vāk parimitā padāni tāni vidur brāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ 
AVŚc guhā trīṇi nihitā neṅgayanti turīyaṃ vāco manuṣyā vadanti 
AVŚa indraṃ mitraṃ varuṇam agnim āhur atho divyaḥ sa suparṇo garutmān 
AVŚc ekaṃ sad viprā bahudhā vadanty agniṃ yamaṃ mātariśvānam āhuḥ  
AVŚa yāṃ kalpayanti vahatau vadhūm iva viśvarūpāṃ hastakṛtāṃ cikitsavaḥ 
AVŚc sārād etv apa nudāma enām 
AVŚa śīrṣaṇvatī nasvatī karṇiṇī kṛtyākṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśvarūpā 
AVŚc sārād etv apa nudāma enām 
AVŚa śūdrakṛtā rājakṛtā strīkṛtā brahmabhiḥ kṛtā 
AVŚc jāyā patyā nutteva kartāraṃ bandhv ṛchatu 
AVŚa anayāham oṣadhyā sarvāḥ kṛtyā adūduṣam 
AVŚc yāṃ kṣetre cakrur yāṃ goṣu yāṃ vā te puruṣeṣu 
AVŚa agham astv aghakṛte śapathaḥ śapathīyate 
AVŚc pratyak pratiprahiṇmo yathā kṛtyākṛtaṃ hanat 
AVŚa pratīcīna āṅgiraso 'dhyakṣo naḥ purohitaḥ 
AVŚc pratīcīḥ kṛtyā ākṛtyāmūn kṛtyākṛto jahi 
AVŚa yas tvovāca parehīti pratikūlam udāyyam 
AVŚc taṃ kṛtye 'bhinivartasva māsmān icho anāgasaḥ 
AVŚa yas te parūṃṣi saṃdadhau rathasyeva rbhur dhiyā 
AVŚc taṃ gacha tatra te 'yanam ajñātas te 'yaṃ janaḥ 
AVŚa ye tvā kṛtvālebhire vidvalā abhicāriṇaḥ 
AVŚc śaṃbhv idaṃ kṛtyādūṣaṇaṃ prativartma punaḥsaraṃ tena tvā snapayāmasi 
AVŚa yad durbhagāṃ prasnapitāṃ mṛtavatsām upeyima 
AVŚc apaitu sarvaṃ mat pāpaṃ draviṇaṃ mopa tiṣṭhatu  
AVŚa yat te pitṛbhyo dadato yajñe vā nāma jagṛhuḥ 
AVŚc saṃdeśyāt sarvasmāt pāpād imā muñcantu tvauṣadhīḥ 
AVŚa devainasāt pitryān nāmagrāhāt saṃdeśyād abhiniṣkṛtāt 
AVŚc muñcantu tvā vīrudho vīryeṇa brahmaṇā ṛgbhiḥ payasā ṛṣīṇām 
AVŚa yathā vātaś cyāvayati bhūmyā reṇum antarikṣāc cābhram 
AVŚc evā mat sarvaṃ durbhūtaṃ brahmanuttam apāyati 
AVŚa apa krāma nānadatī vinaddhā gardabhīva 
AVŚc kartṝn nakṣasveto nuttā brahmaṇā vīryāvatā 
AVŚa ayaṃ panthāḥ kṛtyeti tvā nayāmo 'bhiprahitāṃ prati tvā pra hiṇmaḥ 
AVŚc tenābhi yāhi bhañjaty anasvatīva vāhinī viśvarūpā kurūtinī 
AVŚa parāk te jyotir apathaṃ te arvāg anyatrāsmad ayanā kṛṇuṣva 
AVŚc pareṇehi navatiṃ nāvyā ati durgāḥ srotyā mā kṣaṇiṣṭhāḥ parehi 
AVŚa vāta iva vṛkṣān ni mṛṇīhi pādaya mā gām aśvaṃ puruṣam uc chiṣa eṣām 
AVŚc kartṝn nivṛtyetaḥ kṛtye 'prajāstvāya bodhaya 
AVŚa yāṃ te barhiṣi yāṃ śmaśāne kṣetre kṛtyāṃ valagaṃ vā nicakhnuḥ 
AVŚc agnau vā tvā gārhapatye 'bhiceruḥ pākaṃ santaṃ dhīratarā anāgasam 
AVŚa upāhṛtam anubuddhaṃ nikhātaṃ vairaṃ tsāry anv avidāma kartram 
AVŚc tad etu yata ābhṛtaṃ tatrāśva iva vi vartatāṃ hantu kṛtyākṛtaḥ prajām 
AVŚa svāyasā asayaḥ santi no gṛhe vidmā te kṛtye yatidhā parūṃṣi 
AVŚc ut tiṣṭhaiva parehīto 'jñāte kim ihechasi  
AVŚa grīvās te kṛtye pādau cāpi kartsyāmi nir drava 
AVŚc indrāgnī asmān rakṣatāṃ yau prajānāṃ prajāvatī 
AVŚa somo rājādhipā mṛḍitā ca bhūtasya naḥ patayo mṛḍayantu 
AVŚa bhavāśarvāv asyatāṃ pāpakṛte kṛtyākṛte 
AVŚc duṣkṛte vidyutaṃ devahetim 
AVŚa yady eyatha dvipadī catuṣpadī kṛtyākṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśvarūpā 
AVŚc seto 'ṣṭāpadī bhūtvā punaḥ parehi duchune 
AVŚa abhyaktāktā svaraṃkṛtā sarvaṃ bharantī duritaṃ parehi 
AVŚc jānīhi kṛtye kartāraṃ duhiteva pitaraṃ svam 
AVŚa parehi kṛtye mā tiṣṭho viddhasyeva padaṃ naya 
AVŚc mṛgaḥ sa mṛgayus tvaṃ na tvā nikartum arhati 
AVŚa uta hanti pūrvāsinaṃ pratyādāyāpara iṣvā 
AVŚc uta pūrvasya nighnato ni hanty aparaḥ prati 
AVŚa etad dhi śṛṇu me vaco 'thehi yata eyatha 
AVŚc yas tvā cakāra taṃ prati 
AVŚa anāgohatyā vai bhīmā kṛtye mā no gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ vadhīḥ 
AVŚc yatrayatrāsi nihitā tatas tvot thāpayāmasi parṇāl laghīyasī bhava 
AVŚa yadi stha tamasāvṛtā jālenabhihitā iva 
AVŚc sarvāḥ saṃlupyetaḥ kṛtyāḥ punaḥ kartre pra hiṇmasi 
AVŚa kṛtyākṛto valagino 'bhiniṣkāriṇaḥ prajām 
AVŚc mṛṇīhi kṛtye moc chiṣo 'mūn kṛtyākṛto jahi 
AVŚa yathā sūryo mucyate tamasas pari rātriṃ jahāty uṣasaśca ketūn 
AVŚc evāhaṃ sarvaṃ durbhūtaṃ kartraṃ kṛtyākṛtā kṛtaṃ hastīva rajo duritaṃ jahāmi  
AVŚa kena pārṣṇī ābhṛte pūruṣasya kena māṃsaṃ saṃbhṛtaṃ kena gulphau 
AVŚc kenāṅgulīḥ peśanīḥ kena khāni kenocchlaṅkhau madhyataḥ kaḥ pratiṣṭhām 
AVŚa kasmān nu gulphāv adharāv akṛṇvann aṣṭhīvantāv uttarau puruṣasya 
AVŚc jaṅghe nirṛtya ny adadhuḥ kva svij jānunoḥ saṃdhī ka u tac ciketa 
AVŚa catuṣṭayaṃ yujate saṃhitāntaṃ jānubhyām ūrdhvaṃ śithiraṃ kabandham 
AVŚc śroṇī yad ūrū ka u taj jajāna yābhyāṃ kusindhaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ babhūva 
AVŚa kati devāḥ katame ta āsan ya uro grīvāś cikyuḥ puruṣasya 
AVŚc kati stanau vy adadhuḥ kaḥ kaphodau kati skandhān kati pṛṣṭīr acinvan 
AVŚa ko asya bāhū sam abharad vīryāṃ karavād iti 
AVŚc aṃsau ko asya tad devaḥ kusindhe adhy ā dadhau 
AVŚa kaḥ sapta khāni vi tatarda śīrṣaṇi karṇāv imau nāsike cakṣaṇī mukham 
AVŚc yeṣāṃ purutrā vijayasya mahnani catuṣpādo dvipado yanti yāmam 
AVŚa hanvor hi jihvām adadhāt purūcīm adhā mahīm adhi śiśrāya vācam 
AVŚc sa ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣv antar apo vasānaḥ ka u tac ciketa 
AVŚa mastiṣkam asya yatamo lalātaṃ kakāṭikāṃ prathamo yaḥ kapālam 
AVŚc citvā cityaṃ hanvoḥ pūruṣasya divaṃ ruroha katamaḥ sa devaḥ 
AVŚa priyāpriyāṇi bahulā svapnaṃ saṃbādhatandyaḥ 
AVŚc ānandān ugro nandāṃś ca kasmād vahati pūruṣaḥ 
AVŚa ārtir avartir nirṛtiḥ kuto nu puruṣe 'matiḥ 
AVŚc rāddhiḥ samṛddhir avyṛddhir matir uditayaḥ kutaḥ  
AVŚa ko asminn āpo vy adadhāt viṣūvṛtaḥ purūvṛtaḥ sindhusṛtyāya jātāḥ 
AVŚc tīvrā aruṇā lohinīs tāmradhūmrā ūrdhvā avācīḥ puruṣe tiraścīḥ 
AVŚa ko asmin rūpam adadhāt ko mahmānaṃ ca nāma ca 
AVŚc gātuṃ ko asmin kaḥ ketuṃ kaś caritrāni puruṣe 
AVŚa ko asmin prāṇaṃ avayat ko apānaṃ vyānam u 
AVŚc samānam asmin ko devo 'dhi śiśrāya puruṣe 
AVŚa ko asmin yajñam adadhād eko devo 'dhi puruṣe 
AVŚc ko asmint satyaṃ ko 'nṛtaṃ kuto mṛtyuḥ kuto 'mṛtam 
AVŚa ko asmai vāsaḥ pary adadhāt ko asyāyur akalpayat 
AVŚc balaṃ ko asmai prāyachat ko asyākalpayaj javam 
AVŚa kenāpo anv atanuta kenāhar akarod ruce 
AVŚc uṣasaṃ kenānv ainddha kena sāyaṃbhavaṃ dade 
AVŚa ko asmin reto ny adadhāt tantur ā tāyatām iti 
AVŚc medhāṃ ko asminn adhy auhat ko bāṇaṃ ko nṛto dadhau 
AVŚa kenemāṃ bhūmim aurṇot kena pary abhavad divam 
AVŚc kenābhi mahnā parvatān kena karmāṇi puruṣaḥ 
AVŚa kena parjanyam anv eti kena somaṃ vicakṣaṇam 
AVŚc kena yajñam ca śraddhāṃ ca kenāsmin nihitaṃ manaḥ 
AVŚa kena śrotriyam āpnoti kenemaṃ parameṣṭhinam 
AVŚc kenemam agniṃ pūruṣaḥ kena saṃvatsaraṃ mame  
AVŚa brahma śrotriyam āpnoti brahmemaṃ parameṣṭhinam 
AVŚc brahmemam agniṃ pūruṣo brahma saṃvatsaraṃ mame 
AVŚa kena devāṃ anu kṣiyati kena daivajanīr viśaḥ 
AVŚc kenedam anyan nakṣatraṃ kena sat kṣatram ucyate 
AVŚa brahma devāṃ anu kṣiyati brahma daivajanīr viśaḥ 
AVŚc brahmedam anyan nakṣatraṃ brahma sat kṣatram ucyate 
AVŚa keneyaṃ bhūmir vihitā kena dyaur uttarā hitā 
AVŚc kenedam ūrdhvaṃ tiryak cāntarikṣam vyaco hitam 
AVŚa brahmaṇā bhūmir vihitā brahma dyaur uttarā hitā 
AVŚc brahmedam ūrdhvaṃ tiryak cāntarikṣaṃ vyaco hitam 
AVŚa mūrdhānam asya saṃsīvyātharvā hṛdayaṃ ca yat 
AVŚc mastiṣkād ūrdhvaḥ prairayat pavamāno 'dhi śīrṣataḥ 
AVŚa tad vā atharvaṇaḥ śiro devakośaḥ samubjitaḥ 
AVŚc tat prāṇo abhi rakṣati śiro annam atho manaḥ 
AVŚa ūrdhvo nu sṛṣṭās tiryaṅ nu sṛṣṭās sarvā diśaḥ puruṣa ā babhūvāṃ 
AVŚc puraṃ yo brahmaṇo veda yasyāḥ puruṣa ucyate 
AVŚa yo vai tāṃ brahmaṇo vedāmṛtenāvṛtāṃ puram 
AVŚc tasmai brahma ca brāhmāś ca cakṣuḥ prāṇaṃ prajāṃ daduḥ 
AVŚa na vai tam cakṣur jahāti na prāṇo jarasaḥ purā 
AVŚc puraṃ yo brahmaṇo veda yasyāḥ puruṣa ucyate 
AVŚa aṣṭācakrā navadvārā devānāṃ pūr ayodhyā 
AVŚc tasyāṃ hiraṇyayaḥ kośaḥ svargo jyotiṣāvṛtaḥ 
AVŚa tasmin hiraṇyaye kośe tryare tripratiṣṭhite 
AVŚc tasmin yad yakṣam ātmanvat tad vai brahmavido viduḥ 
AVŚa prabhrājamānāṃ hariṇīṃ yaśasā saṃparīvṛtām 
AVŚc puraṃ hiraṇyayīṃ brahmā viveśāparājitām  
AVŚa ayaṃ me varaṇo maṇiḥ sapatnakṣayaṇo vṛṣā 
AVŚc tenā rabhasva tvaṃ śatrūn pra mṛṇīhi durasyataḥ 
AVŚa praiṇān chṛṇīhi pra mṛṇā rabhasva maṇis te astu puraetā purastāt 
AVŚc avārayanta varaṇena devā abhyācāram asurāṇāṃ śvaḥśvaḥ 
AVŚa ayaṃ maṇir varaṇo viśvabheṣajaḥ sahasrākṣo harito hiraṇyayaḥ 
AVŚc sa te śatrūn adharān pādayāti pūrvas tān dabhnuhi ye tvā dviṣanti 
AVŚa ayaṃ te kṛtyāṃ vitatām pauruṣeyād ayaṃ bhayāt 
AVŚc ayaṃ tvā sarvasmāt pāpād varaṇo vārayiṣyate 
AVŚa varaṇo vārayātā ayaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ 
AVŚc yakṣmo yo asminn āviṣṭas tam u devā avīvaran 
AVŚa svapnaṃ suptvā yadi paśyāsi pāpaṃ mṛgaḥ sṛtiṃ yati dhāvād ajuṣṭām 
AVŚc parikṣavāc chakuneḥ pāpavādād ayaṃ maṇir varaṇo vārayiṣyate 
AVŚa arātyās tvā nirṛtyā abhicārād atho bhayāt 
AVŚc mṛtyor ojīyaso vadhād varaṇo vārayiṣyate 
AVŚa yan me mātā yan me pitā bhrātaro yac ca me svā yad enaś cakṛmā vayam 
AVŚc tato no vārayiṣyate 'yaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ 
AVŚa varaṇena pravyathitā bhrātṛvyā me sabandhavaḥ 
AVŚc asūrtaṃ rajo apy agus te yantv adhamaṃ tamaḥ 
AVŚa ariṣṭo 'ham ariṣṭagur āyuṣmānt sarvapūruṣaḥ 
AVŚc tam māyaṃ varaṇo maṇiḥ pari pātu diśodiśaḥ  
AVŚa ayaṃ me varaṇa urasi rājā devo vanaspatiḥ 
AVŚc sa me śatrūn vi bādhatām indro dasyūn ivāsurān 
AVŚa imaṃ bibharmi varaṇam āyuṣmān chataśāradaḥ 
AVŚc sa me rāṣṭraṃ ca kṣatraṃ ca paśūn ojaś ca me dadhat 
AVŚa yathā vāto vanaspatīn vṛkṣān bhanakty ojasā 
AVŚc evā sapatnān me bhaṅgdhi pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa yathā vātaś cāgniś ca vṛkṣān psāto vanaspatīn 
AVŚc evā sapatnān me psāhi pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa yathā vātena prakṣīṇā vṛkṣāḥ śere nyarpitāḥ 
AVŚc evā sapatnāṃs tvaṃ mama pra kṣiṇīhi ny arpaya 
AVŚe pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa tāṃs tvaṃ pra chinddhi varaṇa purā diṣṭāt purāyuṣaḥ 
AVŚc ya enaṃ paśuṣu dipsanti ye cāsya rāṣṭradipsavaḥ 
AVŚa yathā sūryo atibhāti yathāsmin teja āhitam 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā 
AVŚa yathā yaśaś candramasy āditye ca nṛcakṣasi 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā 
AVŚa yathā yaśaḥ pṛthivyāṃ yathāsmin jātavedasi 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā 
AVŚa yathā yaśaḥ kanyāyāṃ yathāsmint saṃbhṛte rathe 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
AVŚa yathā yaśaḥ somapīthe madhuparke yathā yaśaḥ 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā 
AVŚa yathā yaśo 'gnihotre vaṣaṭkāre yathā yaśaḥ 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā 
AVŚa yathā yaśo yajamāne yathāsmin yajña āhitam 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā 
AVŚa yathā yaśaḥ prajāpatau yathāsmin parameṣṭhini 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā 
AVŚa yathā deveṣv amṛtaṃ yathaiṣu satyam āhitam 
AVŚc evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚe tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā  
AVŚa indrasya prathamo ratho devānām aparo ratho varuṇasya tṛtīya it 
AVŚc ahīnām apamā ratha sthānum ārad athārṣat 
AVŚa darbhaḥ śocis tarūṇakam aśvasya vāraḥ paruṣasya vāraḥ 
AVŚc rathasya bandhuram 
AVŚa ava śveta padā jahi pūrveṇa cāpareṇa ca 
AVŚc udaplutam iva dārv ahīnām arasaṃ viṣaṃ vār ugram 
AVŚa araṃghuṣo nimajyonmaja punar abravīt 
AVŚc udaplutam iva dārv ahīnām arasaṃ viṣaṃ vār ugram 
AVŚa paidvo hanti kasarṇīlaṃ paidvaḥ śvitram utāsitam 
AVŚc paidvo ratharvyāḥ śiraḥ saṃ bibheda pṛdākvāḥ 
AVŚa paidva prehi prathamo 'nu tvā vayam emasi 
AVŚc ahīn vy asyatāt patho yena smā vayam emasi 
AVŚa idaṃ paidvo ajāyatedam asya parāyaṇam 
AVŚc imāny arvataḥ padāhighnyo vājinīvataḥ 
AVŚa saṃyataṃ na vi ṣparad vyāttaṃ na saṃ yamat 
AVŚc asmin kṣetre dvāv ahī strī ca pumāṃś ca tāv ubhāv arasā 
AVŚa arasāsa ihāhayo ye anti ye ca dūrake 
AVŚc ghanena hanmi vṛścikam ahiṃ daṇḍenāgatam 
AVŚa aghāśvasyedaṃ bheṣajam ubhayo svajasya ca 
AVŚc indro me 'him aghāyantam ahiṃ paidvo arandhayat  
AVŚa paidvasya manmahe vayaṃ sthirasya sthiradhāmnaḥ 
AVŚc ime paścā pṛdākavaḥ pradīdhyata āsate 
AVŚa naṣṭāsavo naṣṭaviṣā hatā indreṇa vajriṇā 
AVŚc jaghānendro jaghnimā vayam 
AVŚa hatās tiraścirājayo nipiṣṭāsaḥ pṛdākavaḥ 
AVŚc darviṃ karikrataṃ śvitraṃ darbheṣv asitaṃ jahi 
AVŚa kairātikā kumārikā sakā khanati bheṣajam 
AVŚc hiraṇyayībhir abhribhir girīnām upa sānuṣu 
AVŚa āyam agan yuvā bhiṣak pṛśnihāparājitaḥ 
AVŚc sa vai svajasya jambhana ubhayor vṛścikasya ca 
AVŚa indro me 'him arandhayan mitraś ca varuṇaś ca 
AVŚc vātāparjanyobhā 
AVŚa indro me 'him arandhayat pṛdākuṃ ca pṛdākvam 
AVŚc svajaṃ tiraścirājiṃ kasarṇīlaṃ daśonasim 
AVŚa indro jaghāna prathamaṃ janitāram ahe tava 
AVŚc teṣām u tṛhyamāṇānāṃ kaḥ svit teṣām asad rasaḥ 
AVŚa saṃ hi śīrṣāṇy agrabhaṃ pauñjiṣṭha iva karvaram 
AVŚc sindhor madhyaṃ paretya vy anijam aher viṣam 
AVŚa ahīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ parā vahantu sindhavaḥ 
AVŚc hatās tiraścirājayo nipiṣṭāsaḥ pṛdākavaḥ  
AVŚa oṣadhīnām ahaṃ vṛṇa urvarīr iva sādhuyā 
AVŚc nayāmy arvatīr ivāhe niraitu viṣam 
AVŚa yad agnau sūrye viṣaṃ pṛthivyām oṣadhīṣu yat 
AVŚc kāndāviṣaṃ kanaknakaṃ niraitv aitu te viṣam 
AVŚa ye agnijā oṣadhijā ahīnāṃ ye apsujā vidyuta ābabhūvuḥ 
AVŚc yeṣāṃ jātāni bahudhā mahānti tebhyaḥ sarpebhyo namasā vidhema 
AVŚa taudī nāmāsi kanyā ghṛtācī nāma vā asi 
AVŚc adhaspadena te padam ā dade viṣadūṣaṇam 
AVŚa aṅgādaṅgāt pra cyāvaya hṛdayam pari varjaya 
AVŚc adhā viṣasya yat tejo 'vācīnaṃ tad etu te 
AVŚa āre abhūd viṣam araud viṣe viṣam aprāg api 
AVŚc agnir viṣam aher nir adhāt somo nir aṇayīt 
AVŚe daṃṣṭāram anv agād viṣam ahir amṛta  
AVŚa indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha 
AVŚc jiṣṇave yogāya brahmayogair vo yunajmi 
AVŚa indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha 
AVŚc jiṣṇave yogāya kṣatrayogair vo yunajmi 
AVŚa indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha 
AVŚc jiṣṇave yogāyendrayogair vo yunajmi 
AVŚa indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha 
AVŚc jiṣṇave yogāya somayogair vo yunajmi 
AVŚa indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha 
AVŚc jiṣṇave yogāyāpsuyogair vo yunajmi 
AVŚa indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha 
AVŚc jiṣṇave yogāya viśvāni mā bhūtāny upa tiṣṭhantu yuktā ma āpa stha 
AVŚa agner bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye 
AVŚa indrasya bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye 
AVŚa somasya bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye 
AVŚa varuṇasya bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye  
AVŚa mitrāvaruṇayor bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye 
AVŚa yamasya bhāga stha apām śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye 
AVŚa pitṝṇāṃ bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye 
AVŚa devasya savitur bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta 
AVŚc prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye 
AVŚa yo va āpo 'pāṃ bhāgo 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ 
AVŚc idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi 
AVŚe tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚg taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā   
AVŚa yo va āpo 'pām ūrmir apsv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ 
AVŚc idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi 
AVŚe tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚg taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā   
AVŚa yo va āpo 'pām vatso 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ 
AVŚc idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi 
AVŚe tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚg taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā   
AVŚa yo va āpo 'pāṃ vṛṣabho 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ 
AVŚc idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi 
AVŚe tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚg taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā   
AVŚa yo va āpo 'pāṃ hiraṇyagarbho 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ 
AVŚc idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi 
AVŚe tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚg taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā   
AVŚa yo va āpo 'pāṃ aśmā pṛśnir divyo 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ 
AVŚc idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi 
AVŚe tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚg taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā   
AVŚa yo va āpo 'pāṃ agnayo 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ 
AVŚc idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi 
AVŚe tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚg taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā   
AVŚa yad arvācīnaṃ traihāyaṇād anṛtaṃ kiṃ codima 
AVŚc āpo mā tasmāt sarvasmād duritāt pāntv aṃhasaḥ 
AVŚa samudraṃ vaḥ pra hiṇomi svāṃ yonim apītana 
AVŚc ariṣṭāḥ sarvahāyaso mā ca naḥ kiṃ canāmamat 
AVŚa ariprā āpo apa ripram asmat 
AVŚc prāsmad eno duritaṃ supratīkāḥ pra duṣvapnyam pra malaṃ vahantu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā pṛthivīsaṃśito 'gnitejāḥ 
AVŚc pṛthivīm anu vi krame 'haṃ pṛthivyās taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāntarikṣasaṃśito vāyutejāḥ 
AVŚc antarikṣam anu vi krame 'haṃ antarikṣāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā dyausaṃśitaḥ sūryatejāḥ 
AVŚc divam anu vi krame 'haṃ divas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jivīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā diksaṃśito manastejāḥ 
AVŚc diśo anu vi krame 'haṃ digbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāśāsaṃśito vātatejāḥ 
AVŚc āśā anu vi krame 'haṃ āśābhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā ṛksaṃśito sāmatejāḥ 
AVŚc ṛco 'nu vi krame 'haṃ ṛgbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu  
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā yajñasaṃśito brahmatejāḥ 
AVŚc yajñam anu vi krame 'haṃ yajñāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahauṣadhīsaṃśito somatejāḥ 
AVŚc oṣadhīr anu vi krame 'haṃ oṣadhībhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāpsusaṃśito varuṇatejāḥ 
AVŚc apo 'nu vi krame 'haṃ adbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā kṛṣisaṃśito 'nnatejāḥ 
AVŚc kṛṣim anu vi krame 'haṃ kṛṣyās taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa visṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā prāṇasaṃśitaḥ puruṣatejāḥ 
AVŚc prāṇam anu vi krame 'haṃ prāṇāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ 
AVŚe sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu 
AVŚa jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam abhy aṣṭhāṃ viśvāḥ pṛtanā arātīḥ 
AVŚc idam aham āmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasya varcas tejaḥ prāṇam āyur ni veṣṭayāmīdam enam adharāñcaṃ pādayāmi 
AVŚa sūryasyāvṛtam anvāvarte dakṣiṇām anv āvṛtam 
AVŚc sā me draviṇaṃ yachatu sā me brāhmaṇavarcasam 
AVŚa diśo jyotiṣmatīr abhyāvarte 
AVŚc tā me draviṇaṃ yachantu tā me brāhmaṇavarcasam 
AVŚa saptaṛṣīn abhyāvarte 
AVŚc te me draviṇaṃ yachantu te me brāhmaṇavarcasam 
AVŚa brahmābhyāvarte 
AVŚc tan me draviṇaṃ yachantu tan me brāhmaṇavarcasam  
AVŚa brāhmaṇāṃ abhyāvarte 
AVŚc te me draviṇaṃ yachantu te me brāhmaṇavarcasam 
AVŚa yam vayaṃ mṛgayāmahe taṃ vadhai stṛṇavāmahai 
AVŚc vyātte parameṣṭhino brahmaṇāpīpadāma tam 
AVŚa vaiśvānarasya daṃṣṭrābhyāṃ hetis taṃ sam adhād abhi 
AVŚc iyaṃ taṃ psātv āhutiḥ samid devī sahīyasī 
AVŚa rājño varuṇasya bandho 'si 
AVŚc so 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram anne prāṇe badhāna 
AVŚa yat te annaṃ bhuvas pata ākṣiyati pṛthivīm anu 
AVŚc tasya nas tvaṃ bhuvas pate saṃprayacha prajāpate 
AVŚa apo divyā acāyiṣaṃ rasena sam apṛkṣmahi 
AVŚc payasvān agna āgamaṃ taṃ mā saṃ sṛja varcasā 
AVŚa saṃ māgne varcasā sṛja saṃ prajayā sam āyuṣā 
AVŚc vidyur me asya devā indro vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ 
AVŚa yad agne adya mithunā śapato yad vācas tṛṣṭaṃ janayanta rebhāḥ 
AVŚc manyor manasaḥ śaravyā jāyate yā tayā vidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān 
AVŚa parā śṛṇīhi tapasā yātudhānān parāgne rakṣo harasā śṛṇīhi 
AVŚc parārciṣā mūradevāṃ chṛṇīhi parāsutṛpaḥ śośucataḥ śṛṇīhi 
AVŚa apām asmai vajraṃ pra harāmi caturbhṛṣṭiṃ śīrṣabhidyāya vidvān 
AVŚc so asyāṅgāni pra śṛṇātu sarvā tan me devā anu jānantu viśve  
AVŚa arātīyor bhrātṛvyasya durhārdo dviṣataḥ śiraḥ 
AVŚc api vṛścāmy ojasā 
AVŚa varma mahyam ayaṃ maṇiḥ phālāj jātaḥ kariṣyati 
AVŚc pūrṇo manthena māgamad rasena saha varcasā 
AVŚa yat tvā śikvaḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāsyā 
AVŚc āpas tvā tasmaj jīvalāḥ punantu śucayaḥ śucim 
AVŚa hiraṇyasrag ayaṃ maṇiḥ śraddhāṃ yajñaṃ maho dadhat 
AVŚc gṛhe vasatu no 'tithiḥ 
AVŚa tasmai ghṛtaṃ suraṃ madhv annamannam kṣadāmahe 
AVŚc sa naḥ piteva putrebhyaḥ śreyaḥśreyaś cikitsatu bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvo devebhyo maṇir etya 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ kadhiram ojase 
AVŚc tam agniḥ praty amuñcata so asmai duha ājyaṃ bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ kadhiram ojase 
AVŚc tam indraḥ praty amuñcataujase vīryāya kam 
AVŚe so asmai balam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugram kadhiram ojase 
AVŚc taṃ somaḥ praty amuñcata mahe śrotrāya cakṣase 
AVŚe so asmai varca id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvam dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ khadiram ojase 
AVŚc taṃ sūryaḥ praty amuñcata tenemā ajayad diśaḥ 
AVŚe so asmai bhūtim id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugram khadiram ojase 
AVŚc tam bibhrac candramā maṇim asurāṇāṃ puro 'jayad dānavānāṃ hiraṇyayīḥ 
AVŚe so asmai śriyam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi  
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave 
AVŚc so asmai vājinam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave 
AVŚc tenemāṃ maṇinā kṛṣim aśvināv abhi rakṣataḥ 
AVŚe sa bhiṣagbhyāṃ maho duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave 
AVŚc tam bibhrat savitā maṇiṃ tenedam ajayat svaḥ 
AVŚe so asmai sūnṛtāṃ duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave 
AVŚc tam āpo bibhratīr maṇiṃ sadā dhāvanty akṣitāḥ 
AVŚe sa ābhyo 'mṛtam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave 
AVŚc tam rājā varuṇo maṇiṃ praty amuñcata śaṃbhuvam 
AVŚe so asmai satyam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave 
AVŚc taṃ devā bibhrato maṇiṃ sarvāṃl lokān yudhājayan 
AVŚe sa ebhyo jitim id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave 
AVŚc tam imaṃ devatā maṇiṃ praty amuñcanta śambhuvam 
AVŚe sa ābhyo viśvam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa ṛtavas tam abadhnatārtavās tam abadhnata 
AVŚc saṃvatsaras taṃ baddhvā sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ vi rakṣati 
AVŚa antardeśā abadhnata pradiśas tam abadhnata 
AVŚc prajāpatisṛṣṭo maṇir dviṣato me 'dharāṃ akaḥ 
AVŚa atharvāṇo abadhnatātharvaṇā abadhnata 
AVŚc tair medino aṅgiraso dasyūnāṃ bibhiduḥ puras tena tvam dviṣato jahi  
AVŚa taṃ dhātā praty amuñcata sa bhūtaṃ vy akalpayat 
AVŚc tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim 
AVŚc sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamad rasena saha varcasā 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim 
AVŚc sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat saha gobhir ajāvibhir annena prajayā saha 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim 
AVŚc sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat saha vrīhiyavābhyāṃ mahasā bhūtyā saha 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim 
AVŚc sa māyaṃ maṇir āgaman madhor ghṛtasya dhārayā kīlālena maṇiḥ saha 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim 
AVŚc sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamad ūrjayā payasā saha draviṇena śriyā saha 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim 
AVŚc sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat tejasā tviṣyā saha yaśasā kīrtyā saha 
AVŚa yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim 
AVŚc sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat sarvābhir bhūtibhiḥ saha 
AVŚa tam imaṃ devatā maṇiṃ mahyaṃ dadatu puṣṭaye 
AVŚc abhibhuṃ kṣatravardhanaṃ sapatnadambhanaṃ maṇim 
AVŚa brahmaṇā tejasā saha prati muñcāmi me śivam 
AVŚc asapatnaḥ sapatnahā sapatnān me 'dharāṃ akaḥ  
AVŚa uttaraṃ dviṣato mām ayaṃ maṇiḥ kṛṇotu devajāḥ 
AVŚc yasya lokā ime trayaḥ payo dugdham upāsate 
AVŚe sa māyam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ 
AVŚa yaṃ devāḥ pitaro manuṣyā upajīvanti sarvadā 
AVŚc sa māyam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ 
AVŚa yathā bījam urvarāyāṃ kṛṣṭe phālena rohati 
AVŚc evā mayi prajā paśavo 'nnamannaṃ vi rohatu 
AVŚa yasmai tvā yajñavardhana maṇe pratyamucaṃ śivam 
AVŚc taṃ tvaṃ śatadakṣiṇa maṇe śraiṣṭhyāya jinvatāt 
AVŚa etam idhmaṃ samāhitaṃ juṣaṇo agne prati harya homaiḥ 
AVŚc tasmin vidhema sumatiṃ svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūnt samiddhe jātavedasi brahmaṇā  
AVŚa kasminn aṅge tapo asyādhi tiṣṭhati kasminn aṅga ṛtam asyādhy āhitam 
AVŚc kva vrataṃ kva śraddhāsya tiṣṭhati kasminn aṅge satyam asya pratiṣṭhitam 
AVŚa kasmād aṅgād dīpyate agnir asya kasmād aṅgāt pavate mātariśva 
AVŚc kasmād aṅgād vi mimīte 'dhi candramā maha skambhasya mimāno aṅgam 
AVŚa kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhati bhūmir asya kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty antarikṣam 
AVŚc kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty āhitā dyauḥ kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty uttaraṃ divaḥ 
AVŚa kva prepsan dīpyata ūrdhvo agniḥ kva prepsan pavate mātariśvā 
AVŚc yatra prepsantīr abhiyanty āvṛtaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa kvārdhamāsāḥ kva yanti māsāḥ saṃvatsareṇa saha saṃvidānāḥ 
AVŚc yatra yanty ṛtavo yatrārtavāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa kva prepsantī yuvatī virūpe ahorātre dravataḥ saṃvidāne 
AVŚc yatra prepsantīr abhiyanty āpaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yasmint stabdhvā prajāpatir lokānt sarvāṃ adhārayat 
AVŚc skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yat paramam avamam yac ca madhyamaṃ prajāpatiḥ sasṛje viśvarūpam 
AVŚc kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra yan na prāviśat kiyat tad babhūva 
AVŚa kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa bhūtam kiyad bhaviṣyad anvāśaye 'sya 
AVŚc ekaṃ yad aṅgam akṛṇot sahasradhā kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra 
AVŚa yatra lokāmś ca kośāṃś cāpo brahma janā viduḥ 
AVŚc asac ca yatra sac cānta skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
AVŚa yatra tapaḥ parākramya vrataṃ dhārayaty uttaram 
AVŚc ṛtaṃ ca yatra śraddhā cāpo brahma samāhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yasmin bhūmir antarikṣaṃ dyaur yasminn adhy āhitā 
AVŚc yatrāgniś candramāḥ sūryo vātas tiṣṭhanty ārpitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yasya trayastriṃśad devā aṅge sarve samāhitāḥ 
AVŚc skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathamajā ṛcaḥ sāma yajur mahī 
AVŚc ekarṣir yasminn ārpitaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yatrāmṛtaṃ ca mṛtyuś ca puruṣe 'dhi samāhite 
AVŚc samudro yasya nāḍyaḥ puruṣe 'dhi samāhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yasya catasraḥ pradiśo nāḍyas tiṣṭhanti prathamāḥ 
AVŚc yajño yatra parākrāntaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa ye puruṣe brahma vidus te viduḥ parameṣṭhinam 
AVŚc yo veda parameṣṭhinaṃ yaś ca veda prajāpatim 
AVŚe jyeṣṭhaṃ ye brāhmaṇaṃ vidus te skambham anusaṃviduḥ 
AVŚa yasya śiro vaiśvānaraś cakṣur aṅgiraso 'bhavan 
AVŚc aṅgāni yasya yātavaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yasya brahma mukham āhur jihvāṃ madhukaśām uta 
AVŚc virājam ūdho yasyāhuḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yasmād ṛco apātakṣan yajur yasmād apākaṣan 
AVŚc sāmāni yasya lomāny atharvāṅgiraso mukhaṃ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ  
AVŚa asaccākhāṃ pratiṣṭhantīṃ paramam iva janā viduḥ 
AVŚc uto san manyante 'vare ye te śākhām upāsate 
AVŚa yatrādityāś ca rudrāś ca vasavaś ca samāhitāḥ 
AVŚc bhūtaṃ ca yatra bhavyaṃ ca sarve lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ 
AVŚa yasya trayastriṃśad devā nidhiṃ rakṣanti sarvadā 
AVŚc nidhiṃ tam adya ko veda yaṃ devā abhirakṣatha 
AVŚa yatra devā brahmavido brahma jyeṣṭham upāsate 
AVŚc yo vai tān vidyāt pratyakṣaṃ sa brahmā veditā syāt 
AVŚa bṛhanto nāma te devā ye 'sataḥ pari jajñire 
AVŚc ekaṃ tad aṅgaṃ skambhasyāsad āhuḥ paro janāḥ 
AVŚa yatra skambhaḥ prajanayan purāṇaṃ vyavartayat 
AVŚc ekaṃ tad aṅgaṃ skambhasya purāṇam anusaṃviduḥ 
AVŚa yasya trayastriṃśad devā aṅge gātrā vibhejire 
AVŚc tān vai trayastriṃśad devān eke brahamvido viduḥ
