AVŚc āgne yāhi suvidatrebhir arvāṅ paraiḥ pūrvair ṛṣibhir gharmasadbhiḥ 
AVŚa upa sarpa mātaraṃ bhūmim etām uruvyacasaṃ pṛthivīṃ suśevām 
AVŚc ūrṇamradāḥ pṛthivī dakṣiṇāvata eṣā tvā pātu prapathe purastāt 
AVŚa uc chvañcasva pṛthivi mā ni bādhathāḥ sūpāyanāsmai bhava sūpasarpaṇā 
AVŚc mātā putraṃ yathā sicābhy enaṃ bhūma ūrṇuhi  
AVŚa ucchvañcamānā pṛthivī su tiṣṭhatu sahasraṃ mita upa hi śrayantām 
AVŚc te gṛhāso ghṛtaścutaḥ syonā viśvāhāsmai śaraṇāḥ santv atra 
AVŚa ut te stabhnāmi pṛthivīṃ tvat parīmaṃ logaṃ nidadhan mo aham riṣam 
AVŚc etāṃ sthūṇāṃ pitaro dhārayanti te tatra yamaḥ sādanā te kṛṇotu 
AVŚa imam agne camasaṃ mā vi jihvaraḥ priyo devānām uta somyānām 
AVŚc ayaṃ yaś camaso devapānas tasmin devā amṛtā mādayantām 
AVŚa atharvā pūrṇam camasam yam indrāyābibhar vājinīvate 
AVŚc tasmin kṛṇoti sukṛtasya bhakṣaṃ tasmin induḥ pavate viśvadānim 
AVŚa yat te kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna ātutoda pipīlaḥ sarpa uta vā śvāpadaḥ 
AVŚc agniṣ ṭad viśvād agadaṃ kṛṇotu somaś ca yo brāhmaṇāṃ āviveśa 
AVŚa payasvatīr oṣadhayaḥ payasvan māmakaṃ payaḥ 
AVŚc apāṃ payaso yat payas tena mā saha śumbhatu 
AVŚa imā nārīr avidhavāḥ supatnīr āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃ spṛśantām 
AVŚc anaśravo anamīvāḥ suratnā ā rohantu janayo yonim agre 
AVŚa saṃ gachasva pitṛbhiḥ saṃ yameneṣṭāpūrtena parame vyoman 
AVŚc hitvāvadyaṃ punar astam ehi saṃ gachatāṃ tanvā suvarcāḥ 
AVŚa ye naḥ pituḥ pitaro ye pitāmahā ya āviviśur urv antarikṣam 
AVŚc tebhyaḥ svarād asunītir no adya vathāvaśaṃ tanvaḥ kalpayāti 
AVŚa śaṃ te nīhāro bhavatu śaṃ te pruṣvāva śīyatām 
AVŚc śītike śītikāvati hlādike hlādikāvati 
AVŚe maṇḍūky apsu śaṃ bhuva imaṃ sv agniṃ śamaya  
AVŚa vivasvān no abhayaṃ kṛṇotu yaḥ sutrāmā jīradānuḥ sudānuḥ 
AVŚc iheme vīrā bahavo bhavantu gomad aśvavan mayy astu puṣṭam 
AVŚa vivasvān no amṛtatve dadhātu paraitu mṛtyur amṛtaṃ na aitu 
AVŚc imān rakṣatu puruṣān ā jarimṇo mo sv eṣām asavo yamaṃ guḥ 
AVŚa yo dadhre antarikṣe na mahnā pitṝṇāṃ kaviḥ pramatir matīnām 
AVŚc tam arcata viśvamitrā havirbhiḥ sa no yamaḥ prataraṃ jīvase dhāt 
AVŚa ā rohata divam uttamām ṛṣayo mā bibhītana 
AVŚc somapāḥ somapāyina idaṃ vaḥ kriyate havir aganma jvotir uttamam 
AVŚa pra ketunā bṛhatā bhāty agnir ā rodasī vṛṣabho roravīti 
AVŚc divaś cid antād upamām ud ānaḍ apām upasthe mahiṣo vavardha 
AVŚa nāke suparṇam upa yat patantaṃ hrdā venanto abhyacakṣata tvā 
AVŚc hiraṇyapakṣaṃ varuṇasya dūtaṃ yamasya yonau śakunaṃ bhuranyum 
AVŚa indra kratuṃ na ā bhara pitā putrebhyo yathā 
AVŚc śikṣā ṇo asmin puruhūta yāmani jīvā jyotir aśīmahi 
AVŚa apūpāpihitān kumbhān yāṃs te devā adhārayan 
AVŚc te te santu svadhāvanto madhumanto ghṛtaścutaḥ 
AVŚa yās te dhānā anukirāmi tilamiśrā svadhāvatīḥ 
AVŚc tās te santu vibhvīḥ prabhvīs tās te yamo rājānu manyatām 
AVŚa punar dehi vanaspate ya eṣa nihitas tvayi 
AVŚc yathā yamasya sādana āsātau vidathā vadan 
AVŚa ā rabhasva jātavedas tejasvad dharo astu te 
AVŚc śarīram asya saṃ dahāthainaṃ dehi sukṛtām u loke 
AVŚa ye te pūrve parāgatā apare pitaraś ca ye 
AVŚc tebhyo ghṛtasya kulyaitu śatadhārā vyundatī 
AVŚa etad ā roha vaya unmṛjānaḥ svā iha bṛhad u dīdayante 
AVŚc abhi prehi madhyato māpa hāsthāḥ pitṝnāṃ lokaṃ prathamo yo atra  
AVŚa ā rohata janitrīṃ jātavedasaḥ pitṛyānaiḥ saṃ va ā rohayāmi 
AVŚc avāḍ ḍhavyeṣito havyavāha ījānaṃ yuktāḥ sukṛtāṃ dhatta loke 
AVŚa devā yajñam ṛtavaḥ kalpayanti haviḥ puroḍāśaṃ sruco yajñāyudhāni 
AVŚc tebhir yāhi pathibhir devayānair yair ījānāḥ svargaṃ yanti lokam 
AVŚa ṛtasya panthām anu paśya sādhv aṅgirasaḥ sukṛto yena yanti 
AVŚc tebhir yāhi pathibhiḥ svargaṃ yatrādityā madhu bhakṣayanti tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayasva 
AVŚa trayaḥ suparṇā uparasya māyū nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi viṣṭapi śritāḥ 
AVŚc svargā lokā amṛtena viṣṭhā iṣam ūrjaṃ yajamānāya duhrām 
AVŚa juhūr dādhāra dyām upabhṛd antarikṣaṃ dhruvā dādhāra pṛthivīṃ pratiṣṭhām 
AVŚc pratīmāṃ lokā ghṛtapṛṣṭhāḥ svargāḥ kāmaṃkāmaṃ yajamānāya duhrām 
AVŚa dhruva ā roha pṛthivīṃ viśvabhojasam antarikṣam upabhṛd ā kramasva 
AVŚc juhu dyāṃ gacha yajamānena sākaṃ sruveṇa vatsena diśaḥ prapīnāḥ sarvā dhukṣvāhṛṇyamānaḥ 
AVŚa tīrthais taranti pravato mahīr iti yajñakṛtaḥ sukṛto yena yanti 
AVŚc atrādadhur yajamānāya lokaṃ diśo bhūtāni yad akalpayanta 
AVŚa aṅgirasām ayanaṃ pūrvo agnir ādityānām ayanaṃ gārhapatyo dakṣiṇānām ayanaṃ dakṣiṇāgniḥ 
AVŚc mahimānam agner vihitasya brahmaṇā samaṅgaḥ sarva upa yāhi śagmaḥ 
AVŚa pūrvo agniṣ ṭvā tapatu śaṃ purastāc chaṃ paścāt tapatu gārhapatyaḥ 
AVŚc dakṣiṇāgniṣ ṭe tapatu śarma varmottarato madhyato antarikṣād diśodiśo agne pari pāhi ghorāt 
AVŚa yūyam agne śaṃtamābhis tanūbhir ījānam abhi lokaṃ svargam 
AVŚc aśvā bhūtvā pṛṣṭivāho vahātha yatra devaiḥ sadhamādaṃ madanti  
AVŚa śam agne paścāt tapa śaṃ purastāc cham uttarāc cham adharāt tapainam 
AVŚc ekas tredhā vihito jātavedaḥ samyag enaṃ dhehi sukṛtām u loke 
AVŚa śam agnayaḥ samiddhā ā rabhantāṃ prājāpatyaṃ medhyaṃ jātavedasaḥ 
AVŚc śṛtaṃ kṛṇvanta iha māva cikṣipan 
AVŚa yajña eti vitataḥ kalpamāna ījānam abhi lokaṃ svargam 
AVŚc tam agnayaḥ sarvahutaṃ juṣantāṃ prājāpatyaṃ medhyaṃ jātavedasaḥ 
AVŚa ījānaś citam ārukṣad agniṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhād divam utpatiṣyan 
AVŚc tasmai pra bhāti nabhaso jyotiṣīmānt svargaḥ panthāḥ sukṛte devayānaḥ 
AVŚa agnir hotādhvaryuṣ ṭe bṛhaspatir indro brahmā dakṣiṇatas te astu 
AVŚc huto 'yaṃ saṃsthito yajña eti yatra pūrvam ayanaṃ hutānām 
AVŚa apūpavān kṣīravāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpavān dadhivāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpavān drapsavāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpavān ghṛtavāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpavān māṃsavāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha  
AVŚa apūpavān annavāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpavān madhumāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpavān rasavāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpavān apavāṃś carur eha sīdatu 
AVŚc lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha 
AVŚa apūpāpihitān kumbhān yāṃs te devā adhārayan 
AVŚc te te santu svadhāvanto madhumanto ghṛtaścutaḥ 
AVŚa yās te dhānā anukirāmi tilamiśrāḥ svadhāvatīḥ 
AVŚc tās te santūdbhvīḥ prabhvīs tās te yamo rājānu manyatām 
AVŚa akṣitiṃ bhūyasīm 
AVŚa drapsaś caskanda pṛthivīm anu dyām imaṃ ca yonim anu yaś ca pūrvaḥ 
AVŚc samānaṃ yonim anu samcarantaṃ drapsam juhomy anu sapta hotrāḥ 
AVŚa śatadhāraṃ vāyum arkaṃ svarvidaṃ nṛcakṣasas te abhi cakṣate rayim 
AVŚc ye pṛnanti pra ca yachanti sarvadā te duhrate dakṣiṇāṃ saptamātaram 
AVŚa kośaṃ duhanti kalaśaṃ caturbilam iḍāṃ dhenuṃ madhumatīṃ svastaye 
AVŚc ūrjaṃ madantīm aditiṃ janeṣv agne mā hiṃsīḥ parame vyoman  
AVŚa etat te devaḥ savitā vāso dadāti bhartave 
AVŚc tat tvaṃ yamasya rājye vasānas tārpyaṃ cara 
AVŚa dhānā dhenur abhavad vatso asyās tilo 'bhavat 
AVŚc tāṃ vai yamasya rājye akṣitām upa jīvati 
AVŚa etās te asau dhenavaḥ kāmadughā bhavantu 
AVŚc enīḥ śyenīḥ sarūpā virūpās tilavatsā upa tiṣṭhantu tvātra 
AVŚa enīr dhānā hariṇīḥ śyenīr asya kṛṣṇā dhānā rohiṇīr dhenavas te 
AVŚc tilavatsā ūrjam asmai duhānā viśvāhā santv anapasphurantīḥ 
AVŚa vaiśvānare havir idaṃ juhomi sāhasraṃ śatadhāram utsam 
AVŚc sa bibharti pitaraṃ pitāmahān prapitāmahān bibharti pinvamānaḥ 
AVŚa sahasradhāraṃ śatadhāram utsam akṣitaṃ vyacyamānaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe 
AVŚc ūrjaṃ duhānam anapasphurantam upāsate pitaraḥ svadhābhiḥ 
AVŚa idaṃ kasāmbu cayanena citaṃ tat sajātā ava paśyateta 
AVŚc martyo 'yam amṛtatvam eti tasmai gṛhān kṛṇuta yāvatsabandhu 
AVŚa ihaivaidhi dhanasanir ihacitta ihakratuḥ 
AVŚc ihaidhi vīryavattaro vayodhā aparāhataḥ 
AVŚa putraṃ pautram abhitarpayantīr āpo madhumatīr imāḥ 
AVŚc svadhāṃ pitṛbhyo amṛtaṃ duhānā āpo devīr ubhayāṃs tarpayantu 
AVŚa āpo agniṃ pra hiṇuta pitṝṃr upemaṃ yajñaṃ pitaro me juṣantām 
AVŚc āsīnām ūrjam upa ye sacante te no rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yachān  
AVŚa sam indhate amartyaṃ havyavāhaṃ ghṛtapriyam 
AVŚc sa veda nihitān nidhīn pitṝn parāvato gatān 
AVŚa yaṃ te manthaṃ yam odananaṃ yan māṃsaṃ nipṛṇāmi te 
AVŚc te te santu svadhāvanto madhumanto ghṛtaścutaḥ 
AVŚa yās te dhānā anukirāmi tilamiśrāḥ svadhāvatīḥ 
AVŚc tās te santūdbhvīḥ prabhvīs tās te yamo rājānu manyatām 
AVŚa idaṃ pūrvam aparaṃ niyānaṃ yenā te pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ 
AVŚc purogavā ye abhisāco asya te tvā vahanti sukṛtām u lokam 
AVŚa sarasvatīṃ devayanto havante sarasvatīm adhvare tāyamāne 
AVŚc sarasvatīṃ sukṛto havante sarasvatī dāśuṣe vāryaṃ dāt 
AVŚa sarasvatīṃ pitaro havante dakṣiṇā yajñam abhinakṣamāṇāḥ 
AVŚc āsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam anamīvā iṣa ā dhehy asme 
AVŚa sarasvati yā sarathaṃ yayāthokthaiḥ svadhābhir devi pitṛbhir madantī 
AVŚc sahasrārgham iḍo atra bhāgaṃ rāyas poṣaṃ yajamānāya dhehi 
AVŚa pṛthivīṃ tvā pṛthivyām ā veśayāmi devo no dhātā pra tirāty āyuḥ 
AVŚc parāparaitā vasuvid vo astv adhā mṛtāḥ pitṛṣu saṃ bhavantu 
AVŚa ā pra cyavethām apa tan mṛjethāṃ yad vām abhibhā atrocuḥ 
AVŚc asmād etam aghnyau tad vaśīyo dātuḥ pitṛṣv ihabhojanau mama 
AVŚa eyam agan dakṣiṇā bhadrato nā anena dattā sudughā vayodhāḥ 
AVŚc yauvane jīvān upapṛñcatī jarā pitṛbhya upasaṃparāṇayād imān  
AVŚa idaṃ pitṛbhyaḥ pra bharāmi barhir jīvaṃ devebhya uttaraṃ stṛṇāmi 
AVŚc tad ā roha puruṣa medhyo bhavan prati tvā jānantu pitaraḥ paretam 
AVŚa edaṃ barhir asado medhyo 'bhūḥ prati tvā jānantu pitaraḥ paretam 
AVŚc yathāparu tanvaṃ saṃ bharasva gātrāṇi te brahmaṇā kalpayāmi 
AVŚa parṇo rājāpidhānaṃ carūṇām ūrjo balaṃ saha ojo na āgan 
AVŚc āyur jīvebhyo vidadhad dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya 
AVŚa ūrjo bhāgo ya imaṃ jajānāśmānnānām ādhipatyaṃ jagāma 
AVŚc tam arcata viśvamitrā havirbhiḥ sa no yamaḥ prataraṃ jīvase dhāt 
AVŚa yathā yamāya harmyam avapan pañca mānavāḥ 
AVŚc evā vapāmi harmyaṃ yathā me bhūrayo 'sata 
AVŚa idaṃ hiraṇyaṃ bibhṛhi yat te pitābibhaḥ purā 
AVŚc svargaṃ yataḥ pitur hastaṃ nir mṛḍḍhi dakṣiṇam 
AVŚa ye ca jīvā ye ca mṛtā ye jātā ye ca yajñiyāḥ 
AVŚc tebhyo ghṛtasya kulyaitu madhudhārā vyundatī 
AVŚa vṛṣā matīnāṃ pavate vicakṣaṇaḥ sūro ahnāṃ pratarītoṣasāṃ divaḥ 
AVŚc prāṇaḥ sindhūnāṃ kalaśāṃ acikradad indrasya hārdim āviśan manīṣayā 
AVŚa tveṣas te dhūma ūrṇotu divi ṣaṃ chukra ātataḥ 
AVŚc sūro na hi dyutā tvaṃ kṛpā pāvaka rocase 
AVŚa pra vā etīndur indrasya niṣkṛtiṃ sakhā sakhyur na pra mināti saṃgiraḥ 
AVŚc marya iva yoṣāḥ sam arṣase somaḥ kalaśe śatayāmanā pathā  
AVŚa akṣann amīmadanta hy ava priyāṃ adhūṣata 
AVŚc astoṣata svabhānavo viprā yaviṣṭhā īmahe 
AVŚa ā yāta pitaraḥ somyāso gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ 
AVŚc āyur asmabhyaṃ dadhataḥ prajāṃ ca rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacadhvam 
AVŚa parā yāta pitaraḥ somyāso gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pūryāṇaiḥ 
AVŚc adhā māsi punar ā yāta no gṛhān havir attuṃ suprajasaḥ suvīrāḥ 
AVŚa yad vo agnir ajahād ekam aṅgaṃ pitṛlokaṃ gamayaṃ jātavedāḥ 
AVŚc tad va etat punar ā pyāyayāmi sāṅgāḥ svarge pitaro mādayadhvam 
AVŚa abhūd dūtaḥ prahito jātavedāḥ sāyaṃ nyahna upavandyo nṛbhiḥ 
AVŚc prādāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhayā te akṣann addhi tvaṃ deva prayatā havīṃṣi 
AVŚa asau hā iha te manaḥ kakutsalam iva jāmayaḥ 
AVŚc abhy enaṃ bhūma ūrṇuhi 
AVŚa śumbhantāṃ lokāḥ pitṛṣadanāḥ pitṛṣadane tvā loka ā sādayāmi 
AVŚa ye asmākaṃ pitaras teṣāṃ barhir asi 
AVŚa ud uttamaṃ varuṇa pāśam asmad avādhamaṃ śrathāya 
AVŚc adhā vayam āditya vrate tavānāgaso aditaye syāma 
AVŚa prāsmat pāśān varuṇa muñca sarvān yaiḥ samāme badhyate yair vyāme 
AVŚc adhā jīvema śaradaṃ śatāni tvayā rājan gupitā rakṣamāṇāḥ  
AVŚa agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā namaḥ 
AVŚa somāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ 
AVŚa pitṛbhyaḥ somavadbhyaḥ svadhā namaḥ 
AVŚa yamāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ 
AVŚa etat te pratatāmaha svadhā ye ca tvām anu 
AVŚa etat te tatāmaha svadhā ye ca tvām anu 
AVŚa etat te tata svadhā 
AVŚa svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthiviṣadbhyaḥ 
AVŚa svadhā pitṛbhyo antarikṣasadbhyaḥ 
AVŚa svadhā pitṛbhyo diviṣadbhyaḥ  
AVŚa namo vaḥ pitara ūrje namo vaḥ pitaro rasāya 
AVŚa namo vaḥ pitaro bhāmāya namo vaḥ pitaro manyave 
AVŚa namo vaḥ pitaro yad ghoraṃ tasmai namo vaḥ pitaro yat krūraṃ tasmai 
AVŚa namo vaḥ pitaro yac chivaṃ tasmai namo vaḥ pitaro yat syonaṃ tasmai 
AVŚa namo vaḥ pitaraḥ svadhā vaḥ pitaraḥ 
AVŚa ye 'tra pitaraḥ pitaro ye 'tra yūyaṃ stha yuṣmāṃs te 'nu yūyaṃ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhā bhūyāstha 
AVŚa ya iha pitaro jīvā iha vayaṃ smaḥ 
AVŚc asmāṃs te 'nu vayaṃ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhā bhūyāsma 
AVŚa ā tvāgna idhīmahi dyumantaṃ devājaram 
AVŚc yad gha sā te panīyasī samid dīdayati dyavi 
AVŚe iṣaṃ stotṛbhya ā bhara 
AVŚa candramā apsv antar ā suparṇo dhāvate divi 
AVŚc na vo hiraṇyanemayaḥ padaṃ vindanti vidyuto vittaṃ me asya rodasī  
AVŚa saṃsaṃ sravantu nadyaḥ saṃ vātāḥ saṃ patatriṇaḥ 
AVŚc yajñam imaṃ vardhayatā giraḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi 
AVŚa imaṃ homā yajñam avatemaṃ saṃsrāvaṇā uta yajñam imaṃ vardhayatā giraḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi 
AVŚa rūpaṃrūpaṃ vayovayaḥ saṃrabhyainaṃ pari ṣvaje 
AVŚc yajñam imaṃ catasraḥ pradiśo vardhayantu saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi 
AVŚa śaṃ ta āpo haimavatīḥ śam u te santūtsyāḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ te saniṣyadā āpaḥ śam u te santu varṣyāḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ ta āpo dhanvanyāḥ śaṃ te santv anūpyāḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ te khanitrimā āpaḥ śaṃ yāḥ kumbhebhir ābhṛtāḥ 
AVŚa anabhrayaḥ khanamānā viprā gambhīre apasaḥ 
AVŚc bhiṣagbhyo bhiṣaktarā āpo achā vadāmasi 
AVŚa apām aha divyānām apāṃ srotasyānām 
AVŚc apām aha praṇejane 'śvā bhavatha vājinaḥ 
AVŚa tā apaḥ śivā apo 'yakṣmaṃkaraṇīr apaḥ 
AVŚc yathaiva tṛpyate mayas tās ta ā datta bhesajīḥ 
AVŚa divas pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣād vanaspatibhyo adhy oṣadhībhyaḥ 
AVŚc yatrayatra vibhṛto jātavedās tata stuto juṣamāṇo na ehi 
AVŚa yas te apsu mahimā yo vaneṣu ya oṣadhīṣu paśuṣv apsv antaḥ 
AVŚc agne sarvās tanvaḥ saṃ rabhasva tābhir na ehi draviṇodā ajasraḥ 
AVŚa yas te deveṣu mahimā svargo yā te tanuḥ pitṛṣv āviveśa 
AVŚc puṣṭir yā te manuṣyeṣu paprathe 'gne tayā rayim asmāsu dhehi 
AVŚa śrutkarṇāya kavaye vedyāya vacobhir vākair upa yāmi rātim 
AVŚc yato bhayam abhayaṃ tan no astv ava devānāṃ yaja heḍo agne 
AVŚa yām āhutiṃ prathamām atharvā yā jātā yā havyam akṛṇoj jātavedāḥ 
AVŚc tāṃ ta etāṃ prathamo johavīmi tābhiṣ ṭupto vahatu havyam agnir agnaye svāha 
AVŚa ākūtiṃ devīṃ subhagāṃ puro dadhe cittasya mātā suhavā no astu 
AVŚc yām āśām emi kevalī sā me astu videyam enāṃ manasi praviṣṭām 
AVŚa ākūtyā no bṛhaspata ākūtyā na upā gahi 
AVŚc atho bhagasya no dhehy atho naḥ suhavo bhava 
AVŚa bṛhaspatir ma ākūtim āṅgirasaḥ prati jānātu vācam etām 
AVŚc yasya devā devatāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ sa supraṇītāḥ kāmo anv etv asmān 
AVŚa indro rājā jagataś carṣaṇīnām adhi kṣami viṣurūpaṃ yad asti 
AVŚc tato dadāti dāśuṣe vasūni codad rādha upastutaś cid arvāk 
AVŚa sahasrabāhuḥ puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt 
AVŚc sa bhūmiṃ viśvato vṛtvāty atiṣṭhad daśāṅgulam 
AVŚa tribhiḥ padbhir dyām arohat pād asyehābhavat punaḥ 
AVŚc tathā vy akrāmad viṣvaṅ aśanānaśane anu 
AVŚa tāvanto asya mahimānas tato jyāyāṃś ca pūruṣaḥ 
AVŚc pādo 'sya viśvā bhūtāni tripād asyāmṛtaṃ divi 
AVŚa puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam 
AVŚc utāmṛtatvasyeśvaro yad anyenābhavat saha 
AVŚa yat puruṣaṃ vy adadhuḥ katidhā vy akalpayan 
AVŚc mukhaṃ kim asya kim bāhū kim ūrū pādā ucyate 
AVŚa brāhmaṇo 'sya mukham āsīd bāhū rājanyo 'bhavat 
AVŚc madhyaṃ tad asya yad vaiśyaḥ padbhyāṃ śūdro ajāyata 
AVŚa candramā manaso jātaś cakṣoḥ sūryo ajāyata 
AVŚc mukhād indraś cāgniś ca prāṇād vāyur ajāyata 
AVŚa nābhyā āsīd antarikṣaṃ śīrṣṇo dyauḥ sam avartata 
AVŚc padbhyāṃ bhūmir diśaḥ śrotrāt tathā lokāṃ akalpayan 
AVŚa virāḍ agre sam abhavad virājo adhi pūruṣaḥ 
AVŚc sa jāto aty aricyata paścād bhūmim atho puraḥ 
AVŚa yat puruṣeṇa haviṣā devā yajñam atanvata 
AVŚc vasanto asyāsīd ājyaṃ grīṣma idhmaḥ śarad dhaviḥ 
AVŚa taṃ yajñaṃ prāvṛṣā praukṣan puruṣaṃ jātam agraśaḥ 
AVŚc tena devā ayajanta sādhyā vasavaś ca ye 
AVŚa tasmād aśvā ajāyanta ye ca ke cobhayādataḥ 
AVŚc gāvo ha jajñire tasmāt tasmāj jātā ajāvayaḥ 
AVŚa tasmād yajñāt sarvahuta ṛcaḥ sāmāni jajñire 
AVŚc chando ha jajñire tasmād yajus tasmād ajāyata 
AVŚa tasmād yajñāt sarvahutaḥ saṃbhṛtaṃ pṛṣadājyam 
AVŚc paśūṃs tāṃś cakre vāyavyān āraṇyā grāmyāś ca ye 
AVŚa saptāsyāsan paridhayas triḥ sapta samidhaḥ kṛtāḥ 
AVŚc devā yad yajñaṃ tanvānā abadhnan puruṣaṃ paśum 
AVŚa mūrdhno devasya bṛhato aṃśavaḥ sapta saptatīḥ 
AVŚc rājñaḥ somasyājāyanta jātasya puruṣād adhi 
AVŚa citrāṇi sākaṃ divi rocanāni sarīsṛpāṇi bhuvane javāni 
AVŚc turmiśaṃ sumatim ichamāno ahāni gīrbhiḥ saparyāmi nākam 
AVŚa suhavam agne kṛttikā rohiṇī cāstu bhadraṃ mṛgaśiraḥ śam ārdrā 
AVŚc punarvasū sūnṛtā cāru puṣyo bhānur āśleṣā ayanaṃ maghā me 
AVŚa puṇyaṃ pūrvā phalgunyau cātra hastaś citrā śivā svāti sukho me astu 
AVŚc rādhe viśākhe suhavānurādhā jyeṣṭhā sunakṣatram ariṣṭa mūlam 
AVŚa annaṃ pūrvā rāsatāṃ me aṣādhā ūrjaṃ devy uttarā ā vahantu 
AVŚc abhijin me rāsatāṃ puṇyam eva śravaṇaḥ śraviṣṭhāḥ kurvatāṃ supuṣṭim 
AVŚa ā me mahac chatabhiṣag varīya ā me dvayā proṣṭhapadā suśarma 
AVŚc ā revatī cāśvayujau bhagaṃ ma ā me rayiṃ bharaṇya ā vahantu 
AVŚa yāni nakṣatrāṇi divy antarikṣe apsu bhūmau yāni nageṣu dikṣu 
AVŚc prakalpayaṃś candramā yāny eti sarvāṇi mamaitāni śivāni santu 
AVŚa aṣṭāviṃśāni śivāni śagmāni saha yogaṃ bhajantu me 
AVŚc yogaṃ pra padye kṣemaṃ ca kṣemaṃ pra padye yogaṃ ca namo 'horātrābhyām astu 
AVŚa svastitaṃ me suprātaḥ susāyaṃ sudivaṃ sumṛgaṃ suśakunaṃ me astu 
AVŚc suhavam agne svasty amartyaṃ gatvā punar āyābhinandan 
AVŚa anuhavaṃ parihavaṃ parivādaṃ parikṣavam 
AVŚc sarvair me riktakumbhān parā tānt savitaḥ suva 
AVŚa apapāpaṃ parikṣavaṃ puṇyaṃ bhakṣīmahi kṣavam 
AVŚc śivā te pāpa nāsikāṃ puṇyagaś cābhi mehatām 
AVŚa imā yā brahmaṇas pate viṣucīr vāta īrate 
AVŚc sadhrīcīr indra tāḥ kṛtvā mahyaṃ śivatamās kṛdhi 
AVŚa svasti no astv abhayaṃ no astu namo 'horatrābhyām astu 
AVŚa śāntā dyauḥ śāntā pṛthivī śāntam idam urv antarikṣam 
AVŚc śāntā udanvatīr āpaḥ śāntā naḥ santv oṣadhīḥ 
AVŚa śāntāni pūrvarūpāṇi śāntaṃ no astu kṛtākṛtam 
AVŚc śāntaṃ bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca sarvam eva śam astu naḥ 
AVŚa iyaṃ yā parameṣṭhinī vāg devī brahmasaṃśitā 
AVŚc yayaiva sasṛje ghoraṃ tayaiva śāntir astu naḥ 
AVŚa idaṃ yat parameṣṭhinaṃ mano vāṃ brahmasaṃśitam 
AVŚc yenaiva sasṛje ghoraṃ tenaiva śāntir astu naḥ 
AVŚa imāni yāni pañcendriyāni manaḥṣaṣṭhāni me hṛdi brahmaṇā saṃśitāni 
AVŚc yair eva sasṛje ghoraṃ tair eva śāntir astu naḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ viṣṇuḥ śaṃ prajāpatiḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ na indro bṛhaspatiḥ śaṃ no bhavatv aryamā 
AVŚa śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ vivasvāṃ cham antakaḥ 
AVŚc utpātāḥ pārthivāntarikṣāḥ śaṃ no divicarā grahāḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ no bhūmir vepyamānā śam ulkā nirhataṃ ca yat 
AVŚc śaṃ gāvo lohitakṣīrāḥ śaṃ bhūmir ava tīryatīḥ 
AVŚa nakṣatram ulkābhihataṃ śam astu naḥ śaṃ no 'bhicārāḥ śam u santu kṛtyāḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ no nikhātā valgāḥ śam ulkā deśopasargāḥ śam u no bhavantu 
AVŚa śaṃ no grahāś cāndramasāḥ śam ādityaś ca rāhuṇā 
AVŚc śaṃ no mṛtyur dhūmaketuḥ śaṃ rudrās tigmatejasaḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ rudrāḥ śaṃ vasavaḥ śam ādityāḥ śam agnayaḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ no maharṣayo devāḥ śaṃ devāḥ śaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ 
AVŚa brahma prajāpatir dhātā lokā vedāḥ saptaṛṣayo 'gnayaḥ 
AVŚc tair me kṛtaṃ svastyayanam indro me śarma yachatu brahmā me śarma yachatu 
AVŚe viśve me devāḥ śarma yachantu sarve me devāḥ śarma yachantu 
AVŚa yāni kāni cic chāntāni loke saptaṛṣayo viduḥ 
AVŚc sarvāṇi śaṃ bhavantu me śaṃ me astv abhayaṃ me astu 
 AVŚa pṛthivī śāntir antarikṣaṃ śāntir dyauḥ śāntir āpaḥ śāntir oṣadhayaḥ śāntir vanaspatayaḥ śāntir viśve me devāḥ śāntiḥ sarve me  
devāḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntibhiḥ  
AVŚc yad iha ghoraṃ yad iha krūraṃ yad iha pāpaṃ tac chāntaṃ tac chivaṃ sarvam eva śam astu naḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ na indrāgnī bhavatām avobhiḥ śaṃ na indrāvaruṇā rātahavyā 
AVŚc śam indrāsomā suvitāya śaṃ yoḥ śaṃ na indrāpūṣaṇā vājasātau 
AVŚa śaṃ no bhagaḥ śam u naḥ śaṃso astu śaṃ naḥ puraṃdhiḥ śam u santu rāyaḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ naḥ satyasya suyamasya śaṃsaḥ śaṃ no aryamā purujāto astu 
AVŚa śaṃ no dhātā śam u dhartā no astu śaṃ na urūcī bhavatu svadhābhiḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ rodasī bṛhatī śaṃ no adriḥ śaṃ no devānāṃ suhavāni santu 
AVŚa śaṃ no agnir jyotiranīko astu śaṃ no mitrāvaruṇāv aśvinā śam 
AVŚc śaṃ naḥ sukṛtāṃ sukṛtāni santu śaṃ na iṣiro abhi vātu vātaḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ no dyāvāpṛthivī pūrvahūtau śam antarikṣaṃ dṛśaye no astu 
AVŚc śaṃ na oṣadhīr vanino bhavantu śaṃ no rajasas patir astu jiṣṇuḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ na indro vasubhir devo astu śam ādityebhir varuṇaḥ suśaṃsaḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ no rudro rudrebhir jalāṣaḥ śaṃ nas tvaṣṭā gnābhir iha śṛṇotu 
AVŚa śaṃ naḥ somo bhavatu brahma śaṃ naḥ śaṃ no grāvāṇaḥ śam u santu yajñāḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ naḥ svarūnāṃ mitayo bhavantu śaṃ naḥ prasvaḥ śam v astu vediḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ naḥ sūrya urucakṣā ud etu śaṃ no bhavantu pradiśaś catasraḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ naḥ parvatā dhruvayo bhavantu śaṃ naḥ sindhavaḥ śam u santv āpaḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ no aditir bhavatu vratebhiḥ śaṃ no bhavantu marutaḥ svarkāḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ no viṣṇuḥ śam u pūṣā no astu śaṃ no bhavitraṃ śam v astu vāyuḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ no devaḥ savitā trāyamāṇaḥ śaṃ no bhavantūṣaso vibhātīḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ naḥ parjanyo bhavatu prajābhyaḥ śaṃ naḥ kṣetrasya patir astu śaṃbhuḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ naḥ satyasya patayo bhavantu śaṃ no arvantaḥ śam u santu gāvaḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ na ṛbhavaḥ sukṛtaḥ suhastāḥ śaṃ no bhavatu pitaro haveṣu 
AVŚa śaṃ no devā viśvadevā bhavantu śaṃ sarasvatī saha dhībhir astu 
AVŚc śam abhiṣācaḥ śam u rātiṣācaḥ śaṃ no divyāḥ pārthivāḥ śaṃ no apyāḥ 
AVŚa śaṃ no aja ekapād devo astu śam ahir budhnyaḥ śaṃ samudraḥ 
AVŚc śaṃ no apāṃ napāt perur astu śaṃ naḥ pṛṣṇir bhavatu devagopā 
AVŚa ādityā rudrā vasavo juṣantām idaṃ brahma kriyamāṇaṃ navīyaḥ 
AVŚc sṛṇvantu no divyāḥ pārthivāso gojātā uta ye yajñiyāsaḥ 
AVŚa ye devānām ṛtvijo yajñiyāso manor yajatrā amṛtā ṛtajñāḥ 
AVŚc te no rāsantām urugāyam adya yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ 
AVŚa tad astu mitrāvaruṇā tad agne śaṃ yor asmabhyam idam astu śastam 
AVŚc aśīmahi gādham uta pratiṣṭhāṃ namo dive bṛhate sādanāya 
AVŚa uṣā apa svasus tamaḥ saṃ vartayati vartaniṃ sujātatā 
AVŚc ayā vājaṃ devahitaṃ sanema madema śatahimāḥ suvīrāḥ 
AVŚa indrasya bāhū sthavirau vṛṣāṇau citrā imā vṛṣabhau pārayiṣṇū 
AVŚc tau yokṣe prathamo yoga āgate yābhyāṃ jitam asurāṇāṃ svar yat 
AVŚa āśuḥ śiśāno vṛṣabho na bhīmo ghanāghanaḥ kṣobhaṇaś carṣaṇīnām 
AVŚc saṃkrandano 'nimiṣa ekavīraḥ śataṃ senā ajayat sākam indraḥ 
AVŚa saṃkrandanenānimiṣeṇa jiṣṇunāyodhyena duścyavanena dhṛṣṇunā 
AVŚc tad indreṇa jayata tat sahadhvaṃ yudho nara iṣuhastena vṛṣṇā 
AVŚa sa iṣuhastaiḥ sa niṣaṅgibhir vaśī saṃsraṣṭā sa yudha indro gaṇena 
AVŚc saṃsṛṣṭajit somapā bāhuśardhy ugradhanvā pratihitābhir astā 
AVŚa balavijñāyaḥ sthaviraḥ pravīraḥ sahasvān vājī sahamāna ugraḥ 
AVŚc abhivīro abhiṣatvā sahojij jaitram indra ratham ā tiṣṭha govidam 
AVŚa imaṃ vīram anu harṣadhvam ugram indraṃ sakhāyo anu saṃ rabhadhvam 
AVŚc grāmajitaṃ gojitaṃ vajrabāhuṃ jayantam ajma pramṛṇantam ojasā 
AVŚa abhi gotrāṇi sahasā gāhamāno 'dāya ugraḥ śatamanyur indraḥ 
AVŚc duścyavanaḥ pṛtanāṣāḍ ayodhyo 'smākaṃ senā avatu pra yutsu 
AVŚa bṛhaspate pari dīyā rathena rakṣohāmitrāṃ apabādhamānaḥ 
AVŚc prabhañjaṃ chatrūn pramṛṇann amitrān asmākam edhy avitā tanūnām 
AVŚa indra eṣāṃ netā bṛhaspatir dakṣiṇā yajñaḥ pura etu somaḥ 
AVŚc devasenānām abhibhañjatīnāṃ jayantīnāṃ maruto yantu madhye 
AVŚa indrasya vṛṣṇo varuṇasya rājña ādityānāṃ marutāṃ śardha ugram 
AVŚc mahāmanasāṃ bhuvanacyavānāṃ ghoṣo devānāṃ jayatām ud asthāt 
AVŚa asmākam indraḥ samṛteṣu dhvajeṣv asmākaṃ yā iṣavas tā jayantu 
AVŚc asmākaṃ vīrā uttare bhavantv asmān devāso 'vatā haveṣu 
AVŚa idam ucchreyo 'vasānam āgāṃ śive me dyāvāpṛthivī abhūtām 
AVŚc asapatnāḥ pradiśo me bhavantu na vai tvā dviṣmo abhayaṃ no astu 
AVŚa yata indra bhayāmahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi 
AVŚc maghavaṃ chagdhi tava tvaṃ na ūtibhir vi dviṣo vi mṛdho jahi 
AVŚa indraṃ vayam anūrādhaṃ havāmahe 'nu rādhyāsma dvipadā catuṣpadā 
AVŚc mā naḥ senā araruṣīr upa gur viṣūcir indra druho vi nāśaya 
AVŚa indras trātota vṛtrahā parasphāno vareṇyaḥ 
AVŚc sa rakṣitā caramataḥ sa madhyataḥ sa paścāt sa purastān no astu 
AVŚa uruṃ no lokam anu neṣi vidvānt svar yaj jyotir abhayaṃ svasti 
AVŚc ugrā ta indra sthavirasya bāhū upa kṣayema śaraṇā bṛhantā 
AVŚa abhayaṃ naḥ karaty antarikṣam abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime 
AVŚc abhayaṃ paścād abhayaṃ purastād uttarād adharād abhayaṃ no astu 
AVŚa abhayaṃ mitrād abhayam amitrād abhayaṃ jñātād abhayaṃ puro yaḥ 
AVŚc abhayaṃ naktam abhayaṃ divā naḥ sarvā āśā mama mitraṃ bhavantu 
AVŚa asapatnaṃ purastāt paścān no abhayaṃ kṛtam 
AVŚc savitā mā dakṣiṇata uttarān mā śacīpatiḥ 
AVŚa divo mādityā rakṣatu bhūmyā rakṣantv agnayaḥ 
AVŚc indrāgnī rakṣatāṃ mā purastād aśvināv abhitaḥ śarma yachatām 
AVŚe tiraścīn aghnyā rakṣatu jātavedā bhūtakṛto me sarvataḥ santu varma 
AVŚa agnir mā pātu vasubhiḥ purastāt tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa vāyur māntarikṣeṇaitasyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa somo mā rudrair dakṣiṇāyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa varuṇo mādityair etasyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānam pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa sūryo mā dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ pratīcyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa āpo mauṣadhīmatīr etasyā diśaḥ pāntu tāsu krame tāsu śraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc tā mā rakṣantu tā mā gopāyantu tābhya ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa viśvakarmā mā saptaṛṣibhir udīcyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa indro mā marutvān etasyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa prajāpatir mā prajananavānt saha pratiṣṭhayā dhruvāyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa bṛhaspatir mā viśvair devair ūrdhvāyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi 
AVŚc sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā 
AVŚa agniṃ te vasuvantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyavaḥ prācyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa vāyuṃ te 'ntarikṣavantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa somaṃ te rudravantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyavo dakṣiṇāyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa varuṇaṃ ta ādityavantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa sūryaṃ te dyāvāpṛthivīvantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyava pratīcyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa apas ta oṣadhīmatīr ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa viśvakarmāṇaṃ te saptaṛṣivantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyava udīcyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa indraṃ te marutvantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa prajāpatiṃ te prajananavantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyavo dhruvāyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa bṛhaspatiṃ te viśvadevavantam ṛchantu 
AVŚc ye māghāyava ūrdhvāyā diśo 'bhidāsān 
AVŚa mitraḥ pṛthivyod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa vāyur antarikṣeṇod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa sūryo divod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa candramā nakṣatrair ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa soma oṣadhībhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa yajño dakṣiṇābhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa samudro nadībhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa brahma brahmacāribhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa indro vīryeṇod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa devā amṛtenod akrāmaṃs tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa prajāpatiḥ prajābhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ 
AVŚc tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu 
AVŚa apa nyadhuḥ pauruṣeyaṃ vadhaṃ yam indrāgnī dhātā savitā bṛhaspatiḥ 
AVŚc somo rājā varuṇo aśvinā yamaḥ pūṣāsmān pari pātu mṛtyoḥ 
AVŚa yāni cakāra bhuvanasya yas patiḥ prajāpatir mātariśvā prajābhyaḥ 
AVŚc pradiśo yāni vasate diśaś ca tāni me varmāṇi bahulāni santu 
AVŚa yat te tanūṣv anahyanta devā dyurājayo dehinaḥ 
AVŚc indro yac cakre varma tad asmān pātu viśvataḥ 
AVŚa varma me dyāvāpṛthivī varmāhar varma sūryaḥ 
AVŚc varma me viśve devāḥ kran mā mā prāpat pratīcikā 
AVŚa gāyatry uṣṇig anuṣṭub bṛhatī paṅktis triṣṭub jagatyai 
AVŚa āṅgirasānām ādyaiḥ pañcānuvākaiḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ṣaṣṭhāya svāhā 
AVŚa saptamāṣṭamābhyāṃ svāhā 
AVŚa nīlanakhebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa haritebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa kṣudrebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa paryāyikebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa prathamebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa dvitīyebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa tṛtīyebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa upottamebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa uttamebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa uttarebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ṛṣibhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa śikhibhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa gaṇebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa mahāgaṇebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa sarvebhyo 'ṅgirobhyo vidagaṇebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa pṛthaksahasrābhyāṃ svāhā 
AVŚa brahmaṇe svāhā 
AVŚa brahmajyeṣṭhā sambhṛtā viryāṇi brahmāgre jyeṣṭhaṃ divam ā tatāna 
AVŚc bhūtānāṃ brahmā prathamota jajñe tenārhati brahmaṇā spardhituṃ kaḥ 
AVŚa ātharvaṇānāṃ caturṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa pañcarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ṣaḷṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa saptarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa aṣṭarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa navarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa daśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ekādaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa dvādaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa trayodaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa caturdaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa pañcadaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ṣoḍaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa saptadaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa aṣṭādaśarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ekonaviṃśatiḥ svāhā 
AVŚa viṃśatiḥ svāhā 
AVŚa mahatkāṇḍāya svāhā 
AVŚa tṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ekarcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa kṣudrebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa ekānṛcebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa rohitebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa sūryābhyāṃ svāhā 
AVŚa vrātyābhyāṃ svāhā 
AVŚa prājāpatyābhyāṃ svāhā 
AVŚa viṣāsahyai svāhā 
AVŚa maṅgalikebhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa brahmaṇe svāhā 
AVŚa brahmajyeṣṭhā saṃbhṛtā vīryāṇi brahmāgre jyeṣṭhaṃ divam ā tatāna 
AVŚc bhūtānāṃ brahmā prathamota jajñe tenārhati brahmaṇā spardhituṃ kaḥ 
AVŚa yena devaṃ savitāraṃ pari devā adhārayan 
AVŚc tenemaṃ brahmaṇas pate pari rāṣṭrāya dhattana 
AVŚa parīmam indram āyuṣe mahe kṣatrāya dhattana 
AVŚc yathainaṃ jarase nayāj jyok kṣatre 'dhi jāgarat 
AVŚa parīmam indram āyuṣe mahe śrotrāya dhattana 
AVŚc yathainaṃ jarase nayāj jyok śrotre 'dhi jāgarat 
AVŚa pari dhatta dhatta no varcasemaṃ jarāmṛtyuṃ kṛṇuta dīrgham āyuḥ 
AVŚc bṛhaspatiḥ prāyachad vāsa etat somāya rājñe paridhātavā u 
AVŚa jarāṃ su gacha pari dhatsva vāso bhavā gṛṣṭīnām abhiśastipā u 
AVŚc śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcī rāyaś ca poṣam upasaṃvyayasva 
AVŚa parīdaṃ vāso adhithāḥ svastaye 'bhūr vāpīnām abhiśastipā u 
AVŚc śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcīr vasūni cārur vi bhajāsi jīvan 
AVŚa yogeyoge tavastaraṃ vājevāje havāmahe 
AVŚc sakhāya indram ūtaye 
AVŚa hiraṇyavarṇo ajaraḥ suvīro jarāmṛtyuḥ prajayā saṃ viśasva 
AVŚc tad agnir āha tad u soma āha bṛhaspatiḥ savitā tad indraḥ 
AVŚa aśrāntasya tvā manasā yunajmi prathamasya ca 
AVŚc utkūlam udvaho bhavoduhya prati dhāvatāt 
AVŚa agneḥ prajātaṃ pari yad dhiraṇyam amṛtaṃ dadhre adhi martyeṣu 
AVŚc ya enad veda sa id enam arhati jarāmṛtyur bhavati yo bibharti 
AVŚa yad dhiraṇyaṃ sūryeṇa suvarṇam prajāvanto manavaḥ pūrva īṣire 
AVŚc tat tvā candraṃ varcasā saṃ sṛjaty āyuṣmān bhavati yo bibharti 
AVŚa āyuṣe tvā varcase tvaujase ca balāya ca 
AVŚc yathā hiraṇyatejasā vibhāsāsi janāṃ anu 
AVŚa yad veda rājā varuṇo veda devo bṛhaspatiḥ 
AVŚc indro yad vṛtrahā veda tat ta āyuṣyaṃ bhuvat tat te varcasyaṃ bhuvat 
AVŚa gobhiṣ ṭvā pātv ṛṣabho vṛṣā tvā pātu vājibhiḥ 
AVŚc vāyuṣ ṭvā brahmaṇā pātv indras tvā pātv indriyaiḥ 
AVŚa somas tvā pātv oṣadhībhir nakṣatraiḥ pātu sūryaḥ 
AVŚc mādbhyas tvā candro vṛtrahā vātaḥ prāṇena rakṣatu 
AVŚa tisro divas tisraḥ pṛthivīs trīṇy antarikṣāṇi caturaḥ samudrān 
AVŚc trivṛtaṃ stomaṃ trivṛta āpa āhus tās tvā rakṣantu trivṛtā trivṛdbhiḥ 
AVŚa trīn nākāṃs trīn samudrāṃs trīn bradhnāṃs trīn vaiṣṭapān 
AVŚc trīn mātariśvanas trīnt sūryān goptṝn kalpayāmi te 
AVŚa ghṛtena tvā sam ukṣāmy agne ājyena vardhayan 
AVŚc agneś candrasya sūryasya mā prāṇaṃ māyino dabhan 
AVŚa mā vaḥ prāṇaṃ mā vo 'pānaṃ mā haro māyino dabhan 
AVŚc bhrājanto viśvavedaso devā daivyena dhāvata 
AVŚa prāṇenāgniṃ saṃ sṛjati vātaḥ prāṇena saṃhitaḥ 
AVŚc prāṇena viśvatomukhaṃ sūryaṃ devā ajanayan 
AVŚa āyuṣāyuḥkṛtāṃ jīvāyuṣmān jīva mā mṛthāḥ 
AVŚc prāṇenātmanvatām jīva mā mṛtyor ud agā vaśam 
AVŚa devānāṃ nihitaṃ nidhiṃ yam indro 'nvavindat pathibhir devayānaiḥ 
AVŚc āpo hiraṇyaṃ jugupus trivṛdbhis tās tvā rakṣantu trivṛtā trivṛdbhiḥ 
AVŚa trayastriṃśad devatās trīṇi ca vīryāṇi priyāyamāṇā jugupur apsv antaḥ 
AVŚc asmiṃś candre adhi yad dhiraṇyaṃ tenāyaṃ kṛṇavad vīryāṇi 
AVŚa ye devā divy ekādaśa stha te devāso havir idaṃ juṣadhvam 
AVŚa ye devā antarikṣa ekādaśa stha te devāso havir idaṃ juṣadhvam 
AVŚa ye devā pṛthivyām ekādaśa stha te devāso havir idaṃ juṣadhvam 
AVŚa asapatnaṃ purastāt paścān no abhayaṃ kṛtam 
AVŚc savitā mā dakṣiṇata uttarān mā śacīpatiḥ 
AVŚa divo mādityā rakṣantu bhūmyā rakṣantv agnayaḥ 
AVŚc indrāgnī rakṣatāṃ mā purastād aśvināv abhitaḥ śarma yachatām 
AVŚe tiraścīn aghnyā rakṣatu jātavedā bhūtakṛto me sarvataḥ santu varma 
AVŚa imaṃ badhnāmi te maṇiṃ dīrghāyutvāya tejase 
AVŚc darbhaṃ sapatnadambhanaṃ dviṣatas tapanaṃ hṛdaḥ 
AVŚa dviṣatas tāpayan hṛdaḥ śatrūṇāṃ tāpayan manaḥ 
AVŚc durhārdaḥ sarvāṃs tvaṃ darbha gharma ivābhīnt saṃtāpayan 
AVŚa gharma ivābhitapan darbha dviṣato nitapan maṇe 
AVŚc hṛdaḥ sapatnānāṃ bhinddhīndra iva virujaṃ balam 
AVŚa bhinddhi darbha sapatnānāṃ hṛdayaṃ dviṣatāṃ maṇe 
AVŚc udyan tvacam iva bhūmyāḥ śira eṣāṃ vi pātaya 
AVŚa bhinddhi darbha sapatnān me bhinddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc bhinddhi me sarvān durhārdo bhinddhi me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa chinddhi darbha sapatnān me chinddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc chinddhi me sarvān durhārdo chinddhi me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa vṛśca darbha sapatnān me vṛśca me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc vṛśca me sarvān durhārdo vṛśca me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa kṛnta darbha sapatnān me kṛnta me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc kṛnta me sarvān durhārdo kṛnta me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa piṃśa darbha sapatnān me piṃśa me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc piṃśa me sarvān durhārdo piṃśa me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa vidhya darbha sapatnān me vidhya me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc vidhya me sarvān durhārdo vidhya me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa nikṣa darbha sapatnān me nikṣa me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc nikṣa me sarvān durhārdo nikṣa me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa tṛnddhi darbha sapatnān me tṛnddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc tṛnddhi me sarvān durhārdo tṛnddhi me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa runddhi darbha sapatnān me runddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc runddhi me sarvān durhārdo runddhi me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa mṛṇa darbha sapatnān me mṛṇa me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc mṛṇa me sarvān durhārdo mṛṇa me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa mantha darbha sapatnān me mantha me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc mantha me sarvān durhārdo mantha me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa piṇḍḍhi darbha sapatnān me piṇḍḍhi me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc piṇḍḍhi me sarvān durhārdo piṇḍḍhi me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa oṣa darbha sapatnān me oṣa me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc oṣa me sarvān durhārdo oṣa me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa daha darbha sapatnān me daha me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc daha me sarvān durhārdo daha me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa jahi darbha sapatnān me jahi me pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc jahi me sarvān durhārdo jahi me dviṣato maṇe 
AVŚa yat te darbha jarāmṛtyu śataṃ varmasu varma te 
AVŚc tenemaṃ varmiṇaṃ kṛtvā sapatnāṃ jahi vīryaiḥ 
AVŚa śataṃ te darbha varmāṇi sahasraṃ vīryāṇi te 
AVŚc tam asmai viśve tvāṃ devā jarase bhartavā aduḥ 
AVŚa tvām āhur devavarma tvāṃ darbha brahmaṇas patim 
AVŚc tvām indrasyāhur varma tvaṃ rāṣṭrāṇi rakṣasi 
AVŚa sapatnakṣayaṇaṃ darbha dviṣatas tapanaṃ hṛdaḥ 
AVŚc maṇiṃ kṣatrasya vardhanaṃ tanūpānaṃ kṛṇomi te 
AVŚa yat samudro abhyakrandat parjanyo vidyutā saha 
AVŚc tato hiranyayo bindus tato darbho ajāyata 
AVŚa audumbareṇa maṇinā puṣṭikāmāya vedhasā 
AVŚc paśūṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ sphātiṃ goṣṭhe me savitā karat 
AVŚa yo no agnir gārhapatyaḥ paśūnām adhipā asat 
AVŚc audumbaro vṛṣā maṇiḥ saṃ mā sṛjatu puṣṭyā 
AVŚa karīṣiṇīṃ phalavatīṃ svadhām irāṃ ca no gṛhe 
AVŚc audumbarasya tejasā dhātā puṣṭiṃ dadhātu me 
AVŚa yad dvipāc ca catuṣpāc ca yāny annāni ye rasāḥ 
AVŚc gṛhṇe 'haṃ tv eṣāṃ bhūmānaṃ bibhrad audumbaraṃ maṇim 
AVŚa puṣṭiṃ paśūnām pari jagrabhāhaṃ catuṣpadāṃ dvipadāṃ yac ca dhānyam 
AVŚc payaḥ paśūnāṃ rasam oṣadhīnāṃ bṛhaspatiḥ savitā me ni yachāt 
AVŚa ahaṃ paśūnām adhipā asāni mayi puṣṭaṃ puṣṭapatir dadhātu 
AVŚc mahyam audumbaro maṇir draviṇāni ni yachatu 
AVŚa upa maudumbaro maṇiḥ prajayā ca dhanena ca 
AVŚc indreṇa jinvito maṇir ā māgant saha varcasā 
AVŚa devo maṇiḥ sapatnahā dhanasā dhanasātaye 
AVŚc paśor annasya bhūmānaṃ gavāṃ sphātiṃ ni yachatu 
AVŚa yathāgre tvaṃ vanaspate puṣṭhyā saha jajñiṣe 
AVŚc evā dhanasya me sphātim ā dadhātu sarasvatī 
AVŚa ā me dhanaṃ sarasvatī payasphātiṃ ca dhānyam 
AVŚc sinīvāly upā vahād ayaṃ caudumbaro maṇiḥ 
AVŚa tvaṃ maṇīṇām adhipā vṛṣāsi tvayi puṣṭaṃ puṣṭapatir jajāna 
AVŚc tvayīme vājā draviṇāni sarvaudumbaraḥ sa tvam asmat sahasvārād ārād arātim amatiṃ kṣudhaṃ ca 
AVŚa grāmaṇīr asi grāmaṇīr utthāya abhiṣikto 'bhi mā siñca varcasā 
AVŚc tejo 'si tejo mayi dhārayādhi rayir asi rayiṃ me dhehi 
AVŚa puṣṭir asi puṣṭyā mā sam aṅgdhi gṛhamedhī gṛhapatiṃ mā kṛṇu 
AVŚc audumbaraḥ sa tvam asmāsu dhehi rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīraṃ ni yacha rāyas poṣāya prati muñce ahaṃ tvām 
AVŚa ayam audumbaro maṇir vīro vīrāya badhyate 
AVŚc sa naḥ saniṃ madhumatīṃ kṛṇotu rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīram ni yachāt 
AVŚa śatakāṇḍo duścyavanaḥ sahasraparṇa uttiraḥ 
AVŚc darbho ya ugra oṣadhis taṃ te badhnāmy āyuṣe 
AVŚa nāsya keśān pra vapanti norasi tāḍam ā ghnate 
AVŚc yasmā achinnaparṇena darbhena śarma yachati 
AVŚa divi te tūlam oṣadhe pṛthivyām asi niṣṭhitaḥ 
AVŚc tvayā sahasrakāṇḍenāyuḥ pra vardhayāmahe 
AVŚa tisro divo aty atṛṇat tisra imāḥ pṛthivīr uta 
AVŚc tvayāhaṃ durhārdo jihvāṃ ni tṛṇadmi vacāṃsi 
AVŚa tvam asi sahamāno 'ham asmi sahasvān 
AVŚc ubhau sahasvantau bhūtvā sapatnān sahiṣīvahi 
AVŚa sahasva no abhimātiṃ sahasva pṛtanāyataḥ 
AVŚc sahasva sarvān durhārdaḥ suhārdo me bahūn kṛdhi 
AVŚa darbheṇa devajātena divi ṣṭambhena śaśvad it 
AVŚc tenāhaṃ śaśvato janāṃ asanaṃ sanavāni ca 
AVŚa priyaṃ mā darbha kṛṇu brahmarājanyābhyām śūdrāya cāryāya ca 
AVŚc yasmai ca kāmayāmahe sarvasmai ca vipaśyate 
AVŚa yo jāyamānaḥ pṛthivīm adṛṃhad yo astabhnād antarikṣaṃ divaṃ ca 
AVŚc yaṃ bibhrataṃ nanu pāpmā viveda sa no 'yaṃ darbho varuṇo divā kaḥ 
AVŚa sapatnahā śatakāṇḍaḥ sahasvān oṣadhīnāṃ prathamaḥ saṃ babhūva 
AVŚc sa no 'yaṃ darbhaḥ pari pātu viśvatas tena sākṣīya pṛtanāḥ pṛtanyataḥ 
AVŚa sahasrārghaḥ śatakāṇḍaḥ payasvān apām agnir vīrudhāṃ rājasūyam 
AVŚc sa no 'yaṃ darbhaḥ pari pātu viśvato devo maṇir āyuṣā saṃ sṛjāti naḥ 
AVŚa ghṛtād ullupto madhumān payasvān bhūmidṛṃho 'cyutaś cyāvayiṣṇuḥ 
AVŚc nudant sapatnān adharāṃś ca kṛṇvan darbhā roha mahatām indriyeṇa 
AVŚa tvaṃ bhūmim aty eṣy ojasā tvaṃ vedyāṃ sīdasi cārur adhvare 
AVŚc tvāṃ pavitram ṛṣayo 'bharanta tvaṃ punīhi duritāny asmat 
AVŚa tīkṣṇo rājā viṣāsahī rakṣohā viśvacarṣaṇiḥ 
AVŚc ojo devānāṃ balam ugram etat taṃ te badhnāmi jarase svastaye 
AVŚa darbheṇa tvaṃ kṛṇavad vīryāṇi darbhaṃ bibhrad ātmanā mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ 
AVŚc atiṣṭhāya varcasādhānyānt sūrya ivā bhāhi pradiśaś catasraḥ 
AVŚa jāṅgiḍo 'si jaṅgiḍo rakṣitāsi jaṅgidaḥ 
AVŚc dvipāc catuṣpād asmākaṃ sarvaṃ rakṣatu jaṅgidaḥ 
AVŚa yā gṛtsyas tripañcāśīḥ śataṃ kṛtyākṛtaś ca ye 
AVŚc sarvān vinaktu tejaso 'rasāṃ jaṅgidas karat 
AVŚa arasaṃ kṛtrimaṃ nādam arasāḥ sapta visrasaḥ 
AVŚc apeto jaṅgiḍāmatim iṣum asteva śātaya 
AVŚa kṛtyādūṣaṇa evāyam atho arātidūṣaṇaḥ 
AVŚc atho sahasvāñ jaṅgiḍaḥ pra na āyumṣi tāriṣat 
AVŚa sa jaṅgiḍasya mahimā pari ṇaḥ pātu viśvataḥ 
AVŚc viṣkandhaṃ yena sāsaha saṃskandham oja ojasā 
AVŚa triṣ ṭvā devā ajanayan niṣṭhitaṃ bhūmyām adhi 
AVŚc tam u tvāṅgirā iti brāhmaṇāḥ pūrvyā viduḥ 
AVŚa na tvā pūrvā oṣadhayo na tvā taranti yā navāḥ 
AVŚc vibādha ugro jaṅgiḍaḥ paripāṇaḥ sumaṅgalaḥ 
AVŚa athopadāna bhagavo jāṅgiḍāmitavīrya 
AVŚc purā ta ugrā grasata upendro vīryaṃ dadau 
AVŚa ugra it te vanaspata indra ojmānam ā dadhau 
AVŚc amīvāḥ sarvāś cātayaṃ jahi rakṣāṃsy oṣadhe 
AVŚa āśarīkaṃ viśarīkaṃ balāsaṃ pṛṣṭyāmayam 
AVŚc takmānaṃ viśvaśāradam arasāṃ jaṅgiḍas karat 
AVŚa indrasya nāma gṛhṇanta ṛsayo jaṅgidaṃ daduḥ 
AVŚc devā yaṃ cakrur bheṣajam agre viṣkandhadūṣaṇam 
AVŚa sa no rakṣatu jaṅgiḍo dhanapālo dhaneva 
AVŚc devā yaṃ cakrur brāhmaṇāḥ paripāṇam arātiham 
AVŚa durhārdaḥ saṃghoraṃ cakṣuḥ pāpakṛtvānam āgamam 
AVŚc tāṃs tvaṃ sahasracakṣo pratībodhena nāśaya paripāṇo 'si jaṅgiḍaḥ 
AVŚa pari mā divaḥ pari mā pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣāt pari mā vīrudbhyaḥ 
AVŚc pari mā bhūtāt pari mota bhavyād diśodiśo jaṅgiḍaḥ pātv asmān 
AVŚa ya ṛṣṇavo devakṛtā ya uto vavṛte 'nyaḥ 
AVŚc sarvāṃ stān viśvabheṣajo 'rasāṃ jaṅgiḍas karat 
AVŚa śatavāro anīnaśad yakṣmān rakṣāṃsi tejasā 
AVŚc ārohan varcasā saha maṇir durṇāmacātanaḥ 
AVŚa śṛṅgābhyāṃ rakṣo nudate mūlena yātudhānyaḥ 
AVŚc madhyena yakṣmaṃ bādhate nainaṃ pāpmāti tatrati 
AVŚa ye yakṣmāso arbhakā mahānto ye ca śabdinaḥ 
AVŚc sarvāṃ durṇāmahā maṇiḥ śatavāro anīnaśat 
AVŚa śataṃ vīrān ajanayac chataṃ yakṣmān apāvapat 
AVŚc durṇāmnaḥ sarvān hatvāva rakṣāṃsi dhūnute 
AVŚa hiraṇyaśṛṅga ṛṣabhaḥ śātavāro ayaṃ maṇiḥ 
AVŚc durṇāmnaḥ sarvāṃs tṛdhvāva rakṣāṃsy akramīt 
AVŚa śatam ahaṃ durṇāmnīnāṃ gandharvāpsarasāṃ śatam 
AVŚc śatam śaśvanvatīnāṃ śatavāreṇa vāraye 
AVŚa idaṃ varco agninā dattam āgan bhargo yaśaḥ saha ojo vayo balam 
AVŚc trayastriṃśad yāni ca vīryāṇi tāny agniḥ pra dadātu me 
AVŚa varca ā dhehi me tanvāṃ saha ojo vayo balam 
AVŚc indriyāya tvā karmaṇe vīryāya prati gṛhṇāmi śataśāradāya 
AVŚa ūrje tvā balāya tvaujase sahase tvā 
AVŚc abhibhūyāya tvā rāṣṭrabhṛtyāya pary ūhāmi śataśāradāya 
AVŚa ṛtubhyaṣ ṭvārtavebhyo mādbhyaḥ saṃvatsarebhyaḥ 
AVŚc dhātre vidhātre samṛdhe bhūtasya pataye yaje 
AVŚa na taṃ yakṣmā arundhate nainaṃ śapatho aśnute 
AVŚc yaṃ bheṣajasya gulguloḥ surabhir gandho aśnute 
AVŚa viṣvañcas tasmād yakṣmā mṛgā aśvā iverate 
AVŚc yad gulgulu saindhavaṃ yad vāpy asi samudriyam 
AVŚa ubhayor agrabhaṃ nāmāsmā ariṣṭatātaye 
AVŚa aitu devas trāyamāṇaḥ kuṣṭho himavatas pari 
AVŚc takmānaṃ sarvaṃ nāśaya sarvāś ca yātudhānyaḥ 
AVŚa trīṇi te kuṣṭha nāmāni nadyamāro nadyāriṣaḥ 
AVŚc nadyāyaṃ puruṣo riṣat 
AVŚe yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyaṃprātar atho divā 
AVŚa jīvalā nāma te mātā jīvanto nāma te pitā 
AVŚc nadyāyaṃ puruṣo riṣat 
AVŚe yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyaṃprātar atho divā 
AVŚa uttamo asy oṣadhīnām anaḍvān jagatām iva vyāghraḥ śvapadām iva 
AVŚc nadyāyaṃ puruṣo riṣat 
AVŚe yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyaṃprātar atho divā 
AVŚa triḥ śāmbubhyo aṅgirebhyas trir ādityebhyas pari 
AVŚc trir jāto viśvadevebhyaḥ 
AVŚe sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati 
AVŚa aśvattho devasadanas tṛtīyasyām ito divi 
AVŚc tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuṣṭho ajāyata 
AVŚe sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati 
AVŚa hiraṇyayī naur acarad dhiraṇyabandhanā divi 
AVŚc tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuṣṭho ajāyata 
AVŚe sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati 
AVŚa yatra nāvaprabhraṃśanaṃ yatra himavataḥ śiraḥ 
AVŚc tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuṣṭho ajāyata 
AVŚe sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati 
AVŚa yaṃ tvā veda pūrva ikṣvāko yaṃ vā tvā kuṣṭha kāmyaḥ 
AVŚc yaṃ vā vaso yam ātsyas tenāsi viśvabheṣajaḥ 
AVŚa śīrṣaśokaṃ tṛtīyakaṃ sadaṃdir yaś ca hāyanaḥ 
AVŚc takmānaṃ viśvadhāvīryādharāñcaṃ parā suva 
AVŚa yan me chidraṃ manaso yac ca vācaḥ sarasvatī manyumantaṃ jagāma 
AVŚc viśvais tad devaiḥ saha saṃvidānaḥ saṃ dadhātu bṛhaspatiḥ 
AVŚa mā na āpo medhāṃ mā brahma pra mathiṣṭana 
AVŚc suṣyadā yūyaṃ syandadhvam upahūto 'haṃ sumedhā varcasvī 
AVŚa mā no medhāṃ mā no dīkṣāṃ mā no hiṃsiṣṭaṃ yat tapaḥ 
AVŚc śivā naḥ śaṃ santv āyuṣe śivā bhavantu mātaraḥ 
AVŚa yā naḥ pīparad aśvinā jyotiṣmatī tamas tiraḥ 
AVŚc tām asme rāsatām iṣam 
AVŚa bhadram ichanta ṛṣayaḥ svarvidas tapo dīkṣām upaniṣedur agre 
AVŚc tato rāṣṭraṃ balam ojaś ca jātaṃ tad asmai devā upasaṃnamantu 
AVŚa brahma hotā brahma yajñā brahmaṇā svaravo mitāḥ 
AVŚc adhvaryur brahmaṇo jāto brahmaṇo 'ntarhitaṃ haviḥ 
AVŚa brahma sruco ghṛtavatīr brahmaṇā vedir uddhitā 
AVŚc brahma yajñasya tattvaṃ ca ṛtvijo ye haviṣkṛtaḥ 
AVŚe śamitāya svāhā 
AVŚa aṃhomuce pra bhare manīṣām ā sutrāvṇe sumatim āvṛṇānaḥ 
AVŚc imam indra prati havyaṃ gṛbhāya satyāḥ santu yajamānasya kāmāḥ 
AVŚa aṃhomucaṃ vrṣabhaṃ yajñiyānāṃ virājantaṃ prathamam adhvarāṇam 
AVŚc apāṃ napātam aśvinā huve dhiya indriyeṇa ta indriyaṃ dattam ojaḥ 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc agnir mā tatra nayatv agnir medhā dadhātu me 
AVŚe agnaye svāhā 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc vāyur mā tatra nayatu vāyuḥ praṇān dadhātu me vāyave svāhā 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc sūryo mā tatra nayatu cakṣuḥ sūryo dadhātu me 
AVŚe sūryāya svāhā 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc candro mā tatra nayatu manaś candro dadhātu me 
AVŚe candrāya svāhā 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc somo mā tatra nayatu payaḥ somo dadhātu me 
AVŚe somāya svāhā 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc indro mā tatra nayatu balam indro dadhātu me 
AVŚe indrāya svāhā 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc āpo mā tatra nayatv amṛtam mopa tiṣṭhatu 
AVŚe adbhyaḥ svāhā 
AVŚa yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha 
AVŚc brahmā mā tatra nayatu brahmā brahma dadhātu me 
AVŚe brahmaṇe svāhā 
AVŚa āyuṣo 'si prataraṇaṃ vipraṃ bheṣajam ucyase 
AVŚc tad āñjana tvaṃ śaṃtāte śam āpo abhayaṃ kṛtam 
AVŚa yo harimā jāyānyo 'ṅgabhedo viṣalpakaḥ 
AVŚc sarvaṃ te yakṣmam aṅgebhyo bahir nir hantv āñjanam 
AVŚa āñjanaṃ pṛthivyāṃ jātaṃ bhadraṃ puruṣajīvanam 
AVŚc kṛṇotv apramāyukaṃ rathajūtim anāgasam 
AVŚa prāṇa prāṇaṃ trāyasvāso asave mṛḍa 
AVŚc nirṛte nirṛtyā naḥ pāśebhyo muñca 
AVŚa sindhor garbho 'si vidyutāṃ puṣpam 
AVŚc vātaḥ prāṇaḥ sūryaś cakṣur divas payaḥ 
AVŚa devāñjana traikakuda pari mā pāhi viśvataḥ 
AVŚc na tvā taranty oṣadhayo bāhyāḥ parvatīyā uta 
AVŚa vīdaṃ madhyam avāsṛpad rakṣohāmīvacātanaḥ 
AVŚc amīvāḥ sarvāś cātayan nāśayad abhibhā itaḥ 
AVŚa bahv idaṃ rājan varuṇānṛtam āha pūruṣaḥ 
AVŚc tasmāt sahasravīrya muñca naḥ pary aṃhasaḥ 
AVŚa yad āpo aghnyā iti varuṇeti yad ūcima 
AVŚc tasmāt sahasravīrya muñca naḥ pary aṃhasaḥ 
AVŚa mitraś ca tvā varuṇaś cānupreyatur āñjana 
AVŚc tau tvānugatya dūraṃ bhogāya punar ohatuḥ 
AVŚa ṛṇād ṛṇam iva saṃ naya kṛtyāṃ kṛtyākṛto gṛham 
AVŚc cakṣurmantrasya durhārdaḥ pṛṣṭīr api śṛṇāñjana 
AVŚa yad asmāsu duṣvapnyaṃ yad goṣu yac ca no gṛhe 
AVŚc anāmagas taṃ ca durhārdaḥ priyaḥ prati muñcatām 
AVŚa apām ūrja ojaso vāvṛdhānam agner jātam adhi jātavedasaḥ 
AVŚc caturvīraṃ parvatīyaṃ yad āñjanaṃ diśaḥ pradiśaḥ karad ic chivās te 
AVŚa caturvīraṃ badhyata āñjanaṃ te sarvā diśo abhayās te bhavantu 
AVŚc dhruvas tiṣṭhāsi saviteva cārya imā viśo abhi harantu te balim 
AVŚa ākṣvaikaṃ maṇim ekaṃ krṇuṣva snāhy ekenā pibaikam eṣām 
AVŚc caturvīraṃ nairṛtebhyaś caturbhyo grāhyā bandhebhyaḥ pari pātv asmān 
AVŚa agnir māgnināvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase 
AVŚc tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā 
AVŚa indro mendriyeṇāvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase 
AVŚc tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā 
AVŚa somo mā saumyenāvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase 
AVŚc tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā 
AVŚa bhago ma bhagenāvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase 
AVŚc tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā 
AVŚa maruto mā gaṇair avantu prāṇāyāpānāyuṣe varcasa ojase tejase 
AVŚc svastaye subhūtaye svāhā 
AVŚa prajāpatiṣ ṭvā badhnāt prathamam astṛtaṃ vīryāya kam 
AVŚc tat te badhnāmy āyuṣe varcasa ojase ca balāya cāstṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa ūrdhvas tiṣṭhatu rakṣann apramādam astṛtemam mā tvā dabhan paṇayo yātudhānāḥ 
AVŚc indra iva dasyūn ava dhūnuṣva pṛtanyataḥ sarvāṃ chatrūn vi ṣahasvāstṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa śataṃ ca na praharanto nighnanto na tastire 
AVŚc tasminn indraḥ pary adatta cakṣuḥ prāṇam atho balam astṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa indrasya tvā varmaṇā pari dhāpayāmo yo devānām adhirājo babhūva 
AVŚc punas tvā devāḥ pra ṇayantu sarve 'stṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa asmin maṇāv ekaśataṃ vīryāṇi sahasraṃ prāṇā asminn astṛte 
AVŚc vyāghraḥ śatrūn abhi tiṣṭha sarvān yas tvā pṛtanyād adharaḥ so astv astṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa ghṛtād ullupto madhumān payasvānt sahasraprāṇaḥ śatayonir vayodhāḥ 
AVŚc śambhūś ca mayobhūś corjasvāṃś ca payasvāṃś cāstṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa yathā tvam uttaro 'so asapatnaḥ sapatnahā 
AVŚc sajātānām asad vaśī tathā tvā savitā karad astṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu 
AVŚa ā rātri pārthivaṃ rajaḥ pitur aprāyi dhāmabhiḥ 
AVŚc divaḥ sadāṃsi bṛhatī vi tiṣṭhasa ā tveṣaṃ vartate tamaḥ 
AVŚa na yasyāḥ pāraṃ dadṛśe na yoyuvad viśvam asyāṃ ni viśate yad ejati 
AVŚc ariṣṭāsas ta urvi tamasvati rātri pāram aśīmahi bhadre pāram aśīmahi 
AVŚa ye te rātri nṛcakṣaso draṣṭāro navatir nava 
AVŚc aśītiḥ santy aṣṭā uto te sapta saptatiḥ 
AVŚa ṣaṣṭiś ca ṣaṭ ca revati pañcāśat pañca sumnayi 
AVŚc catvāraś catvāriṃśac ca trayas triṃśac ca vājini 
AVŚa dvau ca te viṃśatiś ca te rātry ekādaśāvamāḥ 
AVŚc tebhir no adya pāyubhir nu pāhi duhitar divaḥ 
AVŚa rakṣā mākir no aghaśaṃsa īśata mā no duḥśaṃsa īśata 
AVŚc mā no adya gavāṃ steno māvīnāṃ vṛka īśata 
AVŚa māśvānāṃ bhadre taskaro mā nṛṇāṃ yātudhānyaḥ 
AVŚc paramebhiḥ pathibhi steno dhāvatu taskaraḥ 
AVŚe pareṇa datvatī rajjuḥ pareṇāghāyur arṣatu 
AVŚa adha rātri tṛṣṭadhūmam aśīrṣāṇam ahiṃ kṛṇu 
AVŚc hanū vṛkasya jambhayā stenaṃ drupade jahi 
AVŚa tvayi rātri vasāmasi svapiṣyāmasi jāgṛhi 
AVŚc gobhyo naḥ śarma yachāśvebhyaḥ puruṣebhyaḥ 
AVŚa atho yāni ca yasmā ha yāni cāntaḥ parīṇahi 
AVŚc tāni te pari dadmasi 
AVŚa rātri mātar uṣase naḥ pari dehi 
AVŚc uṣā no ahne pari dadātv ahas tubhyaṃ vibhāvari 
AVŚa yat kiṃ cedaṃ patayati yat kiṃ cedaṃ sarīsṛpam 
AVŚc yat kiṃ ca parvatāyāsatvaṃ tasmāt tvaṃ rātri pāhi naḥ 
AVŚa sā paścāt pāhi sā puraḥ sottarād adharād uta 
AVŚc gopāya no vibhāvari stotāras ta iha smasi 
AVŚa ye rātrim anutiṣṭhanti ye ca bhūteṣu jāgrati 
AVŚc paśūn ye sarvān rakṣanti te na ātmasu jāgrati te naḥ paśuṣu jāgrati 
AVŚa veda vai rātri te nāma ghṛtācī nāma vā asi 
AVŚc tāṃ tvāṃ bharadvājo veda sā no vitte 'dhi jāgrati 
AVŚa iṣirā yoṣā yuvatir damūnā rātrī devasya savitur bhagasya 
AVŚc aśvakṣabhā suhavā saṃbhṛtaśrīr ā paprau dyāvāpṛthivī mahitvā 
AVŚa ati viśvāny aruhad gambhiro varṣiṣṭham aruhanta śraviṣṭhāḥ 
AVŚc uśatī rātry anu sā bhadrābhi tiṣṭhate mitra iva svadhābhiḥ 
AVŚa varye vande subhage sujāta ājagan rātri sumanā iha syām 
AVŚc asmāṃs trāyasva naryāṇi jātā atho yāni gavyāni puṣṭyā 
AVŚa siṃhasya rātry uśatī pīṃṣasya vyāghrasya dvīpino varca ā dade 
AVŚc aśvasya bradhnaṃ puruṣasya māyuṃ puru rūpāṇi kṛṇuṣe vibhātī 
AVŚa śivāṃ rātrim anusūryaṃ ca himasya mātā suhavā no astu 
AVŚc asya stomasya subhage ni bodha yena tvā vande viśvāsu dikṣu 
AVŚa stomasya no vibhāvari rātri rājeva joṣase 
AVŚc asāma sarvavīrā bhavāma sarvavedaso vyuchantīr anūṣasaḥ 
AVŚa śamyā ha nāma dadhiṣe mama dipsanti ye dhanā 
AVŚc rātrīhi tān asutapā ya steno na vidyate yat punar na vidyate 
AVŚa bhadrāsi rātri camaso na viṣṭo viṣvaṅ gorūpaṃ yuvatir bibharṣi 
AVŚc cakṣuṣmatī me uśatī vapūmṣi prati tvaṃ divyā na kṣām amukthāḥ 
AVŚa yo adya stena āyaty aghāyur martyo ripuḥ 
AVŚc rātrī tasya pratītya pra grīvāḥ pra śiro hanat 
AVŚa pra pādau na yathāyati pra hastau na yathāśiṣat 
AVŚc yo malimlur upāyati sa saṃpiṣṭo apāyati 
AVŚe apāyati svapāyati śuṣke sthāṇāv apāyati 
AVŚa adha rātri tṛṣṭadhūmam aśīrṣāṇam ahiṃ kṛṇu 
AVŚc akṣau vṛkasya nir jahyās tena taṃ drupade jahi 
AVŚa ye te rātry anaḍvāhas tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāḥ svāśavaḥ 
AVŚc tebhir no adya pārayāti durgāṇi viśvahā 
AVŚa rātriṃrātrim ariṣyantas tarema tanvā vayam 
AVŚc gambhīram aplavā iva na tareyur arātayaḥ 
AVŚa yathā śāmyākaḥ prapatann apavān nānuvidyate 
AVŚc evā rātri pra pātaya yo asmāṃ abhyaghāyati 
AVŚa apa stenaṃ vāsayo goajam uta taskaram 
AVŚc atho yo arvataḥ śiro 'bhidhāya ninīṣati 
AVŚa yad adya rātri subhage vibhajanty ayo vasu 
AVŚc yad etad asmān bhojaya yathed anyān upāyasi 
AVŚa uṣase naḥ pari dehi sarvān rātry anāgasaḥ 
AVŚc uṣā no ahne ā bhajād ahas tubhyaṃ vibhāvari 
AVŚa ayuto 'ham ayuto ma ātmāyutaṃ me cakṣur ayutaṃ me śrotram 
AVŚc ayuto me prāṇo 'yuto me 'pāno 'yuto me vyāno 'yuto 'haṃ sarvaḥ 
AVŚa devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ prasūta ā rabhe 
AVŚa kāmas tad agre sam avartata manaso retaḥ prathamaṃ yad āsīt 
AVŚc sa kāma kāmena bṛhatā sayonī rāyas poṣaṃ yajamānāya dhehi 
AVŚa tvaṃ kāma sahasāsi pratiṣṭhito vibhur vibhāvā sakha ā sakhīyate 
AVŚc tvam ugraḥ pṛtanāsu sasahiḥ saha ojo yajamānāya dhehi 
AVŚa dūrāc cakamānāya pratipāṇāyākṣaye 
AVŚc āsmā aśṛṇvann āśāḥ kāmenājanayant svaḥ 
AVŚa kāmena mā kāma āgan hṛdayād dhṛdayaṃ pari 
AVŚc yad amīṣām ado manas tad aitūpa mām iha 
AVŚa yat kāma kāmayamānā idaṃ kṛṇmasi te haviḥ 
AVŚc tan naḥ sarvaṃ sam ṛdhyatām athaitasya haviṣo vīhi svāhā 
AVŚa kālo aśvo vahati saptaraśmiḥ sahasrākṣo ajaro bhūriretāḥ 
AVŚc tam ā rohanti kavayo vipaścitas tasya cakrā bhuvanāni viśvā 
AVŚa sapta cakrān vahati kāla eṣa saptāsya nābhīr amṛtaṃ nv akṣaḥ 
AVŚc sa imā viśvā bhuvanāny añjat kālaḥ sa īyate prathamo nu devaḥ 
AVŚa pūrṇaḥ kumbho 'dhi kāla āhitas taṃ vai paśyāmo bahudhā nu santam 
AVŚc sa imā viśvā bhuvanāni pratyaṅ kālaṃ tam āhuḥ parame vyoman 
AVŚa sa eva saṃ bhuvanāny ābharat sa eva saṃ bhuvanāni pary ait 
AVŚc pitā sann abhavat putra eṣāṃ tasmād vai nānyat param asti tejaḥ 
AVŚa kālo 'mūṃ divam ajanayat kāla imāḥ pṛthivīr uta 
AVŚc kāle ha bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ ceṣitaṃ ha vi tiṣṭhate 
AVŚa kālo bhūtim asṛjata kāle tapati sūryaḥ 
AVŚc kāle ha viśvā bhūtāni kāle cakṣur vi paśyati 
AVŚa kāle manaḥ kāle prāṇaḥ kāle nāma samāhitam 
AVŚc kālena sarvā nandanty āgatena prajā imāḥ 
AVŚa kāle tapaḥ kāle jyeṣṭham kāle brahma samāhitam 
AVŚc kālo ha sarvasyeśvaro yaḥ pitāsīt prajāpateḥ 
AVŚa teneṣitaṃ tena jātaṃ tad u tasmin pratiṣṭhitam 
AVŚc kālo ha brahma bhūtvā bibharti parameṣṭhinam 
AVŚa kālaḥ prajā asṛjata kālo agre prajāpatim 
AVŚc svayaṃbhūḥ kaśyapaḥ kālāt tapaḥ kālād ajāyata 
AVŚa kālād āpaḥ sam abhavan kālād brahma tapo diśaḥ 
AVŚc kālenod eti sūryaḥ kāle ni viśate punaḥ 
AVŚa kālena vātaḥ pavate kālena pṛthivī mahī 
AVŚc dyaur mahī kāla āhitā 
AVŚa kālo ha bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ ca putro ajanayat purā 
AVŚc kālād ṛcaḥ sam abhavan yajuḥ kālād ajāyata 
AVŚa kālo yajñaṃ sam airayad devebhyo bhāgam akṣitam 
AVŚc kāle gandharvāpsarasaḥ kāle lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
AVŚa kāle 'yam aṅgirā devo 'tharvā cādhi tiṣṭhataḥ 
AVŚc imaṃ ca lokaṃ paramaṃ ca lokaṃ puṇyāṃś ca lokān vidhṛtīś ca puṇyāḥ 
AVŚe sarvāṃl lokān abhijitya brahmaṇā kālaḥ sa īyate paramo nu devaḥ 
AVŚa rātriṃrātrim aprayātaṃ bharanto 'śvāyeva tiṣṭhate ghāsam asmai 
AVŚc rāyas poṣeṇa sam iṣā madanto mā te agne prativeśā riṣāma 
AVŚa yā te vasor vāta iṣuḥ sā ta eṣā tayā no mṛḍa 
AVŚc rāyas poṣeṇa sam iṣā madanto mā te agne prativeśā riṣāma 
AVŚa sāyaṃsāyaṃ gṛhapatir no agniḥ prātaḥprātaḥ saumanasasya dātā 
AVŚc vasorvasor vasudāna edhi vayaṃ tvendhānās tanvaṃ puṣema 
AVŚa prātaḥprātar gṛhapatir no agniḥ sāyaṃsāyaṃ saumanasasya dātā 
AVŚc vasorvasor vasudāna edhīndhānās tvā śataṃhimā ṛdhema 
AVŚa apaścā dagdhānnasya bhūyāsam 
AVŚc annādāyānnapataye rudrāya namo agnaye 
AVŚe sabhyaḥ sabhāṃ me pāhi ye ca sabhyāḥ sabhāsadaḥ 
AVŚa tvām indrā puruhūta viśvam āyur vy aśnavan 
AVŚc aharahar balim it te haranto 'śvāyeva tiṣṭhate ghāsam agne 
AVŚa yamasya lokād adhy ā babhūvitha pramadā martyān pra yunakṣi dhīraḥ 
AVŚc ekākinā sarathaṃ yāsi vidvānt svapnaṃ mimāno asurasya yonau 
AVŚa bandhas tvāgre viśvacayā apaśyat purā rātryā janitor eke ahni 
AVŚc tataḥ svapnedam adhy ā babhūvitha bhiṣagbhyo rūpam apagūhamānaḥ 
AVŚa bṛhadgāvāsurebhyo 'dhi devān upāvartata mahimānam ichan 
AVŚc tasmai svapnāya dadhur ādhipatyaṃ trayastriṃśāsaḥ svar ānaśānāḥ 
AVŚa naitāṃ viduḥ pitaro nota devā yeṣāṃ jalpiś caraty antaredam 
AVŚc trite svapnam adadhur āptye nara ādityāso varuṇenānuśiṣṭāḥ 
AVŚa yasya krūram abhajanta duṣkṛto 'svapnena sukṛtaḥ puṇyam āyuḥ 
AVŚc svar madasi parameṇa bandhunā tapyamānasya manaso 'dhi jajñiṣe 
AVŚa vidma te sarvāḥ parijāḥ purastād vidma svapna yo adhipā ihā te 
AVŚc yaśaśvino no yaśaseha pāhy ārād dviṣebhir apa yāhi dūram 
AVŚa yathā kalāṃ yathā śaphaṃ yathā rṇaṃ samnayanti 
AVŚc evā duṣvapnyaṃ sarvam apriye saṃ nayāmasi 
AVŚa saṃ rājāno aguḥ sam ṛṇāmy aguḥ saṃ kuṣṭhā aguḥ saṃ kalā aguḥ 
AVŚc sam asmāsu yad duṣvapnyaṃ nir dviṣate duṣvapnyaṃ suvāma 
AVŚa devānāṃ patnīnāṃ garbha yamasya kara yo bhadraḥ svapna 
AVŚc sa mama yaḥ pāpas tad dviṣate pra hiṇmaḥ 
AVŚe mā tṛṣṭānām asi kṛṣṇaśakuner mukham 
AVŚa taṃ tvā svapna tathā saṃ vidma sa tvaṃ svapnāśva iva kāyam aśva iva nīnāham 
AVŚc anāsmākaṃ devapīyuṃ piyāruṃ vapa yad asmāsu duṣvapnyaṃ yad goṣu yac ca no gṛhe 
AVŚa anāsmākas tad devapīyuḥ piyārur niṣkam iva prati muñcatām 
AVŚc navāratnīn apamayā asmākaṃ tataḥ pari 
AVŚe duṣvapnyaṃ sarvaṃ dviṣate nir dayāmasi 
AVŚa ghṛtasya jūtiḥ samanā sadevā saṃvatsaraṃ haviṣā vardhayantī 
AVŚc śrotraṃ cakṣuḥ prāṇo 'chinno no astv achinnā vayam āyuṣo varcasaḥ 
AVŚa upāsmān prāṇo hvayatām upa prāṇaṃ havāmahe 
AVŚc varco jagrāha pṛthivy antarikṣaṃ varcaḥ somo bṛhaspatir vidhattā 
AVŚa varcaso dyāvāpṛthivī saṃgrahaṇī babhūvathur varco gṛhītvā pṛthivīm anu saṃ carema 
AVŚc yaśasam gāvo gopatim upa tiṣṭhanty āyatīr yaśo gṛhītvā pṛthivīm anu saṃ carema 
AVŚa vrajaṃ kṛṇudhvaṃ sa hi vo nṛpāṇo varmā sīvyadhvaṃ bahulā pṛthūni 
AVŚc puraḥ kṛṇudhvam āyasīr adhṛṣṭā mā vaḥ susroc camaso dṛṃhata tam 
AVŚa yajñasya cakṣuḥ prabhṛtir mukhaṃ ca vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi 
AVŚc imaṃ yajñaṃ vitataṃ viśvakarmaṇā devā yantu sumanasyamānāḥ 
AVŚa ye devānām ṛtvijo ye ca yajñiyā yebhyo havyaṃ kriyate bhāgadheyam 
AVŚc imaṃ yajñaṃ saha patnībhir etya yāvanto devās taviṣā mādayantām 
AVŚa tvam agne vratapā asi deva ā martyeṣv ā 
AVŚc tvaṃ yajñeṣv īḍyaḥ 
AVŚa yad vo vayaṃ pramināma vratāni viduṣāṃ devā aviduṣṭarāsaḥ 
AVŚc agniṣ ṭad viśvād ā pṛṇātu vidvānt somasya yo brāhmaṇāṃ āviveśa 
AVŚa ā devānām api panthām aganma yac chaknavāma tad anupravoḍhum 
AVŚc agnir vidvānt sa yajāt sa id dhotā so 'dhvarānt sa ṛtūn kalpayāti 
AVŚa vāṅ ma āsan nasoḥ prāṇaś cakṣur akṣṇoḥ śrotraṃ karṇayoḥ 
AVŚc apalitāḥ keśā aśoṇā dantā bahu bāhvor balam 
AVŚa ūrvor ojo jaṅghayor javaḥ pādayoḥ 
AVŚc pratiṣṭhā ariṣṭāni me sarvātmānibhṛṣṭaḥ 
AVŚa tanūs tanvā me sahe dataḥ sarvam āyur aśīya 
AVŚc syonaṃ me sīda puruḥ pṛṇasva pavamānaḥ svarge 
AVŚa priyaṃ mā kṛṇu deveṣu priyaṃ rājasu mā kṛṇu 
AVŚc priyaṃ sarvasya paśyata uta śūdra utārye 
AVŚa ut tiṣṭha brahmaṇas pate devān yajñena bodhaya 
AVŚc āyuḥ prāṇaṃ prajāṃ paśūn kīrtiṃ yajamānaṃ ca vardhaya 
AVŚa agne samidham āhārṣaṃ bṛhate jātavedase 
AVŚc sa me śraddhāṃ ca medhāṃ ca jātavedāḥ pra yachatu 
AVŚa idhmena tvā jātavedaḥ samidhā vardhayāmasi 
AVŚc tathā tvam asmān vardhaya prajayā ca dhanena ca 
AVŚa yad agne yāni kāni cid ā te dārūṇi dadhmasi 
AVŚc sarvaṃ tad astu me śivaṃ taj juṣasva yaviṣṭhya 
AVŚa etās te agne samidhas tvam iddhaḥ samid bhava 
AVŚc āyur asmāsu dhehy amṛtatvam ācāryāya 
AVŚa hariḥ suparṇo divam āruho 'rciṣā ye tvā dipsanti divam utpatantam 
AVŚc ava tāṃ jahi harasā jātavedo 'bibhyad ugro 'rciṣā divam ā roha sūrya 
AVŚa ayojālā asurā māyino 'yasmayaiḥ pāśair aṅkino ye caranti 
AVŚc tāṃs te randhayāmi harasā jātavedaḥ sahasraṛṣṭiḥ sapatnān pramṛṇan pāhi vajraḥ 
AVŚa paśyema śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa jīvema śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa budhyema śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa rohema śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa pūṣema śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa bhavema śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa bhūṣema śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa bhūyasīḥ śaradaḥ śatam 
AVŚa avyasaś ca vyacasaś ca bilaṃ vi ṣyāmi māyayā 
AVŚc tābhyām uddhṛtya vedam atha karmāṇi kṛṇmahe 
AVŚa jīvā stha jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam 
AVŚa upajīvā sthopa jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam 
AVŚa saṃjīvā stha saṃ jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam 
AVŚa jīvalā stha jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam 
AVŚa indra jīva sūrya jīva devā jīvā jīvyāsam aham 
AVŚc sarvam āyur jīvyāsam 
AVŚa stutā mayā varadā vedamātā pra codayantāṃ pāvamānī dvijānām 
AVŚc āyuḥ prāṇaṃ prajāṃ paśuṃ kīrtiṃ draviṇaṃ brahmavarcasam 
AVŚe mahyaṃ dattvā vrajata brahmalokam 
AVŚa yasmāt kośād udabharāma vedaṃ tasminn antar ava dadhma enam 
AVŚc kṛtam iṣṭaṃ brahmaṇo vīryeṇa tena mā devās tapasāvateha 
AVŚa indra tvā vṛṣabhaṃ vayaṃ sute some havāmahe 
AVŚc sa pāhi madhvo andhasaḥ 
AVŚa maruto yasya hi kṣaye pāthā divo vimahasaḥ 
AVŚc sa sugopātamo janaḥ 
AVŚa ukṣānnāya vaśānnāya somapṛṣṭhāya vedhase 
AVŚc stomair vidhemāgnaye 
AVŚa marutaḥ potrāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibantu 
AVŚa agnir āgnīdhrāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibatu 
AVŚa indro brahmā brāhmaṇāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibatu 
AVŚa devo draviṇodāḥ potrāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibatu 
AVŚa ā yāhi suṣumā hi ta indra somaṃ pibā imam 
AVŚc edaṃ barhiḥ sado mama 
AVŚa ā tvā brahmayujā harī vahatām indra keśinā 
AVŚc upa brahmāṇi naḥ śṛṇu 
AVŚa brahmāṇas tvā vayaṃ yujā somapām indra sominaḥ 
AVŚc sutāvanto havāmahe 
AVŚa ā no yāhi sutāvato 'smākaṃ suṣṭutīr upa 
AVŚc pibā su śiprinn andhasaḥ 
AVŚa ā te siñcāmi kukṣyor anu gātrā vi dhāvatu 
AVŚc gṛbhāya jihvayā madhu 
AVŚa svāduṣ ṭe astu saṃsude madhumān tanve tava 
AVŚc somaḥ śam astu te hṛde 
AVŚa ayam u tvā vicarṣaṇe janīr ivābhi saṃvṛtaḥ 
AVŚc pra soma indra sarpatu 
AVŚa tuvigrīvo vapodaraḥ subāhur andhaso sade 
AVŚc indro vṛtrāṇi jighnate 
AVŚa indra prehi puras tvaṃ viśvasyeśāna ojasā 
AVŚc vṛtrāṇi vṛtrahaṃ jahi 
AVŚa dīrghas te astv aṅkuśo yenā vasu prayachasi 
AVŚc yajamānāya sunvate 
AVŚa ayaṃ ta indra somo nipūto adhi barhiṣi 
AVŚc ehīm asya dravā piba 
AVŚa śācigo śācipūjanāyaṃ raṇāya te sutaḥ 
AVŚc ākhaṇḍala pra hūyase 
AVŚa yas te śṛṅgavṛṣo napāt praṇapāt kuṇḍapāyyaḥ 
AVŚc ny asmin dadhra ā manaḥ 
AVŚa indra tvā vṛṣabhaṃ vayaṃ sute some havāmahe 
AVŚc sa pāhi madhvo andhasaḥ 
AVŚa indra kratuvidaṃ sutaṃ somaṃ harya puruṣṭuta 
AVŚc pibā vṛṣasva tātṛpim 
AVŚa indra pra ṇo dhitāvānaṃ yajñaṃ viśvebhir devebhir 
AVŚc tira stavāna viśpate 
AVŚa indra somāḥ sutā ime tava pra yanti satpate 
AVŚc kṣayaṃ candrāsa indavaḥ 
AVŚa dadhiṣvā jaṭhare sutaṃ somam indra vareṇyam 
AVŚc tava dyukṣāsa indavaḥ 
AVŚa girvaṇaḥ pāhi naḥ sutaṃ madhor dhārābhir ajyase 
AVŚc indra tvādātam id yaśaḥ 
AVŚa abhi dyumnāni vanina indraṃ sacante akṣitā 
AVŚc pītvī somasya vāvṛdhe 
AVŚa arvāvato na ā gahi parāvataś ca vṛtrahan 
AVŚc imā juṣasva no giraḥ 
AVŚa yad antarā parāvatam arvāvataṃ ca hūyase 
AVŚc indreha tata ā gahi 
AVŚa ud ghed abhi śrutāmaghaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ naryāpasam 
AVŚc astāram eṣi sūrya 
AVŚa nava yo navatiṃ puro bibheda bāhvojasā 
AVŚc ahiṃ ca vṛtrahāvadhīt 
AVŚa sa na indraḥ śivaḥ sakhāśvāvad gomad yavamat 
AVŚc urudhāreva dohate 
AVŚa indra kratuvidaṃ sutaṃ somaṃ harya puruṣṭuta 
AVŚc pibā vṛṣasva tātṛpim 
AVŚa evā pāhi pratnathā mandatu tvā śrudhi brahma vāvṛdhasvota gīrbhiḥ 
AVŚc āviḥ sūryaṃ kṛṇuhi pīpihīṣo jahi śatrūṃr abhi gā indra tṛndhi 
AVŚa arvāṅ ehi somakāmaṃ tvāhur ayaṃ sutas tasya pibā madāya 
AVŚc uruvyacā jaṭhara ā vṛṣasva piteva naḥ śṛṇuhi hūyamānaḥ 
AVŚa āpūrṇo asya kalaśaḥ svāhā sekteva kośaṃ siṣice pibadhyai 
AVŚc sam u priyā āvavṛtran madāya pradakṣiṇid abhi somāsa indram 
AVŚa taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣaham vasor mandānam andhasaḥ 
AVŚc abhi vatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava indraṃ gīrbhir navāmahe 
AVŚa dyukṣaṃ sudānuṃ taviṣībhir āvṛtaṃ giriṃ na purubhojasam 
AVŚc kṣumantaṃ vājaṃ śatinaṃ sahasriṇaṃ makṣū gomantam īmahe 
AVŚa tat tvā yāmi suvīryaṃ tad brahma pūrvacittaye 
AVŚc yenā yatibhyo bhṛgave dhane hite yena praskaṇvam āvitha 
AVŚa yenā samudram asṛjo mahīr apas tad indra vṛṣṇi te śavaḥ 
AVŚc sadyaḥ so asya mahimā na saṃnaśe yaṃ kṣoṇīr anucakrade 
AVŚa ud u te madhumattamā gira stomāsa īrate 
AVŚc satrājito dhanasā akṣitotayo vājayanto rathā iva 
AVŚa kaṇvā iva bhṛgavaḥ sūryā iva viśvam id dhītam ānaśuḥ 
AVŚc indraṃ stomebhir mahayanta āyavaḥ priyamedhāso asvaran 
AVŚa indraḥ pūrbhid ātirad dāsam arkair vidadvasur dayamāno vi śatrūn 
AVŚc brahmajūtas tanvā vāvṛdhāno bhūridātra āpṛṇad rodasī ubhe 
AVŚa makhasya te taviṣasya pra jūtim iyarmi vācam amṛtāya bhūṣan 
AVŚc indra kṣitīnām asi mānuṣīṇāṃ viśāṃ daivīnām uta pūrvayāvā 
AVŚa indro vṛtram avṛṇoc chardhanītiḥ pra māyinām aminād varpaṇītiḥ 
AVŚc ahan vyaṃsam uśadhag vaneṣv āvir dhenā akṛṇod rāmyāṇām 
AVŚa indraḥ svarṣā janayann ahāni jigāyośigbhiḥ pṛtanā abhiṣṭiḥ 
AVŚc prārocayan manave ketum ahnām avindaj jyotir bṛhate raṇāya 
AVŚa indras tujo barhaṇā ā viveśa nṛvad dadhāno naryā purūṇi 
AVŚc acetayad dhiya imā jaritre premaṃ varṇam atirac chukram āsām 
AVŚa maho mahāni panayanty asyendrasya karma sukṛtā purūṇi 
AVŚc vṛjanena vṛjinānt saṃ pipeṣa māyābhir dasyūṃr abhibhūtyojāḥ 
AVŚa yudhendro mahnā varivaś cakāra devebhyaḥ satpatiś carṣaṇiprāḥ 
AVŚc vivasvataḥ sadane asya tāni viprā ukthebhiḥ kavayo gṛṇanti 
AVŚa satrāsāhaṃ vareṇyaṃ sahodāṃ sasavāṃsaṃ svar apaś ca devīḥ 
AVŚc sasāna yaḥ pṛthivīṃ dyām utemām indraṃ madanty anu dhīraṇāsaḥ 
AVŚa sasānātyāṃ uta sūryaṃ sasānendraḥ sasāna purubhojasaṃ gām 
AVŚc hiraṇyayam uta bhogaṃ sasāna hatvī dasyūn prāryaṃ varṇam āvat 
AVŚa indra oṣadhīr asanod ahāni vanaspatīṃr asanod antarikṣam 
AVŚc bibheda balaṃ nunude vivāco 'thābhavad damitābhikratūnām 
AVŚa śunaṃ huvema maghavānam indram asmin bhare nṛtamaṃ vājasātau 
AVŚc śṛṇvantam ugram ūtaye samatsu ghnantaṃ vṛtrāṇi saṃjitaṃ dhanānām 
AVŚa ud u brahmāṇy airata śravasyendraṃ samarye mahayā vasiṣṭha 
AVŚc ā yo viśvāni śavasā tatānopaśrotā ma īvato vacāṃsi 
AVŚa ayāmi ghoṣa indra devajāmir irajyanta yac churudho vivāci 
AVŚc nahi svam āyuś cikite janeṣu tānīd aṃhāṃsy ati parṣy asmān 
AVŚa yuje rathaṃ gaveṣaṇaṃ haribhyām upa brahmāṇi jujuṣāṇam asthuḥ 
AVŚc vi bādhiṣṭa sya rodasī mahitvendro vṛtrāṇy apratī jaghanvān 
AVŚa āpaś cit pipyu staryo na gāvo nakṣann ṛtaṃ jaritāras ta indra 
AVŚc yāhi vāyur na niyuto no achā tvaṃ hi dhībhir dayase vi vājān 
AVŚa te tvā madā indra mādayantu śuṣmiṇaṃ tuvirādhasaṃ jaritre 
AVŚc eko devatrā dayase hi martān asmin chūra savane mādayasva 
AVŚa eved indraṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ vajrabāhuṃ vasiṣṭhāso abhy arcanty arkaiḥ 
AVŚc sa na stuto vīravad dhātu gomad yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ 
AVŚa ṛjīṣī vajrī vṛṣabhas turāṣāṭ chuṣmī rājā vṛtrahā somapāvā 
AVŚc yuktvā haribhyām upa yāsad arvāṅ mādhyaṃdine savane matsad indraḥ 
AVŚa indraś ca somaṃ pibataṃ bṛhaspate 'smin yajñe mandasānā vṛṣaṇvasū 
AVŚc ā vāṃ viśantv indavaḥ svābhuvo 'sme rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yachatam 
AVŚa ā vo vahantu saptayo raghuṣyado raghupatvānaḥ pra jigāta bāhubhiḥ 
AVŚc sīdatā barhir uru vaḥ sadas kṛtaṃ mādayadhvaṃ maruto madhvo andhasaḥ 
AVŚa imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedase ratham iva saṃ mahemā manīṣayā 
AVŚc bhadrā hi naḥ pramatir asya saṃsady agne sakhye mā riṣāmā vayaṃ tava 
AVŚa aibhir agne sarathaṃ yāhy arvāṅ nānārathaṃ vā vibhavo hy aśvāḥ 
AVŚc patnīvatas triṃśataṃ trīṃś ca devān anuṣvadham ā vaha mādayasva 
AVŚa vayam u tvām apūrvya sthūraṃ na kac cid bharanto 'vasyavaḥ 
AVŚc vāje citraṃ havāmahe 
AVŚa upa tvā karmann ūtaye sa no yuvograś cakrāma yo dhṛṣat 
AVŚc tvām id dhy avitāraṃ vavṛmahe sakhāya indra sānasim 
AVŚa yo na idamidaṃ purā pra vasya ānināya tam u va stuṣe 
AVŚc sakhāya indram ūtaye 
AVŚa haryaśvaṃ satpatiṃ carṣaṇīsahaṃ sa hi ṣmā yo amandata 
AVŚc ā tu naḥ sa vayati gavyam aśvyaṃ stotṛbhyo maghavā śatam 
AVŚa pra maṃhiṣṭhāya bṛhate bṛhadraye satyaśuṣmāya tavase matiṃ bhare 
AVŚc apām iva pravaṇe yasya durdharaṃ rādho viśvāyu śavase apāvṛtam 
AVŚa adha te viśvam anu hāsad iṣṭaya āpo nimneva savanā haviṣmataḥ 
AVŚc yat parvate na samaśīta haryata indrasya vajraḥ śnathitā hiraṇyayaḥ 
AVŚa asmai bhīmāya namasā sam adhvara uṣo na śubhra ā bharā panīyase 
AVŚc yasya dhāma śravase nāmendriyaṃ jyotir akāri harito nāyase 
AVŚa ime ta indra te vayaṃ puruṣṭuta ye tvārabhya carāmasi prabhūvaso 
AVŚc nahi tvad anyo girvaṇo giraḥ sadhat kṣoṇīr iva prati no harya tad vacaḥ 
AVŚa bhūri ta indra vīryaṃ tava smasy asya stotur maghavan kāmam ā pṛṇa 
AVŚc anu te dyaur bṛhatī vīryaṃ mama iyaṃ ca te pṛthivī nema ojase 
AVŚa tvaṃ tam indra parvataṃ mahām uruṃ vajreṇa vajrin parvaśaś cakartitha 
AVŚc avāsṛjo nivṛtāḥ sartavā apaḥ satrā viśvaṃ dadhiṣe kevalaṃ sahaḥ 
AVŚa udapruto na vayo rakṣamāṇā vāvadato abhriyasyeva ghoṣāḥ 
AVŚc giribhrajo normayo madanto bṛhaspatim abhy arkā anāvan 
AVŚa saṃ gobhir aṅgiraso nakṣamāṇo bhaga ived aryamaṇaṃ nināya 
AVŚc jane mitro na dampatī anakti bṛhaspate vājayāśūṃr ivājau 
AVŚa sādhvaryā atithinīr iṣirā spārhāḥ suvarṇā anavadyarūpāḥ 
AVŚc bṛhaspatiḥ parvatebhyo vitūryā nir gā ūpe yavam iva sthivibhyaḥ 
AVŚa āpruṣāyan madhunā ṛtasya yonim avakṣipann arka ulkām iva dyoḥ 
AVŚc bṛhaspatir uddharann aśmano gā bhūmyā udneva vi tvacaṃ bibheda 
AVŚa apa jyotiṣā tamo antarikṣad udnaḥ śīpālam iva vāta ājat 
AVŚc bṛhaspatir anumṛśyā valasyābhram iva vāta ā cakra ā gāḥ 
AVŚa yadā valasya pīyato jasuṃ bhed bṛhaspatir agnitapobhir arkaiḥ 
AVŚc dadbhir na jihvā pariviṣṭam ādad āvir nidhīṃr akṛṇod usriyāṇām 
AVŚa bṛhaspatir amata hi tyad āsāṃ nāma svarīṇāṃ sadane guhā yat 
AVŚc āṇḍeva bhitvā śakunasya garbham ud usriyāḥ parvatasya tmanājat 
AVŚa aśnāpinaddhaṃ madhu pary apaśyan matsyaṃ na dīna udani kṣiyantam 
AVŚc niṣ ṭaj jabhāra camasaṃ na vṛkṣād bṛhaspatir viraveṇā vikṛtya 
AVŚa soṣām avindat sa svaḥ so agniṃ so arkeṇa vi babādhe tamāṃsi 
AVŚc bṛhaspatir govapuṣo valasya nir majjānaṃ na parvaṇo jabhāra 
AVŚa himeva parṇā muṣitā vanāni bṛhaspatinākṛpayad valo gāḥ 
AVŚc anānukṛtyam apunaś cakāra yāt sūryāmāsā mitha uccarātaḥ 
AVŚa abhi śyāvaṃ na kṛśanebhir aśvaṃ nakṣatrebhiḥ pitaro dyām apiṃśan 
AVŚc rātryāṃ tamo adadhur jyotir ahan bṛhaspatir bhinad adriṃ vidad gāḥ 
AVŚa idam akarma namo abhriyāya yaḥ pūrvīr anv ānonavīti 
AVŚc bṛhaspatiḥ sa hi gobhiḥ so aśvaiḥ sa vīrebhiḥ sa nṛbhir no vayo dhāt 
AVŚa achā ma indraṃ matayaḥ svarvidaḥ sadhrīcīr viśvā uśatīr anūṣata 
AVŚc pari ṣvajante janayo yathā patiṃ maryaṃ na śundhyuṃ maghavānam ūtaye 
AVŚa na ghā tvadrig apa veti me manas tve it kāmaṃ puruhūta śiśraya 
AVŚc rājeva dasma ni ṣado 'dhi barhiṣy asmint su some 'vapānam astu te 
AVŚa viṣūvṛd indro amuter uta kṣudhaḥ sa id rāyo maghavā vasva īśate 
AVŚc tasyed ime pravaṇe sapta sindhavo vayo vardhanti vṛṣabhasya śuṣmiṇaḥ 
AVŚa vayo na vṛkṣaṃ supalāśam āsadant somāsa indraṃ mandinaś camūṣadaḥ 
AVŚc praiṣām anīkaṃ śavasā davidyutad vidat svar manave jyotir āryam 
AVŚa kṛtaṃ na śvaghnī vi cinoti devane saṃvargaṃ yan maghavā sūryaṃ jayat 
AVŚc na tat te anyo anu vīryaṃ śakan na purāṇo maghavan nota nūtanaḥ 
AVŚa viśaṃviśaṃ maghavā pary aśāyata janānāṃ dhenā avacākaśad vṛṣā 
AVŚc yasyāha śakraḥ savaneṣu raṇyati sa tīvraiḥ somaiḥ sahate pṛtanyataḥ 
AVŚa āpo na sindhum abhi yat samakṣarant somāsa indraṃ kulyā iva hradam 
AVŚc vardhanti viprā maho asya sādane yavaṃ na vṛṣṭir divyena dānunā 
AVŚa vṛṣā na kruddhaḥ patayad rajaḥsv ā yo aryapatnīr akṛṇod imā apaḥ 
AVŚc sa sunvate maghavā jīradānave 'vindaj jyotir manave haviṣmate 
AVŚa uj jāyatāṃ paraśu jyotiṣā saha bhūyā ṛtasya sudughā purāṇavat 
AVŚc vi rocatām aruṣo bhānunā śuciḥ svar na śukraṃ śuśucīta satpatiḥ 
AVŚa gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ durevāṃ yavena kṣudhaṃ puruhūta viśvām 
AVŚc vayaṃ rājabhiḥ prathamā dhanāny asmākena vṛjanenā jayema 
AVŚa bṛhaspatir naḥ pari pātu paścād utottarasmād adharād aghāyoḥ 
AVŚc indraḥ purastād uta madhyato naḥ sakhā sakhibhyaḥ varivaḥ kṛṇotu 
AVŚa bṛhaspate yuvam indraś ca vasvo divyasyeśāthe uta pārthivasya 
AVŚc dhattaṃ rayiṃ stuvate kīraye cid yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ 
AVŚa vayam u tvā taditarthā indra tvāyantaḥ sakhāyaḥ 
AVŚc kaṇvā ukthebhir jarante 
AVŚa na ghem anyad ā papana vajrinn apaso naviṣṭau 
AVŚc taved u stomaṃ ciketa 
AVŚa ichanti devāḥ sunvantaṃ na svapnāya spṛhayanti 
AVŚc yanti pramādam atandrāḥ 
AVŚa vayam indra tvāyavo 'bhi pra ṇonumo vṛṣan 
AVŚc viddhi tv asya no vaso 
AVŚa mā no nide ca vaktave 'ryo randhīr arāvne 
AVŚc tve api kratur mama 
AVŚa tvaṃ varmāsi saprathaḥ puroyodhaś ca vṛtrahan 
AVŚc tvayā prati bruve yujā 
AVŚa vārtrahatyāya śavase pṛtanāṣāhyāya ca 
AVŚc indra tvā vartayāmasi 
AVŚa arvācīnaṃ su te mana uta cakṣuḥ śatakrato 
AVŚc indra kṛṇvantu vāghataḥ 
AVŚa nāmāni te śatakrato viśvābhir gīrbhir īmahe 
AVŚc indrābhimātiṣāhye 
AVŚa puruṣṭutasya dhāmabhiḥ śatena mahayāmasi 
AVŚc indrasya carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ 
AVŚa indraṃ vṛtrāya hantave puruhūtam upa bruve 
AVŚc bhareṣu vājasātaye 
AVŚa vājeṣu sāsahir bhava tvām īmahe śatakrato 
AVŚc indra vṛtrāya hantave 
AVŚa dyumneṣu pṛtanājye pṛtsutūrṣu śravaḥsu ca 
AVŚc indra sākṣvābhimātiṣu 
AVŚa śuṣmintamaṃ na ūtaye dyumninaṃ pāhi jāgṛvim 
AVŚc indra somaṃ śatakrato 
AVŚa indriyāṇi śatakrato yā te janeṣu pañcasu 
AVŚc indra tāni ta ā vṛṇe 
AVŚa agann indra śravo bṛhad dyumnaṃ dadhiṣva duṣṭaram 
AVŚc ut te śuṣmaṃ tirāmasi 
AVŚa arvāvato na ā gahy atho śakra parāvataḥ 
AVŚc u loko yas te adriva indreha tata ā gahi 
AVŚa indro aṅgaṃ mahad bhayam abhi ṣad apa cucyavat 
AVŚc sa hi sthiro vicarṣaṇiḥ 
AVŚa indraś ca mṛlayāti no na naḥ paścād aghaṃ naśat 
AVŚc bhadraṃ bhavāti naḥ puraḥ 
AVŚa indra āśābhyas pari sarvābhyo abhayaṃ karat 
AVŚc jetā śatrūn vicarṣaṇiḥ 
AVŚa ny ū ṣu vācaṃ pra mahe bharāmahe gira indrāya sadane vivasvataḥ 
AVŚc nū cid dhi ratnaṃ sasatām ivāvidan na duṣṭutir draviṇodeṣu śasyate 
AVŚa duro aśvasya dura indra gor asi duro yavasya vasuna inas patiḥ 
AVŚc śikṣānaraḥ pradivo akāmakarśanaḥ sakhā sakhibhyas tam idaṃ gṛṇīmasi 
AVŚa śacīva indra purukṛd dyumattama taved idam abhitaś cekite vasu 
AVŚc ataḥ saṃgṛbhyābhibhūta ā bhara mā tvāyato jarituḥ kāmam ūnayīḥ 
AVŚa ebhir dyubhir sumanā ebhir indubhir nirundhāno amatiṃ gobhir aśvinā 
AVŚc indreṇa dasyuṃ darayanta indubhir yutadveṣasaḥ sam iṣā rabhemahi 
AVŚa sam indra rāyā sam iṣā rabhemahi saṃ vājebhiḥ puruścandrair abhidyubhiḥ 
AVŚc saṃ devyā pramatyā vīraśuṣmayā goagrayāśvāvatyā rabhemahi 
AVŚa te tvā madā amadan tāni vṛṣṇyā te somāso vṛtrahatyeṣu satpate 
AVŚc yat kārave daśa vṛtrāṇy aprati barhiṣmate ni sahasrāṇi barhayaḥ 
AVŚa yudhā yudham upa ghed eṣi dhṛṣṇuyā purā puraṃ sam idaṃ haṃsy ojasā 
AVŚc namyā yad indra sakhyā parāvati nibarhayo namuciṃ nāma māyinam 
AVŚa tvaṃ karañjam uta parṇayaṃ vadhīs tejiṣṭhayātithigvasya vartanī 
AVŚc tvaṃ śatā vaṅgṛdasyābhinat puro 'nānudaḥ pariṣūtā ṛjiśvanā 
AVŚa tvam etāṃ janarājño dvir daśābandhunā suśravasopajagmuṣaḥ 
AVŚc ṣaṣṭiṃ sahasrā navatiṃ nava śruto ni cakreṇa rathyā duṣpadāvṛṇak 
AVŚa tvam āvitha suśravasaṃ tavotibhis tava trāmabhir indra tūrvayāṇam 
AVŚc tva asmai kutsam atithigvam āyuṃ mahe rājñe yūne arandhanāyaḥ 
AVŚa ya udṛcīndra devagopāḥ sakhāyas te śivatamā asāma 
AVŚc tvāṃ stoṣāma tvayā suvīrā drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ dadhānāḥ 
AVŚa abhi tvā vṛṣabhā sute sutaṃ sṛjāmi pītaye 
AVŚc tṛmpā vy aśnuhī madam 
AVŚa mā tvā mūrā aviṣyavo mopahasvāna ā dabhan 
AVŚc mākīṃ brahmadviṣo vanaḥ 
AVŚa iha tvā goparīṇasā mahe mandantu rādhase 
AVŚc saro gauro yathā piba 
AVŚa abhi pra gopatiṃ girendram arca yathā vide 
AVŚc sūnuṃ satyasya satpatim 
AVŚa ā harayaḥ sasṛjrire 'ruṣīr adhi barhiṣi 
AVŚc yatrābhi saṃnavāmahe 
AVŚa indrāya gāva āśiraṃ duduhre vajriṇe madhu 
AVŚc yat sīm upahvare vidat 
AVŚa ā tū na indra madryag ghuvānaḥ somapītaye 
AVŚc haribhyāṃ yāhy adrivaḥ 
AVŚa satto hotā na ṛtviyas tistire barhir ānuṣak 
AVŚc ayujran prātar adrayaḥ 
AVŚa imā brahma brahmavāhaḥ kriyanta ā barhiḥ sīda 
AVŚc vīhi śūra purolāśam 
AVŚa rārandhi savaneṣu ṇa eṣu stomeṣu vṛtrahan 
AVŚc uktheṣv indra girvaṇaḥ 
AVŚa matayaḥ somapām uruṃ rihanti śavasas patim 
AVŚc indraṃ vatsaṃ na mātaraḥ 
AVŚa sa mandasvā hy andhaso rādhase tanvā mahe 
AVŚc na stotāraṃ nide karaḥ 
AVŚa vayam indra tvāyavo haviṣmanto jarāmahe 
AVŚc uta tvam asmayur vaso 
AVŚa māre asmad vi mumuco haripriyārvāṅ yāhi 
AVŚc indra svadhāvo matsveha 
AVŚa arvāñcaṃ tvā sukhe rathe vahatām indra keśinā 
AVŚc ghṛtasnū barhir āsade 
AVŚa upa naḥ sutam ā gahi somam indra gavāśiram 
AVŚc haribhyāṃ yas te asmayuḥ 
AVŚa tam indra madam ā gahi barhiṣṭhāṃ grāvabhiḥ sutam 
AVŚc kuvin nv asya tṛpṇavaḥ 
AVŚa indram itthā giro mamāchāgur iṣitā itaḥ 
AVŚc āvṛte somapītaye 
AVŚa indraṃ somasya pītaye stomair iha havāmahe 
AVŚc ukthebhiḥ kuvid āgamat 
AVŚa indra somāḥ sutā ime tān dadhiṣva śatakrato 
AVŚc jathare vājinīvaso 
AVŚa vidmā hi tvā dhanaṃjayaṃ vājeṣu dadhṛṣaṃ kave 
AVŚc adhā te sumnam īmahe 
AVŚa imam indra gavāśiraṃ yavāśiraṃ ca naḥ piba 
AVŚc āgatyā vṛṣabhiḥ sutam 
AVŚa tubhyed indra sva okye somaṃ codāmi pītaye 
AVŚc eṣa rārantu te hṛdi 
AVŚa tvāṃ sutasya pītaye pratnam indra havāmahe 
AVŚc kuśikāso avasyavaḥ 
AVŚa aśvāvati prathamo goṣu gachati suprāvīr indra martyas tavotibhiḥ 
AVŚc tam it pṛṇakṣi vasunā bhavīyasā sindhum āpo yathābhito vicetasaḥ 
AVŚa āpo na devīr upa yanti hotriyam avaḥ paśyanti vitataṃ yathā rajaḥ 
AVŚc prācair devāsaḥ pra ṇayanti devayuṃ brahmapriyaṃ joṣayante varā iva 
AVŚa adhi dvayor adadhā ukthyaṃ vaco yatasrucā mithunā yā saparyataḥ 
AVŚc asaṃyatto vrate te kṣeti puṣyati bhadrā śaktir yajamānāya sunvate 
AVŚa ād aṅgirāḥ prathamaṃ dadhire vaya iddhāgnayaḥ śamyā ye sukṛtyayā 
AVŚc sarvaṃ paṇeḥ sam avindanta bhojanam aśvāvantaṃ gomantam ā paśuṃ naraḥ 
AVŚa yajñair atharvā prathamaḥ pathas tate tataḥ sūryo vratapā vena ājani 
AVŚc ā gā ājad uśanā kāvyaḥ sacā yamasya jātam amṛtaṃ yajāmahe 
AVŚa barhir vā yat svapatyāya vṛjyate 'rko vā ślokam āghoṣate divi 
AVŚc grāvā yatra vadati karur ukthyas tasyed indro abhipitveṣu raṇyati 
AVŚa progrāṃ pītiṃ vṛṣṇa iyarmi satyāṃ prayai sutasya haryaśva tubhyam 
AVŚc indra dhenābhir iha mādayasva dhībhir viśvābhiḥ śacyā gṛṇānaḥ 
AVŚa yogeyoge tavastaraṃ vājevāje havāmahe 
AVŚc sakhāya indram ūtaye 
AVŚa ā ghā gamad yadi śravat sahasriṇībhir ūtibhiḥ 
AVŚc vājebhir upa no havam 
AVŚa anu pratnasyaukaso huve tuvipratiṃ naram 
AVŚc yaṃ te pūrvaṃ pitā huve 
AVŚa yuñjanti bradhnam aruṣaṃ carantaṃ pari tasthuṣaḥ 
AVŚc rocante rocanā divi 
AVŚa yuñjanti asya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe 
AVŚc śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛvāhasā 
AVŚa ketuṃ kṛṇvann aketave peśo maryā apeśase 
AVŚc sam uṣadbhir ajāyathāḥ 
AVŚa yad indrāhaṃ yathā tvam īśīya vasva eka it 
AVŚc stotā me goṣakhā syāt 
AVŚa śikṣeyam asmai ditseyaṃ śacīpate manīṣiṇe 
AVŚc yad ahaṃ gopatiḥ syām 
AVŚa dhenuṣ ṭa indra sūnṛtā yajamānāya sunvate 
AVŚc gām aśvaṃ pipyuṣī duhe 
AVŚa na te vartāsti rādhasa indra devo na martyaḥ 
AVŚc yad ditsasi stuto magham 
AVŚa yajña indram avardhayad yad bhūmiṃ vy avartayat 
AVŚc cakrāṇa opaśaṃ divi 
AVŚa vāvṛdhānasya te vayaṃ viśvā dhanāni jigyuṣaḥ 
AVŚc ūtim indrā vṛṇīmahe 
AVŚa vy antarikṣam atiran made somasya rocanā 
AVŚc indro yad abhinad valam 
AVŚa ud gā ājad aṅgirobhya āviṣ krṇvan guhā satīḥ 
AVŚc arvāñcaṃ nunude valam 
AVŚa indreṇa rocanā divo dṛlhāni dṛṃhitāni ca 
AVŚc sthirāṇi na parāṇude 
AVŚa apām ūrmir madann iva stoma indrājirāyate 
AVŚc vi te madā arājiṣuḥ 
AVŚa tvaṃ hi stomavardhana indrāsy ukthavardhanaḥ 
AVŚc stotṝṇām uta bhadrakṛt 
AVŚa indram it keśinā harī somapeyāya vakṣataḥ 
AVŚc upa yajñaṃ surādhasam 
AVŚa apāṃ phenena namuceḥ śira indrod avartayaḥ 
AVŚc viśvā yad ajaya spṛdhaḥ 
AVŚa māyābhir utsisṛpsata indra dyām ārurukṣataḥ 
AVŚc ava dasyūṃr adhūnuthāḥ 
AVŚa asunvām indra saṃsadaṃ viṣūcīṃ vy anāśayaḥ 
AVŚc somapā uttaro bhavan 
AVŚa pra te mahe vidathe śaṃsiṣaṃ harī pra te vanve vanuṣo haryataṃ madam 
AVŚc ghṛtaṃ na yo haribhiś cāru secata ā tvā viśantu harivarpasaṃ giraḥ 
AVŚa hariṃ hi yonim abhi ye samasvaran hinvanto harī divyaṃ yathā sadaḥ 
AVŚc ā yaṃ pṛṇanti haribhir na dhenava indrāya śūśaṃ harivantam arcata 
AVŚa so asya vajro harito ya āyaso harir nikāmo harir ā gabhastyoḥ 
AVŚc dyumnī suśipro harimanyusāyaka indre ni rūpā haritā mimikṣire 
AVŚa divi na ketur adhi dhāyi haryato vivyacad vajro harito na raṃhyā 
AVŚc tudad ahiṃ hariśipro ya āyasaḥ sahasraśokā abhavad dharimbharaḥ 
AVŚa tvaṃtvam aharyathā upastutaḥ pūrvebhir indra harikeśa yajvabhiḥ 
AVŚc tvaṃ haryasi tava viśvam ukthyam asāmi rādho harijāta haryatam 
AVŚa tā vajriṇaṃ mandinaṃ stomyaṃ mada indraṃ rathe vahato haryatā harī 
AVŚc purūṇy asmai savanāni haryata indrāya somā harayo dadhanvire
